# Changelog

All notable changes to TagPulse will be documented in this file.

## Unreleased

### Fixed

- **Sprint 66 closeout — floor-position worker test no longer wall-clock-flaky (tests).** `FloorPositionWorker.run_once` now accepts an optional `now` (defaults to `datetime.now(UTC)`, so production behaviour is unchanged) purely for deterministic testing. `test_worker_run_once_delegates_to_service` pinned its observations to a fixed `NOW` but called the bare `run_once()`, which used real wall-clock time — once the suite ran more than `lookback_s` after that fixed `NOW`, the observations fell outside the estimator's lookback window and the test asserted `0 == 1`. The delegation test now passes `NOW` explicitly. No behaviour change; `make check` green again.

- **Operator runbook — floor-estimator enable targets the worker container (docs).** The Sprint 66 "Indoor positioning estimator" enable steps in [docs/operator-quickstart.md](docs/operator-quickstart.md) said "api/worker container" — corrected to the **`tp${env}-worker`** container with the exact `az containerapp update` command. The api runs `WORKERS_INLINE=false` (HTTP only); the inline workers (incl. `FloorPositionWorker`) run in the dedicated worker container, so setting the flag on the api is a silent no-op (verified live in dev). Also adds the `--set-strategy` step + the `floor-path?source=computed` check. Docs only.

### Added

- **WM `v:2` — `sn` accepts string or number + `lat`/`lon` range-checked (backend).** Follow-up to Sprint 67. The compact-dialect `sn` ([wm_wire_format.py](src/tagpulse/ingestion/wm_wire_format.py)) now accepts a non-empty **string** (UUID, recommended) **or an integer** serial (coerced to its string form) — a `float`/empty/missing `sn` still rejects (`missing_required_field`). Envelope `lat`/`lon` are now **range-validated** when present (`lat` ∈ [-90, 90], `lon` ∈ [-180, 180]; `null` still means "no fix") — an out-of-range or non-number coordinate rejects the message with the new DLQ `reason="invalid_location"`, so a malformed fix can't place a bad map marker. Spec §12.2/§12.6 updated; 9 new tests. `make check` green.
 Follow-up to Sprint 67 ([#127](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/pull/127)). The `fw` firmware token in the WM compact dialect ([wm_wire_format.py](src/tagpulse/ingestion/wm_wire_format.py)) is now **opaque — accepting a string *or* a number** (previously number-only, which would have DLQ'd the whole message the moment WM switched to a semver string). A *float* `fw` can't even order versions (`1.10` collapses to `1.1`; as floats `1.10 < 1.9`), so WM is advised to move to a string `"1.10.2"`; the parser tolerates the migration with **zero wire break** and stores the value verbatim on `tag_data._fw`. Separately, the positional `epcs[]` tuple parser is now **append-tolerant** (length ≥ 5; trailing slots reserved and ignored) so a future field such as the `[NEEDS WM]` peak-RSSI `rpk` can be added without a coordinated break — length < 5 is still rejected. Spec §12.2/§12.3/§12.6 + ADR-025 Amendment 1 updated; 6 new tests. `make check` green.
 [scripts/simulate_floor_positioning.py](scripts/simulate_floor_positioning.py) `--emit` previously sent only a sim URN (`identity.epc` = `urn:epc:sim:floor:NNNN`) and `signal_strength`, so the UI "EPC (hex)" column was blank and reads carried no temperature/humidity. Each placed asset now also gets a **display-only uppercase-hex EPC** surfaced as `identity.epc_hex`, and every read carries synthetic `sensor_data` (`temperature_c` / `humidity_pct`, tunable via new `--temp-c` / `--humidity` base flags with per-read jitter). The URN stays the **binding/positioning key** (`asset_tag_bindings.binding_value`, matched against `tag_reads.epc`), so the estimator is unaffected — the hex EPC and sensors are purely additive (sensors also fan out to `telemetry_readings`). New `PlacedAsset.epc_hex` field; tests updated ([tests/unit/test_floor_positioning_sim.py](tests/unit/test_floor_positioning_sim.py)). Tooling only.

- **Sprint 67 (planning) — WM compact wire dialect (`v:2`), spec + ADR (docs).** Amends the ratified Edge Wire Format v2 to add an **opt-in** compact dialect for WM, the platform's sole edge producer, gated on the reserved envelope field `v:2` (so the v2.0 keyed format and its conformance fixtures are untouched). New **§12** in [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md): a **single uniform 5-tuple** `[epc, rssi, cnt, tmp, hum]` for **all three** message types (snap/add/delete — WM ships one serializer); envelope-level antenna `ant`, firmware `fw`, string `sn` (UUID-shaped), ISO-8601 `ts`, and float `rssi`. On delete the reading slots are `null`/`0` placeholders and ignored (only `epc` is used). [ADR-025](docs/adr/025-edge-wire-format-v2.md) bumped **accepted → amended** with "Amendment 1" recording the decision and the two deliberate bandwidth concessions (string `sn`, ISO `ts`) accepted because WM's current SKU can't emit numeric serial / epoch-ms. Backend parser, subscriber routing, conformance fixtures, simulator, and demo rigs land in follow-up commits on this branch. One `[CONFIRM WM]` detail open: null-vs-zero for the unused delete slots (parser accepts both).

- **Sprint 66 — `--emit` antenna-path fix + dev validation result (tooling).** Fixes a second [simulate_floor_positioning.py](scripts/simulate_floor_positioning.py) `--emit` bug: the port-0 antenna survey PUT used `/device-registry/{id}/antennas/0` (the antenna router is mounted at `/devices/...`) **and didn't `raise_for_status`**, so it silently 404'd → no surveyed antennas → the estimator found zero observations. Now PUTs `/devices/{id}/antennas/0` and raises on failure. **Validated end-to-end in dev**: seeded demo-wm-dc, ran the production pipeline via `azd-job validate_floor_positioning.py --tenant-slug demo-wm-dc` → **8/8 computed fixes written** to `asset_positions(source='computed')`, RMSE 32.9 m (matches the offline ground-truth). Tooling only.

- **Sprint 66 — floor-position dev validator + `--emit` category fix (tooling).** New [scripts/validate_floor_positioning.py](scripts/validate_floor_positioning.py) runs the **production** pipeline (`TimescaleObservationSource` → `rssi_weighted_centroid` → `TimescalePositionWriter`) for one tenant against `--emit`-seeded data and reports **computed-vs-placed** error + RMSE; `--set-strategy` persists `tenants.position_strategy`, `--clean` removes the seed. Resolves any tenant via `--tenant-slug` (`uuid5(NAMESPACE_DNS, "<slug>.tagpulse.local")` — e.g. `demo-wm-dc` = SuperMart) or `--tenant-id`; designed for `azd-job.sh`. Also **fixes [simulate_floor_positioning.py](scripts/simulate_floor_positioning.py) `--emit`**: it omitted the required `category_id` (and the category needs `category_type`/`required_tags`) — the bug only surfaced against a live API, now seeds assets correctly. Verified by seeding demo-wm-dc in dev (9 readers + 8 placed assets + 384 multi-reader reads). Tooling only.

- **Sprint 66 doc hygiene — estimator shipped (gated), operator runbook (docs).** Reconciles the prose docs with the now-shipped (gated-off) Phase 2 estimator. [docs/user-guide.md](docs/user-guide.md): the "homegrown sub-meter estimation … remains deferred" note flips to **shipped Sprint 66, off by default** (operator enables per env after validation). [docs/data-models.md](docs/data-models.md): `tenants.position_strategy` is no longer "created-not-used" (now **read by the estimator**, with the knob list), and the `asset_positions` `computed` source now has a **Sprint 66 writer** (gated off). [docs/operator-quickstart.md](docs/operator-quickstart.md): new **"Indoor positioning estimator (default-off)"** section — validate offline (`simulate_floor_positioning.py --validate`), seed dev (`--emit`), and enable (`POSITION_ESTIMATOR_ENABLED` / `POSITION_ESTIMATOR_INTERVAL_S`) with the per-tenant `position_strategy` knobs. Docs only.

- **Sprint 66 (Phase 2 part 4) — floor-positioning simulator + ground-truth validator (tooling).** New [scripts/simulate_floor_positioning.py](scripts/simulate_floor_positioning.py) closes the validation gap: `simulate_assets.py` sends single-reader reads with **random** RSSI and can't exercise triangulation. The new sim places assets at known floor `(x, y)` and emits reads to the **nearest K readers** with **RSSI = log-distance path loss**. `--validate` (default, **no API/DB**) builds the observation set and runs the **real `rssi_weighted_centroid`**, printing estimated-vs-placed error per asset + summary **RMSE** — the ADR-024 surveyed-ground-truth check. `--emit` back-fills the survey (site `coord_system` + reader `antennas` at known `(x, y)` + `device.site_id`), binds EPCs, and streams distance-based multi-reader reads to a live API (so dev can flip `position_estimator_enabled` and watch the worker + UI trail). Pure model (`rssi_from_distance`, `nearest_k`, `grid_readers`, `estimate_for_asset`) unit-tested in [tests/unit/test_floor_positioning_sim.py](tests/unit/test_floor_positioning_sim.py) (6), incl. a centered-asset recovery + a noiseless-RMSE band. **v1-read-based — not WM-gated** (distinct from the v2 *snap* simulator). `make check` green (1680).

- **Sprint 66 (Phase 2 part 3) — floor-position estimator DB adapters + gated worker (backend).** Concrete TimescaleDB implementations of the three pipeline ports in [src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/floor_position_source.py](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/floor_position_source.py): `TimescaleStrategySource` (tenants with a non-null `position_strategy`, parsed to `PositionStrategy`), `TimescaleObservationSource` (per-tenant RLS-scoped via `tenant_context`: floor sites → fixed sited readers → surveyed `antennas` → recent `tag_reads` → EPC→asset fusion, matching on `tag_reads.epc = binding_value` to avoid the hex-vs-URI gate bug), and `TimescalePositionWriter` (reuses Sprint 65's `TimescaleAssetPositionRepository` with `source='computed'`). The pure mapping helpers `resolve_antenna_xy` (exact-port → port-0 fallback) and `build_floor_observations` are unit-tested ([tests/unit/test_floor_position_source.py](tests/unit/test_floor_position_source.py), 6). The `FloorPositionWorker` is wired into [api/main.py](src/tagpulse/api/main.py) **gated off** behind the new `position_estimator_enabled` setting (default `False`) — the adapters need integration validation before the recompute loop writes `asset_positions(source='computed')` in production. `make check` green (1674).

- **Sprint 66 (Phase 2 part 2) — floor-position estimation pipeline orchestration (backend).** Wires the pure estimator to a recompute loop via small **ports** so the logic is unit-testable ahead of the DB adapters. New [src/tagpulse/services/floor_position_estimator.py](src/tagpulse/services/floor_position_estimator.py): `FloorObservation`, the `ObservationSource` / `PositionWriter` / `StrategySource` Protocols, and `FloorPositionEstimatorService.run_once(now)` — for each opted-in tenant it pulls recent observations over the `lookback_s` window, groups by `(site, asset)`, runs `rssi_weighted_centroid`, and writes one `asset_positions(source='computed')` row per asset (metadata records strategy/antenna-count/τ). New [src/tagpulse/workers/floor_position_worker.py](src/tagpulse/workers/floor_position_worker.py) `FloorPositionWorker` drives it on the **Option-C** cadence (`start`/`stop`/`_loop`/`run_once`, mirroring `DwellWorker`). Tests: [tests/unit/test_floor_position_pipeline.py](tests/unit/test_floor_position_pipeline.py) (7) cover one-fix-per-asset, site/asset separation, lookback-window query, min-antennas skip, no-op when no tenants opt in, and worker delegate + clean start/stop. **No DB adapters / not activated yet** — the concrete Timescale `ObservationSource`/`PositionWriter`/`StrategySource` + `api/main.py` registration are the remaining slice (gated until integration-tested); `[NEEDS WM]` `rpk` + v2 snap simulator stay deferred. `make check` green (1668).

- **Sprint 66 (Phase 2 part 1) — floor-position estimator core (backend).** The pure, I/O-free `rssi_weighted_centroid` estimator + the `position_strategy` config model, per [floor-position-estimation.md](docs/design/floor-position-estimation.md) and the [ADR-024](docs/adr/024-position-estimation.md) amendment. New [src/tagpulse/services/positioning.py](src/tagpulse/services/positioning.py): `PositionStrategy` (the `tenants.position_strategy` JSONB shape — `half_life_s` τ, `recompute_interval_s` D, `lookback_s`, `min_antennas`, `rssi_floor_dbm`), `AntennaObservation` / `PositionFix`, and `rssi_weighted_centroid(observations, *, now, config)`. The algorithm is **relative** (weight `(rssi − min + 1)`, no absolute calibration), **recency-decayed** (`· 0.5^(Δt/τ)`; τ→0 = last-one-wins), and **hull-bounded by construction** (a non-negative-weight centroid is a convex combination of the antenna coordinates), with strongest-tag-per-antenna dedup, `rssi_floor_dbm`/`lookback_s` filtering, a `min_antennas` gate, and honest confidence (geometry × freshness). Tests: [tests/unit/test_position_estimator.py](tests/unit/test_position_estimator.py) (11) validate the design's worked example (τ=3 → (14.5, 16.8); time-agnostic → (16.4, 18.3)), last-wins, single-antenna snap, hull containment, floor/lookback filters, min-antennas gate, per-antenna dedup, and JSONB round-trip. Pure logic — **no worker, no DB writes** (the recompute-tick pipeline that writes `asset_positions(source='computed')` is the next slice); the `[NEEDS WM]` `rpk` wire field + v2 snap simulator stay deferred. `make check` green.

- **Sprint 65 marked shipped (docs).** Flips the roadmap §Sprint 65 heading + status from *active* → *shipped* now that backend PR #120 and UI PR #95 are both merged. Docs only.

- **Sprint 65 (Phase 1) — BYO precomputed floor positions + asset floor-path (backend).** The first writer into the headless Sprint 59 `asset_positions` hypertable, per [floor-position-estimation.md](docs/design/floor-position-estimation.md). **`POST /assets/{id}/position`** ([assets.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/assets.py)) accepts a `FloorPositionCreate` (`site_id`, `x`, `y`, `z?`, `confidence` 0..1 with `allow_inf_nan=False` on coords, `recorded_at?` → server `now()` when omitted, `metadata?`) and writes one row with `source='precomputed'` via the new [`TimescaleAssetPositionRepository`](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/asset_positions.py); guards verify the asset is in the tenant (404) and the `site_id` belongs to the tenant (422, new `AssetPositionSiteError`), and `tenant_id` is always server-stamped so RLS (migration 051) blocks cross-tenant writes. **`GET /assets/{id}/floor-path`** returns `FloorPositionResponse[]` ascending by time with `since`/`until`/`source`/`limit` filters — the floor-frame counterpart to the lat/lon `GET /assets/{id}/path`. Every write audits `asset.floor_position_recorded`. `AssetService` gains `record_floor_position` / `list_floor_path` (wired with the position + site repos in [dependencies.py](src/tagpulse/api/dependencies.py)). Tests: [tests/unit/test_floor_positions.py](tests/unit/test_floor_positions.py) (7 — happy path + audit, default `recorded_at`, missing-asset, foreign-site 422, ascending + source filter, confidence/NaN schema rejection). `openapi.json` regenerated; `make check` green (1650 passed). The `CRS.Simple` trail-layer `[ui]` ships alongside in `TagPulse-UI`; Phase 2 (the `rssi_weighted_centroid` estimator) stays deferred.

- **Design — floor position estimation & asset path (docs, planning).** New [docs/design/floor-position-estimation.md](docs/design/floor-position-estimation.md) designs the two complementary writers into the headless Sprint 59 `asset_positions` hypertable so an asset can show a true floor `(x, y)` + movement trail (the gap left after Sprint 64's reader-snapped markers). **Phase 1 — BYO precomputed** (`source='precomputed'`): `POST /assets/{id}/position` + the shared `GET /assets/{id}/floor-path` read endpoint + a `CRS.Simple` trail layer. **Phase 2 — homegrown estimator** (`source='computed'`): the deferred ADR-024 `rssi_weighted_centroid`, **extended with a recency-decay weight** (half-life `τ`; `τ→0` = last-one-wins), hull-bounded with honest 1/2/3-antenna degradation, driven by a **server-side recompute tick (Option C)** decoupled from the wire `t=0` snap (so it runs off the existing v1-HTTP simulators), using **server ingest time** (no cross-reader clock sync) and a per-`(asset, antenna)` rolling buffer. The two knobs `half_life_s` (τ) and `recompute_interval_s` (D) land in the created-not-used `tenants.position_strategy` JSONB. Records the discussion decisions (D1–D6) and flags that any **v2 wire-format change (e.g. `rpk` peak-RSSI) + a v2 snap simulator are gated on WM protocol sign-off**. Design only — no code on the branch.

- **Chore — Sprints 58–63 doc backfill (docs).** Brings the canonical reference docs current with schema/UX that shipped in Sprints 59–63 but was never back-documented (sibling to the Sprint 64 pass). [docs/data-models.md](docs/data-models.md): adds the **`asset_positions`** hypertable section (Sprint 59 / migration 051 — created-not-written; estimator deferred), the **`tenants.position_strategy`** column (Sprint 59), and the **`tenants.logo_url` / `logo_collapsed_url`** branding columns (Sprint 60 / migration 054, base 036) + the corrected tenants migration list. [docs/user-guide.md](docs/user-guide.md): documents the Sprint 61 **`nav.placement`** capability (relocate a movable item to a different parent) on the `nav` leaf and the **Preferences → Menu** panel, and adds the default-hidden Sprint 63 **EPC (hex)** advanced column to the Tag Reads table. Docs only.

- **Chore — `tag-reads-missing.md` runbook (docs).** Adds [docs/runbooks/tag-reads-missing.md](docs/runbooks/tag-reads-missing.md), the per-device/per-tenant ingestion-gap triage decision tree (`mqtt_tap.py` → worker logs / `ContainerAppConsoleLogs_CL` → `tag_reads_near.py`) for the case where the broker is up, the worker is running, and the ingestion-freshness SLO is green but a specific operator says "I don't see my tag reads." Cross-links to [mqtt-outage.md](docs/runbooks/mqtt-outage.md) (fleet-wide stall), [wm-wire-format-v2.md](docs/runbooks/wm-wire-format-v2.md) (reject reasons), and [operational-tooling.md](docs/runbooks/operational-tooling.md) (the `scripts/azd-*` toolbox), and documents the `azd-job.sh` exit-code / `--update-only` / `--allow-stale` gotchas in one place. Listed under **Day-to-day ops → Incident response** in [docs/runbooks/README.md](docs/runbooks/README.md). Docs only.

- **Sprint 64 docs — user guide + data-models brought current (docs).** Reconciles the prose/reference docs with what Sprint 64 shipped. [docs/data-models.md](docs/data-models.md): adds `devices.site_id` (+ the previously-undocumented `mobility`), `sites.coord_system` (incl. `floorplan_image`), a new **`antennas`** table section, the floor-polygon-zone note on `zones`, and the new **Spatial** API schemas (`CoordSystem`, `GeoAnchor`, `AntennaUpsert`/`AntennaResponse`, `LocationDescriptor`) + `site_id`/`location` on the Device/Tag-Read schemas. [docs/user-guide.md](docs/user-guide.md): rewrites the stale "local `(x, y)` in a warehouse" note (now two tiers — `reader_bound` no-survey fallback vs. surveyed floor plan + placement + floor map), corrects the "reader location is derived / `indoor_position` lives in metadata" guidance (site is now first-class `device.site_id`; indoor position lives on `antennas`, and the stale `indoor_position` key is dropped from the metadata example), and adds the **Antenna / Temp / Humidity** columns to the Data Explorer table. Docs only.


- **Sprint 64 wrap-up — roadmap + design status (docs).** Marks Sprint 64 **shipped** in [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) (with the full backend #111/#112/#113 + UI #92/#93/#94 PR map), and flips the device→site **"blocker" note → resolved** in [fixed-reader-positioning-and-warehouse-map.md](docs/design/fixed-reader-positioning-and-warehouse-map.md) now that the accurate floor-polygon path shipped. Docs only.

- **Sprint 64 follow-up — device→site assignment + floor-polygon zone resolution (accurate D5 path).** Unblocks and implements the accurate zone path parked in [fixed-reader-positioning-and-warehouse-map.md](docs/design/fixed-reader-positioning-and-warehouse-map.md). Design: [device-site-assignment-and-floor-zones.md](docs/design/device-site-assignment-and-floor-zones.md). **(1)** Migration [055](migrations/versions/055_devices_site_id.py) adds a nullable **`devices.site_id`** FK (`ON DELETE SET NULL`) + index, with a **heuristic backfill** (a fixed reader in exactly one `reader_bound` zone inherits that zone's site); `site_id` is exposed on `DeviceCreate`/`Update`/`Response` and persisted, with a service-layer **cross-tenant guard** (a `site_id` from another tenant → 422). **(2)** New [`get_floor_zone_for_point`](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/sites_zones.py) resolves a floor-local `(x, y)` to the containing zone by reusing the coordinate-agnostic ray-casting `point_in_polygon` engine — on a floor-site, a zone's `polygon_geojson` *is* a floor polygon (no new column/kind), oldest-`created_at` wins. **(3)** New [`FloorZoneResolver`](src/tagpulse/api/services/floor_zone_resolver.py) chains device→`site_id` → site `coord_system` → antenna `(port→port-0)` position → point-in-polygon, all cached per query page; the tag-reads **location descriptor** now **prefers** it over the coarse `reader_bound` fallback when the device is sited, the site is a floor, and the antenna is surveyed. Tests: [test_floor_zone_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_floor_zone_resolver.py) (engine), [test_floor_zone_resolver_service.py](tests/unit/test_floor_zone_resolver_service.py) (chain + caching + fallbacks), the descriptor-preference case in [test_query_service.py](tests/unit/test_query_service.py), and the device-schema `site_id` round-trip. `openapi.json` regenerated. `make check` green (1643 passed). UI consumer (Site selector on the device form + implicit assignment on placement) ships alongside in `TagPulse-UI`.


- **Sprint 64 follow-up — `coord_system.floorplan_image` (backend).** Completes the Phase 1/2 deferral: a site's floor `coord_system` ([CoordSystem](src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py)) gains an optional **`floorplan_image`** field so the placement/map UIs can render an uploaded floor plan behind the grid (D4). It rides the existing `coord_system` JSONB — **no schema migration** (the repository already persists the whole dict). The value is either an operator-hosted **`https://`** URL (≤2048 chars) or an inline base64 **`data:image/(png|jpeg|svg+xml|webp|gif)`** URL capped at **~2 MB encoded** (no blob storage — mirrors the branding-logo precedent; the column stays a string so a future move to blob is non-breaking); anything else → 422. Tests in [test_sites_structured_schemas.py](tests/unit/test_sites_structured_schemas.py) cover data-URL/https acceptance, non-image/bare-string rejection, oversize rejection, and null/empty clearing. `openapi.json` regenerated. `make check` green (1630 passed). UI consumer (upload control + image backdrop) ships alongside in `TagPulse-UI`.

- **Sprint 64 Phase 0 — fixed-reader positioning backend contract.** Lands the headless [Sprint 59 spatial schema](docs/design/fixed-reader-positioning-and-warehouse-map.md)'s API surface so the UI placement/map phases have a contract to build against. Four additive pieces, no schema migration (all columns/tables already exist from migration 051): **(1) `coord_system` on the Site API** — new `CoordSystem` / `GeoAnchor` Pydantic models ([src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py](src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py)) with validation (positive extent, `extra="forbid"`, `origin_device_id` required iff `origin_anchor="device_id"`, lat/lon-ranged geo-anchor) exposed on `SiteCreate`/`SiteUpdate`/`SiteResponse` and persisted by [the site repository](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/sites_zones.py); `NULL` ⇒ geographic-only. **(2) Antenna placement CRUD** — `GET/PUT/DELETE /devices/{device_id}/antennas[/{port}]` ([src/tagpulse/api/routes/antennas.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/antennas.py) + [repository](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/antennas.py)) implementing the **port-0 model** (port 0 = the reader's nominal location, reusing the wire format's `an: 0 = unknown/muxed`; ports 1..N are radiators). Tenant isolation flows through the device FK (the `antennas` table has no `tenant_id`), so every method verifies device ownership; RBAC mirrors Sites & Zones (viewer read / admin write); a device-not-found vs antenna-not-found 404 split. **(3) `floor_to_geo` projection seam** ([src/tagpulse/core/coordinates.py](src/tagpulse/core/coordinates.py)) — equirectangular floor-`(x,y)` → `(lat,lon)` via the optional `geo_anchor`; shipped + tested now, consumed by no map yet (the designed-but-deferred unified-overlay seam). **(4) Tag-reads location descriptor** — `GET /tag-reads` now attaches a resolved `location` descriptor per read ([query service](src/tagpulse/api/services/query_service.py)): `kind="geo"` with lat/lon for mobile reads, `kind="floor"` with the resolved `reader_bound` zone id/name for fixed reads (one zone lookup per distinct device, cached per page), else `kind="none"` — so the UI's single "Location" column needs no client-side joins. `openapi.json` regenerated. `make check` green (1624 passed). The accurate D5 path (antenna-position → floor-polygon zone resolution) is deferred to a Phase 0 follow-up; the `reader_bound` fallback powers the descriptor today.

### Fixed

- **Devices showed `online` forever — Readers page now ages out stale connections (bug).** A device's `connection_state` is set to `online` by the ingestion writer on every read but was **never aged back to `offline`** when the device went quiet (MQTT can miss a disconnect), so the Readers page's **Connection** column showed `online` indefinitely — even though the dashboard "Readers" card (which requires a fresh `last_seen`) correctly read `0/N`. The card and the page disagreed. New shared helper [src/tagpulse/core/device_status.py](src/tagpulse/core/device_status.py) is now the single source of truth: a stored `online` whose `last_seen` is outside the 5-minute `ONLINE_WINDOW` resolves to an **effective** `offline`. The per-device API response ([`_to_response`](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/devices.py)) derives the effective state, and the dashboard ([dashboard.py](src/tagpulse/services/dashboard.py)) now imports the same `ONLINE_WINDOW`, so the "Readers" card and the Readers page agree on freshness. No schema/contract change (`connection_state` is the same field, now freshness-derived). Tests in [tests/unit/test_device_status.py](tests/unit/test_device_status.py) cover the freshness edge cases (fresh/stale/missing `last_seen`, window edge, non-`online` pass-through). `make check` green (1594).

### Added

- **Plan: fixed-reader warehouse map & coordinate UI — design doc (planning chore).** Scopes the "movable readers = lat/lon, fixed readers = floor-local `(x, y)`" ask into a design-doc-first plan. New [docs/design/fixed-reader-positioning-and-warehouse-map.md](docs/design/fixed-reader-positioning-and-warehouse-map.md) records that the **schema already exists** (Sprint 59 / migration 051: `antennas(x,y,z)`, `sites.coord_system`, `asset_positions`) but is **headless** — no API surface, no placement UI, no floor map — and that today's "XY grid" answer is to model areas as `reader_bound` zones with no coordinates. Decisions locked: **(D1)** grain is *layered* — per-antenna `(x,y)` stays source-of-truth, a reader's display coordinate = centroid of its antennas, **no `devices.position_*`** re-added; **(D2)** before the (still-deferred) trilateration estimator exists, asset markers **snap to the last reader/zone `(x,y)`**; **(D3)** map renders **pure floorplan first** via Leaflet `CRS.Simple` (floor units, no projection), with the `coord_system.geo_anchor` **seam designed explicitly** (a `floorToGeo` util + validation ship in v1) so a future unified mobile+fixed geographic overlay needs no data rework; **(D4)** an uploaded **floorplan image** renders behind the grid. **(D5)** zone resolution for fixed reads is a *layered fallback* — `reader_bound` (per-`device_id` config) stays the zero-survey default, but it collapses a multi-antenna reader's 2–8 antennas (which routinely span different areas) into one zone, so surveyed sites graduate to **antenna-position → floor-polygon** zones resolved by the *same point-in-polygon engine* as geofence (just in `CRS.Simple` units), converging fixed-reader and geofence zoning; **(D6)** 3D/`z` is **deferred** — `antennas.z` stays an optional estimator-only mount-height field and vertical needs (high-bay racking, multi-storey) are modeled as **discrete level/floor attributes**, never continuous `z`, with no 3D UI/map in scope. Also captures the **Tag Reads location-display** design (the chore's through-line): `location_source` (`gps`/`fixed`/`inferred`) discriminates two regimes in **one contextual "Location" column** — lat/lon for mobile, resolved **zone name** for fixed (coordinates are a *map* concern, not a per-row one, since a fixed read only means "antenna X heard it within range", not a measured point) — fed by a server-side **location descriptor** in the `GET /tag-reads` projection. Both map render modes are immediate/first-class (geographic for mobile/truck-fleet, `CRS.Simple` floor map for warehouse, switched per-site by `coord_system`); **geo-anchor stays deferred** behind a narrow trigger (one facility wanting mobile + fixed on a single canvas). Floorplan image is **optional, stored inline** (~1–2 MB base64 cap, no blob infra) with a **plain-grid fallback** from `coord_system.extent` when absent. Reader/antenna positions use the **port-0 model**: port 0 = the reader's nominal location (reusing the wire format's `an: 0 = unknown/muxed`), ports 1..N are radiators, and position resolves by **availability fallback** (port-N coordinate if surveyed, else port-0) — so a low-precision customer who treats "reader + all its antennas = one location" is just the **default reader-grain tier** (survey only port 0; the `an` value is retained on the read but ignored for positioning), and antenna-grain is an opt-in upgrade on the same data with no mode flag. The Tag Reads "Location" column resolves the fixed-read zone **live (query-time join)** so it shows the reader's *current* zone — a point-in-time/historical variant (denormalize `zone_id` at ingest) stays a deferred additive upgrade. All design-time open questions are resolved; remaining choices are implementation-time only. Docs/planning only; no code, schema, or API change on this branch.

- **Plan: Tag Reads page gains Antenna / Temperature / Humidity columns — design doc (planning chore).** Scopes the "Tag Reads is missing Antenna, Temperature, Humidity" ask into a design-doc-first plan. New [docs/design/tag-reads-sensor-columns.md](docs/design/tag-reads-sensor-columns.md) records that the data is **already in the API contract** — `reader_antenna` is a typed `TagReadResponse` field and temp/humidity live in the free-form `sensor_data` JSONB — so this is a **UI-only** rendering gap with **no backend/schema/`openapi.json` change**. The doc captures the **one non-obvious constraint**: the same physical value is written under **two different keys** depending on ingestion path — real edge devices (wire-format v2 / [mqtt_subscriber.py](src/tagpulse/ingestion/mqtt_subscriber.py) `_wm_sensor_data`) emit `temperature_c` / `humidity_pct`, while simulators & demo seeds ([sim_loop.py](scripts/sim_loop.py), [seed_alerts.py](scripts/seed_alerts.py)) emit `temperature` / `humidity` — so each column must resolve a **fallback chain** (`temperature ?? temperature_c`), not a single `dataIndex`. Decisions locked: static `°C`/`%` headers, sortable via explicit comparators, all three default-visible (registered in the ADR-032 `columns.tag_reads` config + `ColumnChooser`, not behind the Advanced toggle), with CSV-export parity; `battery_pct`/`cnt`, a catch-all sensor column, a chart-mode temp series, and °F handling are out of scope. Docs/planning only; no code, schema, or API change on this branch. Implementation lands as a separate PR in `TagPulse-UI`.

- **Tag Reads `EPC (hex)` column — system-default-hidden, WM tenant flips to hex (chore).** Pairs with the UI chore that adds an `EPC (hex)` column to the Tag Reads page so RFID-only fleets (e.g. WM) can read the raw wire-format hex instead of the decoded SGTIN URI. Rather than make it an `advanced` column (the "Advanced columns" toggle is all-or-nothing, so it couldn't isolate the hex from TID/user-memory), `epc_hex` is a **normal column hidden by the system default**: [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) `SYSTEM_DEFAULT_UI_CONFIG` now carries `columns.tag_reads.hidden = ["epc_hex"]`, so the readable `EPC` URI stays the canonical column for every tenant with no clutter, and a hex-preferring tenant **reveals** it by replacing that `hidden` list (ADR-032 list-replace merge). `WM_DEMO_PRESENTATION` does exactly that — `columns.tag_reads.hidden = ["tag_id", "epc", "epc_scheme"]` (revealing `epc_hex`, hiding the URI + scheme + the now-redundant `Tag ID`) while TID/user-memory stay default-OFF behind the Advanced toggle. No schema/contract change (runtime config constant only). Tests in [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py) updated: the system default hides `epc_hex`, and the WM resolve reveals it + hides the URI columns. `make check` green.

- **Sprint 63 — in-app configurable column visibility, Tier 2 (cross-device): merge-style `PATCH /ui-config/me` + granular reset (backend).** Tier 2 of the [configurable-column-visibility plan](docs/design/configurable-column-visibility.md) makes a user's per-table column choices persist **across devices** (the user layer of the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) four-layer resolve) without clobbering their other prefs. The blocker the design doc called out — `PUT /ui-config/me` replaces the user's prefs blob *wholesale*, and there's no endpoint to read the user's own unmerged layer — is solved with two new write surfaces in [src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py): (1) **`PATCH /ui-config/me`** deep-merges a *sparse* body into the stored prefs per leaf (nested dicts recurse; a **list is a leaf and replaces wholesale**, so `columns.<page>.hidden` is set, not unioned), so the column chooser writing `columns.<page>` no longer wipes the Preferences page's `cards`/`nav` choices — the merged result is re-validated against the §4 schema on every write so a stored doc can't drift out of shape; (2) **`DELETE /ui-config/me/columns/{page}`** is the granular "reset this table to team default" — it drops just `columns.<page>` from the user layer so that page re-inherits the tenant/role/system floor, leaving every other leaf (and other pages' column overrides) intact, and is idempotent (resetting an unset page is a 200 no-op). Both require a real user identity (403 on the X-Tenant-ID backward-compat path, same as `PUT /me`). Reuses the existing `user_ui_prefs` table — **no schema change**. [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) amended to **v1.3**: §2 now spells out the **two reset scopes** (whole-layer via `PUT {}` vs. one-leaf via `DELETE`) and the `PUT`-replaces / `PATCH`-merges write semantics; §5 gains both endpoints. [docs/data-models.md](docs/data-models.md) `user_ui_prefs` notes updated for the new write paths. [openapi.json](openapi.json) regenerated (+`PATCH`/`DELETE` operations). Coverage in [tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py): PATCH composes independent surfaces (column write preserves `cards`, and vice-versa), list-leaf replace semantics, empty-PATCH no-op, 422 on unknown/ill-typed keys + on a merge that would drift the schema, 403 without a user; DELETE resets one page while sparing others, idempotent no-op, and re-inherits the floor. `make check` green (1584 passed). The paired `TagPulse-UI` change (retire the Tier 1 `localStorage` path for a server-backed `useColumnVisibility` + a "reset to team default" control) ships alongside on PR [#89](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/89).

- **Plan: in-app configurable column visibility (two tiers) — design doc + roadmap (planning chore).** Scopes the "hide a column from its header + a 'show all' reset" ask (the Excel/Office grid pattern) into a design-doc-first plan. New [docs/design/configurable-column-visibility.md](docs/design/configurable-column-visibility.md) captures the building blocks already present (the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) `columns` leaf, `applyColumnConfig`, the cross-device `PUT /ui-config/me` path, and the Dashboard `localStorage` "Customize" precedent) and the **one non-obvious constraint** that shapes the whole feature: `PUT /ui-config/me` replaces the user's prefs blob *wholesale* and there is **no endpoint to read the user's own (unmerged) layer**, so a second write surface would clobber the existing `Preferences` (`cards`/`nav`) override, and a clean "reset this table to team default" isn't expressible without new plumbing. It separates the **two resets** ("show all" = user `columns.<page>.hidden = []`, overriding the floor via list-replace merge, vs. "reset to team default" = remove the user's leaf) and lays out a phased rollout: **Tier 1** (Sprint 62, `[ui]`-only) — a reusable per-page `ColumnChooser` + "Show all" persisted to `localStorage`, zero backend; **Tier 2** (Sprint 63, backend + `[ui]`) — cross-device persistence via a new merge-style `PATCH /ui-config/me` + a granular reset endpoint, carrying an **ADR-032 amendment** and an `openapi.json` regen. [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) gains the two planned sprint entries. Docs/planning only; no code, schema, or API change on this branch.

- **Simulator & demo-composer docs brought current (docs chore).** The recent composer additions had outrun the docs, so three docs are reconciled: (1) [docs/guides/demo-guide.md](docs/guides/demo-guide.md)'s "what gets seeded" table now lists **all ten** composer steps (was seven) — adding `seed_register_tags`, `seed_ui_config`, and `seed_branding` — and the static-vs-live **Tags total** expectation is corrected from "3" to "~43 (40 registered inventory EPCs + 3 transfer bootstrap)" to match the registration step; (2) a new **"Running the simulator against Azure dev"** section documents both the laptop (`TAGPULSE_API_URL` + `sim_loop.py`) and in-cluster (`scripts/azd-job.sh dev sim_loop.py`) paths, the dev-only `ENV` guard, and how to stop a run; (3) [scripts/README.md](scripts/README.md) gains a **Demo composer** step-by-step table (every `seed_demo_tenant.py` step → its script + purpose, with combined-only steps flagged) and the now-stale `register_inventory_tags.py` row is corrected to note it's **mostly superseded** by the automatic `seed_register_tags` composer step (and that registering hex tags does not by itself materialize stock items — the ingest-gate bug is separate). Docs only; no code change.

- **Demo Tags KPI reflects the real inventory fleet — composer registers inventory EPCs (chore).** A freshly-seeded demo showed **"Tags: 3"** on the dashboard — only the transfer-seeded tags. Root cause: the **Tags** KPI counts `tags`-registry rows (`status IN ('registered','active')`), but the inventory simulator streams real SGTIN-96 reads **without registering** their EPCs, and the asset simulator binds synthetic `urn:epc:sim:<name>` URIs (not hex, so not registry rows). The prior fix was a manual one-off ([scripts/register_inventory_tags.py](scripts/register_inventory_tags.py), flagged ⚠️ workaround) that didn't survive a reseed — so the count regressed to 3 every time `demo-wm-dc` was rebuilt across Sprints 59–61. New [scripts/seed_register_tags.py](scripts/seed_register_tags.py) registers the **exact** inventory units the seeder created — derived deterministically from the same scenario catalog + serial scheme `simulate_inventory._build_units` uses (`(product_idx+1)*100_000 + unit_idx`), uppercased to satisfy the `TagCreate.epc_hex` pattern — so the registered set equals the streamed set (no over/under-registration, no async-worker/read-timing dependency). It's wired into the demo composer ([scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py](scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py)) as a step gated on `profile.seed_inventory`, so **every** `seed_demo_tenant` run (`combined` + `inventory`) leaves the Tags KPI reflecting the inventory fleet; the asset-only profile (no inventory units) is skipped. Idempotent (409 = already registered). Coverage in [tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py](tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py): the derived EPC set matches `_build_units`' serial scheme per scenario (count parity, uppercase hex), the shim POSTs every EPC to `/tags` with `source='backfill'` + correct auth headers and tolerates 409s, and the step runs for inventory-seeding profiles only. `make check` green (1574 passed). Demo seed tooling only; no product code or schema change. (Asset tags remain `urn:epc:sim` bindings — non-hex by design, tracked via the asset binding API, not the tag registry.) Building on the branding-logo-upload chore, the WM-facing demo tenant (`demo-wm-dc` / "SuperMart Distribution Center") now seeds with a real brand kit instead of the bare display-name fallback. Two trimmed, retina-downscaled PNGs ship in-repo under [scripts/assets/](scripts/assets/) (`demo-supermart-logo-full.png` ≈200×32 wordmark, `demo-supermart-logo-collapsed.png` 32×32 mark — a teal storefront/"M" motif shared between them), so the brand travels with the repo: **no blob storage, no external hosting**. A new [scripts/seed_branding.py](scripts/seed_branding.py) shim reads the two assets at runtime, encodes them as base64 `data:image/png` URLs (each well under the backend's 96 KB cap), and `PATCH`es `/tenant/branding` with both logos + the teal accent `#14B8A6`. The composer ([scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py](scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py)) gains a `seed_branding` profile flag wired **only** to the `combined` WM tenant — the neutral cold-chain / asset-fleet demos keep the unbranded display-name fallback. Idempotent (PATCH last-writer-wins). Coverage in [tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py](tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py): bundled assets exist + are valid PNGs under the data-URL cap, the shim PATCHes both logos + accent with the right auth headers, and only the `combined` profile is branded. Demo seed tooling only; no product default or schema change.

- **Branding logo upload — two uploadable logos, no blob storage (chore).** An admin can now **upload** branding logos (instead of pasting an operator-hosted URL): a **full/expanded** wordmark for the 240px sidebar header and a **collapsed** square mark for the 64px rail. The images are stored inline as size-capped base64 `data:` URLs in the existing branding columns — **zero new infrastructure** (no Azure Blob, no upload endpoint, no SAS/CDN). Migration [054](migrations/versions/054_branding_logo_upload.py) widens `tenants.logo_url` `VARCHAR(2048)` → `TEXT` (so it can hold a data URL) and adds a sibling **`tenants.logo_collapsed_url`** `TEXT` column. [src/tagpulse/api/routes/tenant_branding.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/tenant_branding.py) gains a shared logo validator: a logo may be an `https://` URL (operator-hosted, ≤2048 chars) **or** a base64 `data:image/(png|jpeg|svg+xml|webp|gif)` URL capped at **96 KB encoded** (≈70 KB image — generous for an SVG wordmark or PNG icon, tiny on the row); anything else → 422. The new `logo_collapsed_url` is added to the `TenantBranding` / `TenantBrandingUpdate` / `PublicBranding` models, the `PATCH /tenant/branding` column loop (still PATCH semantics + audited), and the public `GET /branding/{slug}` payload. Because the column stays a *string*, a future move to operator-hosted URLs or blob is non-breaking (same field, different value). [openapi.json](openapi.json) regenerated. Coverage in [tests/unit/test_tenant_branding.py](tests/unit/test_tenant_branding.py): data-URL (PNG + SVG) accepted, oversized data-URL rejected, non-image data-URL rejected, https still accepted/capped, collapsed logo validated identically, and the read/public model shapes updated. `make check` green (1564 passed). UI consumer (file-picker upload + collapsed-sidebar render) ships alongside in `TagPulse-UI`.

- **Sprint 61 PR-E — WM demo seed adopts the entity-first nav.** Now that the UI consumes the entity-first IA + `nav.placement`, `WM_DEMO_PRESENTATION` in [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) gains a **`nav`** leaf: **Inventory is hidden** for the WM persona (`hidden: ["sec-inventory"]` — a *presentation* hide that keeps the demo's cold-chain inventory data/pages intact and reversible, **not** a `tracking_modes` capability change) and the entity sections are **ordered to match the wireframe** (`order: [sec-assets, sec-tags, sec-readers, sec-data-management, sec-alerts]`). Tag Reads keeps its registry-default placement (under Tags), so no `placement` override is needed. Data Management stays visible and the Tags dashboard card stays shown (the Sprint 60 reconciliation holds). The wireframe's fully-flat nav (sections collapsed to bare top-level links) remains a tracked follow-up — top items still render above sections — but the entity-first IA + this ordering get WM very close. Tests in [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py) + [tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py](tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py) pin the new `nav` leaf (Inventory hidden, Data Management kept, sections ordered, placement empty). Demo seed data only; no product default or schema change. `make check` green (1558 passed). Final piece of the Sprint 61 sequence (PR-A IA · PR-B schema · PR-C consume · PR-D Preferences · PR-E seed).

- **Sprint 61 PR-B — `nav.placement`: relocate a movable nav item to a candidate parent (ADR-032 §4 `nav`).** The Sprint 60 `nav` leaf could hide/reorder within the existing hierarchy but **not move an item to a different parent** — the one capability the entity-first IA needs (e.g. *Tag Reads* under *Tags* vs. pinned top-level; *Locations/Map* under *Assets* vs. their own section). [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) adds a curated **`MOVABLE_ITEMS`** registry — each movable item → its enumerated **candidate parents** (first = default) — and a **`placement`** sub-leaf on `NavConfig` (`{ item-key: parent }`). A new `@field_validator` enforces the **closed vocabulary**: a placement entry is valid only if the item is registered *and* the chosen parent is one of its candidates, else `ValidationError` → **422** on the `PUT /ui-config/*` write paths (same posture as the curated `labels` / `theme` catalogues). The reserved parent token **`"top"`** means "ungrouped top-level page". Each movable item resolves to **exactly one** parent (override → default), so mutual exclusion is structural — there is never a "checked in two places" state. `placement` deep-merges per-key across the four layers like every other leaf (a user who relocates one item inherits every other placement default). A `movable_default_parent(item)` helper exposes the default. Registry keys stay in lock-step with the UI nav registry. [openapi.json](openapi.json) regenerated (`NavConfig` gains the `placement` object). Coverage in [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py): default-empty, valid fold-through, unknown-item + non-candidate-parent rejection, per-item cross-layer merge, and a registry-integrity check (every default is a candidate); the two `/ui-config` route shape assertions updated for the new field. `make check` green (1558 passed). Pairs with the UI consumer (PR-C) and the Preferences "Menu" panel (PR-D).

### Changed

- **Dashboard sparklines — real activity series for the Readers / Assets / Tags tiles (Sprint 60).** Three of the four cards the WM demo shows had **flat** sparklines: [src/tagpulse/services/dashboard.py](src/tagpulse/services/dashboard.py) only ran real `date_bin` time-series for `reads-per-hour` and `alerts-open`; the other seven tiles (incl. `devices`, `assets-active`, `tags`) used `_flat_series` — a single point-in-time count repeated across every bucket, so the line never moved. The three count tiles WM surfaces now compute **genuine bucketed activity series** from `tag_reads`: `devices` → distinct active readers (`COUNT(DISTINCT device_id)`) per bucket, `tags` → distinct tags seen (`COUNT(DISTINCT tag_id)`), and `assets-active` → distinct assets seen, resolving each read's `epc_hex` through the asset binding that was **active at read time** (`asset_tag_bindings`, temporal `bound_at`/`unbound_at` match). The headline tile number stays the current total/state; the sparkline is the recent *activity* trend (the same number-vs-series split `reads-per-hour` already uses). The four tiles with no honest historical source (`locations`, `transfers-in-flight`, `recon-backlog`, `low-stock`) stay flat. A shared `_bucketed_series` helper now backs every real series (one place for the bucket/gap-fill/trend handling). New unit test ([tests/unit/test_dashboard_sparklines.py](tests/unit/test_dashboard_sparklines.py)) drives `get_sparklines` with a fake session that reconstructs the bucket boundaries from the query params, proving each query maps to the right tile (not swapped), the three tiles are genuinely non-flat, and the four sourceless tiles stay flat. No schema/API-shape change (`DashboardSparklines` is unchanged — only the data within). `make check` green (1551 passed).

- **Sprint 60 — reconcile `WM_DEMO_PRESENTATION` against the actual focus-group wireframes.** A pre-merge check of the seeded demo config against the four hand-drawn WM wireframes (`wm-feedback{1..4}`) surfaced two values that *contradicted* the sketches, so they're corrected in [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py): (1) the **Data Management nav section is no longer hidden** — every wireframe keeps it in the menu (it's the Asset/Tag/Reader CSV register/export + Categories + Labels destination), so the `nav.hidden = ["sec-data-management"]` override was wrong and is dropped (the `nav` leaf is now absent, i.e. system default); (2) the **dashboard card set now matches the wireframe's exactly four cards** — Readers · Assets · Tags · Alerts — by hiding the *other five* tiles (`reads-per-hour`, `locations`, `transfers-in-flight`, `recon-backlog`, `low-stock`) instead of the previous list that wrongly hid the **Tags** card the wireframe shows. The `Device`→`Reader` label skin, the TID/user-memory advanced columns, the sparkline card style, and the newest-first Tag Reads sort are unchanged (all confirmed consistent with the sketches). The wireframe's *flat* nav (Assets/Tags/Readers promoted to top-level, sections removed) is a structural redesign the `nav` leaf can't express and is tracked as a separate follow-up. Tests in [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py) + [tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py](tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py) updated to pin the reconciled values (Data Management visible, Tags card visible, five tiles hidden). Demo seed data only; no product default or schema change.

- **Fix the real tools-job hang: non-interactive `az` + a bounded log fetch (chore).** The recurring "the job *succeeded* but the wrapper runs for 20 minutes and never returns" symptom was **not** the cold start — it was [scripts/azd-job.sh](scripts/azd-job.sh)'s data-plane log step (`az containerapp job logs show`) hitting an **interactive extension-install prompt**: on a host where the `containerapp` CLI extension is absent, az prints `The command requires the extension containerapp. Do you want to install it now? (Y/n):` and **blocks on stdin forever** — invisibly, because the `$(…)` capture swallows the prompt. Every tools-job invocation (`seed_demo_tenant`, `smoke_setup`, `get_kv_secret`) inherited the hang. Three guards: (1) `export AZURE_EXTENSION_USE_DYNAMIC_INSTALL=yes_without_prompt` at the top of the script so az auto-installs the extension silently instead of prompting; (2) the data-plane log call now reads stdin from `</dev/null` so **no** az prompt can ever block the wrapper; (3) the data-plane fetch is wrapped in `timeout 25` (and the Log-Analytics-fallback query in `timeout 40`) so any future stall falls through to the bounded retry path rather than hanging. Infra/ops only; both validated with `bash -n` and a live end-to-end secret fetch (`EXIT=0`, value returned in seconds).

- **Batch Key Vault secret retrieval — fetch several secrets in one tools-job run (chore).** Pulling demo/test credentials was slow and looked broken: each [scripts/azd-kv-get.sh](scripts/azd-kv-get.sh) call cold-starts the in-VNet tools-job (~1–2 min, because the KV is `publicNetworkAccess=Disabled` per Sprint 23-B and the laptop can't reach it directly), so fetching a tenant's admin+editor+viewer keys meant **three** serial cold starts, and wrapping any of them in `export X=$(…)` hid all progress so a normal 90s run looked like a hang. [scripts/get_kv_secret.py](scripts/get_kv_secret.py) gains a **`--names a,b,c`** batch mode that fetches every named secret in a *single* job execution (sentinel-bracketed `name=value` lines; a missing secret is reported inline as `name=<NOT_FOUND>` instead of aborting the batch), and [scripts/azd-kv-get.sh](scripts/azd-kv-get.sh) gains two front-doors for it: **`--tenant <slug>`** (one job → the `tagpulse-<slug>-{admin,editor,viewer}-key` trio, printed as an aligned labeled table) and a generic **`--names <list>`** passthrough. The existing single-secret and `--list` paths are byte-compatible (single-secret still works in `$(…)`); the new batch modes print a multi-value table and are explicitly documented as *not* for command substitution. `scripts/` is outside the `make check` gate; both scripts pass `py_compile` / `bash -n` and the awk table formatter is unit-checked against values containing `=` and the `<NOT_FOUND>` placeholder.

- **Fix tools-job image drift — auto-refresh on deploy + a staleness guard (chore).** The dev `*-tools` Container Apps Job (which runs operator scripts like `seed_demo_tenant` / `smoke_setup` via [scripts/azd-job.sh](scripts/azd-job.sh)) was **never refreshed by the deploy workflow** — only `api` / `worker` / `migrations` were rolled out. Because `azd-job.sh` deliberately re-uses whatever image the job already carries, the job silently drifted to a **months-old image** (a Sprint-33 build), so newly-merged scripts (e.g. the Sprint 60 `seed_ui_config` step) ran *old code that looked like it succeeded*. Two fixes: (1) [.github/workflows/deploy-azure.yml](.github/workflows/deploy-azure.yml) now discovers the `*-tools` job and pins it to the same `tagpulse-api:<tag>` image on every deploy (optional step — skipped when an env has no tools-job, so non-dev envs are unaffected); (2) [scripts/azd-job.sh](scripts/azd-job.sh) gains a **staleness guard** that compares the job's image tag to the live api app's tag and refuses to run (new exit code `5`) when they differ, printing the exact `az containerapp job update` to refresh it — overridable with `--allow-stale`. Also hardened: the script now resolves `AZURE_SUBSCRIPTION_ID` from the azd env and `az account set`s to it, so a laptop whose default `az` subscription differs from the dev subscription no longer fails with a confusing `ResourceGroupNotFound` / empty Log-Analytics-workspace error. Infra/ops only; no app code.

- **Sprint 60 gap remediation (backend) — full WM presentation seed + docs hygiene.** After a gap audit of Sprint 60, captured the concrete WM-facing values as a canonical **`WM_DEMO_PRESENTATION`** constant in [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) — the demo's interpretation of the June WM focus-group asks expressed against the real nav-section / card / page keys (label skin `Device`→`Reader`; hide the operator-irrelevant *Data Management* nav section; hide the three technical dashboard cards `reads-per-hour` / `tags` / `recon-backlog`; sparkline card style; TID + raw user-memory advanced on Tag Reads; newest-first Tag Reads sort). It is **demo seed data, not a product default** — nothing is baked into `SYSTEM_DEFAULT_UI_CONFIG`. [scripts/seed_ui_config.py](scripts/seed_ui_config.py) now PUTs the **full** presentation (was: label skin only) via `PUT /ui-config/tenant`, still importing from the canonical constant so the demo can't drift. New resolver test proves `WM_DEMO_PRESENTATION` passes `validate_ui_config_override` and folds through the real four-layer merge (so the seed can never push a doc the schema 422s on); the composer shim test now asserts the full presentation is PUT. [docs/user-guide.md](docs/user-guide.md) gains a **Configurable UI & Preferences** section (the six leaves, the Preferences page, admin tenant/role defaults) plus updates to Dashboard (hide cards), Assets (Advanced columns), Data Explorer (TID/User Memory advanced), and Product detail (the §59.8 Units table). [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) §60 reconciled to record the closed gaps + remaining tail (in-app admin UI, `locked` leaf-pin, `metadata` column). `make check` green (1550 passed). Pairs with UI follow-ups (`sprint-60/ui-config-followups`).

- **Sprint 60 — roadmap status reconciliation: mechanism + WM values shipped, tail remaining (planning).** Audited the actual state of the sprint against its two-part scope (build the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) mechanism **and** apply the concrete WM-facing values). The mechanism is shipped end-to-end, `TagPulse-UI` now consumes five leaves — `labels`, `nav` (data-driven sidebar visibility/order), `cards` (`cards.dashboard` as the default layer beneath device-local personalisation), `theme` (reflected onto `<html>` data attributes), and `columns` (the **TID** + **User Memory** plumbing columns on the Tag Reads page are default-OFF behind an "Advanced columns" toggle) — on UI PR [#80](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/80), and the **WM-facing values are applied**: `WM_LABEL_SKIN = {"device": "Reader"}` is seeded onto the `combined` demo tenant via `PUT /ui-config/tenant` (backend PR [#93](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/pull/93)). **Remaining tail:** no list page renders a `metadata` column yet (so `columns.*.advanced` has nothing to cut there until it's added), and the `tables` leaf (default-sort) stays unconsumed. [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) line 4 + the §60 header now state this accurately. Doc-only; no code change.
- **Sprint 60 audit — Configurable-UI docs hygiene + ADR-032 acceptance.** Reconciled the docs with the shipped backend after the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) §7 5-step rollout (PR [#91](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/pull/91)). [docs/data-models.md](docs/data-models.md) now documents the two new storage surfaces it was missing: the `tenants.ui_config` JSONB column (tenant + role default layers; migration 053 added to the `tenants` migration line) and a new `user_ui_prefs` table section (the per-user override layer, `user_id` PK, sparse `prefs` JSONB, no-RLS rationale, migration 052). [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) moves **Proposed → Accepted (sprint-60/configurable-ui)** — the roadmap already records the contract as ratified — with a `v1.1` decision-history entry summarising the steps 1–5 backend rollout and naming the two remaining follow-ons (the deferred `locked` leaf-pin, and `TagPulse-UI` consumption of the resolved document). Doc-only; no code change.
- **Sprint 60 kickoff — merged "Configurable UI" + "Terminology + nav rework" into one sprint (planning).** The originally-separate roadmap items wanted the *same* capability — per-tenant/per-user UI configuration — so Sprint 60 now **builds the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) mechanism and applies the WM-facing values on top of it**, rather than splitting mechanism (dedicated sprint, TBD) from values (Sprint 60). [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) §60 rewritten: locked scope = config storage (`tenants.ui_config` JSONB + `user_ui_prefs`, four-layer System→Tenant→Role→User deep-merge) + the `GET/PUT /ui-config` API family (OpenAPI change) + label skins + column presets (`columns.*.advanced` / "Advanced columns" toggle) + configurable nav + the deferred §59.8 units table; rollout sequenced so user overrides land early. **Track 2 phase H (BYO position ingest + floor-map render) and the AssetList zone-fallback are deferred out of Sprint 60** to a later spatial sprint. Cross-repo (`sprint-60/configurable-ui` in both repos; backend PR [#91](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/pull/91), UI PR [#78](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/78)). Planning only; no code change yet.
- **Sprint 59 audit + status reconciliation (docs hygiene).** Audited the sprint against its phase pass bars: **Track 1 (Phases A–E) is complete** on PR [#89](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/pull/89) — profile-driven composer, scenario depth, multi-tenant `sim_loop` + heartbeat, and the docs split — every pass bar backed by a contract test (`test_combined_profile_matches_legacy_constants` proves the combined `demo-wm-dc` build stays byte-for-byte; `test_*_scenarios_are_registered`, `test_reset_known_slugs_cover_all_profiles`, and the baseline-equals-legacy checks cover the rest), `make check` green, CI green. **Track 2 (Phases F–G — spatial schema + EPC→asset fusion) is not yet started** (only the doc-only ADR-024 amendment landed; zero artifacts in `src/` or `migrations/`); §59.6 / §59.8 remain carried-in, unaddressed. Reconciled the now-stale status lines to say so: [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) §59 gains a status summary in the convention of the Sprint 58 header, and [docs/design/sprint-59-demo-scenarios.md](docs/design/sprint-59-demo-scenarios.md) `Status:` now distinguishes the complete Track 1 from the pending Track 2. Doc-only; no code change.
- **Sprint 59 re-themed to a two-track sprint: demo scenario depth + spatial foundation (planning).** The original §59 was demo-scenario depth only (split the combined `demo-wm-dc` tenant into purpose-built inventory + asset tenants). A re-evaluation concluded the real platform gap is **spatial**: the location model is GPS-biased, with no way to express *where an antenna sits on a floor* or *where an asset is in `(x, y)`*. Sprint 59 keeps Track 1 (demo depth, *compose-don't-rewrite*) and adds **Track 2 — spatial foundation (*lay the schema, defer the math*)**: a normalized `antennas` table holding per-antenna `(x, y, z)` (positioning is per-antenna, not per-device — a fixed reader fans 2–8 antennas across tens of metres of coax), `sites.coord_system`, an `asset_positions` hypertable with a `source` enum (`precomputed | zone | computed`, created-not-written-to in 59), and the **EPC→asset multi-binding fusion** lookup that backs zone-presence today and is step 1 of the future positioning pipeline. Zone/choke-point presence (from existing `tag_presence` + `subject_current_zone`) is the honest headline "where is X" answer. All RF positioning math — the `rssi_weighted_centroid` estimator and the `rpk` (peak-RSSI) wire-format change — is **deferred to a candidate Sprint 61 spike**; BYO-precomputed ingest (`POST /assets/{id}/position`) + floor-map render is **deferred to Sprint 60** (phase H); the configurable-UI framework (label skins + column presets + menu config) is pulled into its **own dedicated sprint**. [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) §59/§60 and [docs/design/sprint-59-demo-scenarios.md](docs/design/sprint-59-demo-scenarios.md) rewritten to carry both tracks. This entry **supersedes the original demo-only Sprint 59 kickoff note** — the terminology/nav re-slotting to §60 and the RSSI-as-OOS framing are folded in here. Planning only; no code change yet.
- **[ADR-024](docs/adr/024-position-estimation.md) amended (v2, Sprint 59) — indoor position estimation.** Three corrections surfaced by scheduling the schema half of this previously-deferred ADR: (1) **position moves `devices` → a normalized `antennas` table** (v1 put `position_*` columns on `devices`, the wrong grain for multi-antenna fixed readers; v2's wire format already carries the antenna port `an` per `(epc, antenna)` observation); (2) the **`PositionEstimator` contract becomes antenna-keyed + asset-grouped** (resolve EPC→`asset_id` via `asset_tag_bindings`, group an asset's 2–3 tags, take the strongest tag per `(asset, antenna)` = best-oriented face — defeats orientation nulls without phase hardware); (3) the reference algorithm is renamed `weighted_centroid_log_distance` → **`rssi_weighted_centroid`** (relative RSSI, bounded to the antenna convex hull, calibration-free; the per-tenant weight formula is `position_strategy` config, not hardcoded). `asset_positions.method` (free `VARCHAR`) becomes a constrained `source` enum. Status moved Deferred → Amended; Sprint 59 implements the schema + fusion, the estimator stays deferred. Doc-only.

### Fixed

- **Batch Key Vault retrieval actually works now — `azd-job.sh` stops mangling comma-bearing args (chore).** The Sprint-61 `--names a,b,c` / `--tenant <slug>` batch modes of [scripts/azd-kv-get.sh](scripts/azd-kv-get.sh) were dead on arrival: every batch call failed with `get_kv_secret.py: error: unrecognized arguments: …editor-key …viewer-key`. Root cause was in the wrapper, not the batch feature — [scripts/azd-job.sh](scripts/azd-job.sh) built the container `args[]` by **joining all script args with commas into one string and then re-splitting that string on commas** (`JOIN_ARGS` → `jq -Rc 'split(",")'`). Any arg whose *value* legitimately contains commas — exactly the `--names tagpulse-x-admin-key,tagpulse-x-editor-key,tagpulse-x-viewer-key` payload — got shattered into four args (`--names`, then three bare positionals), so `get_kv_secret.py`'s `argparse` rejected the extras. The wrapper now builds the JSON `args[]` **directly from the bash array, one element per arg** (`printf '%s\n' … | jq -Rnc '[inputs]'`), preserving each value verbatim; newline is a safe delimiter since script args never contain newlines, and it sidesteps `jq --args`' mis-parsing of values that start with `-` (e.g. `--names`). Purely client-side (the wrapper constructs the ARM PATCH locally), so the fix is live immediately with no redeploy — the deployed image already supports `--names`. Validated end-to-end: `scripts/azd-kv-get.sh dev --tenant test-corp` now returns all three admin/editor/viewer keys in a single tools-job run; single-secret and `--list` paths are unchanged. `scripts/` is outside the `make check` gate; verified with `bash -n` plus a live batch fetch.

 A unit with any `stock_movements` history hit the `stock_movements_stock_item_id_fkey` `ON DELETE RESTRICT` ledger FK (migration [021](migrations/versions/021_inventory_hardening.py)): the repo's `delete()` enforced only a *state* guard, so `force=true` bypassed it and went straight to `session.delete()` → `flush()`, raising an **uncaught `IntegrityError`** that surfaced as a 500 with a poisoned transaction (the route mapped `ValueError`→409 but not `IntegrityError`). New [ADR-031](docs/adr/031-stock-item-force-delete-ledger.md) settles the semantics: **`force=true` bypasses the *state* guard only, never the ledger** — a moved unit is immutable and must be *retired* (soft-deleted via `PATCH state=consumed`, which [scripts/cleanup_demo_stock_items.py](scripts/cleanup_demo_stock_items.py) already does), never hard-deleted. [`InventoryService.delete_stock_item`](src/tagpulse/api/services/inventory_service.py) now **pre-counts** referencing movements (via a new `TimescaleStockMovementRepository.count_for_stock_item`, mirroring the lot-delete precedent) and raises a typed `StockItemLedgerError` (a `ValueError` subclass carrying `movement_count`) **before** any DB delete — so the RESTRICT FK is never reached and the transaction never poisons. The guard is unconditional (independent of `force` and `state`). The route ([src/tagpulse/api/routes/inventory.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/inventory.py)) translates `StockItemLedgerError` into a **structured 409** whose `detail` is `{error: "stock_item_has_ledger", message, movement_count, remediation}`; the plain state-guard `ValueError` keeps its string-detail 409, and `force` still hard-deletes a never-moved `in_stock` unit (audited `stock_item.deleted`). Regression coverage in [tests/unit/test_inventory_service.py](tests/unit/test_inventory_service.py) (moved unit → `StockItemLedgerError`, ledger guard applies to a consumed item, unmoved force-delete succeeds + audits, state guard without force, missing item → False) and a route-level structured-409 assertion in [tests/unit/test_inventory_route_force_delete.py](tests/unit/test_inventory_route_force_delete.py).

- **Sprint 59 Track 1 Phase D follow-up — heartbeat cold-start no longer flakes on a freshly-booted host.** [scripts/sim_loop.py](scripts/sim_loop.py) `_devices_needing_heartbeat` treated a device with no recorded `last_emit` as last-emitted at `0.0`, then compared `now - 0.0 >= interval`. Because `now` is `time.monotonic()` (arbitrary origin), on a host whose monotonic clock is younger than the 4-min interval — e.g. a fresh CI runner — `now < interval`, so the cold-start "warm every reader at startup" branch wrongly returned an empty set and [tests/unit/test_sim_loop.py](tests/unit/test_sim_loop.py) `test_devices_needing_heartbeat_warms_all_at_startup` failed (passed on long-lived dev boxes). Now a missing `last_emit` is treated as unconditionally stale (`d not in state.last_emit or now - state.last_emit[d] >= interval`), independent of the monotonic origin. Behaviour-preserving on warm hosts; fixes the CI flake.

- **`devices_online` dashboard tile always read 0 (chore).** The Sprint 54 [`tagpulse.services.dashboard.get_summary`](src/tagpulse/services/dashboard.py) query required `connection_state == "connected"`, but the rest of the codebase ([`tagpulse.ingestion.service`](src/tagpulse/ingestion/service.py), [`tagpulse.repositories.timescaledb.devices`](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/devices.py), every test, and the `DeviceStatusUpdate` schema) writes `"online"` / `"offline"`. The strict-AND filter on `last_seen` + `connection_state` therefore always returned 0 for real-shaped data, even with a live simulator pumping reads. Pinned the literal to `"online"` to match the canonical writer, updated the docstring on [`DashboardSummary`](src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py) to match, and added the rationale comment next to the SQL filter. No schema change, no migration; the `devices` table values were already correct.

### Added

- **Sprint 60 — apply the WM label skin (`Device` → `Reader`) to the demo tenant (ADR-032).** Closes the long-standing gap where `WM_LABEL_SKIN` was *defined but never seeded*: the mechanism shipped and the UI consumes the `labels` leaf, but no tenant ever carried the value, so the demo never actually rendered `Reader`. New [scripts/seed_ui_config.py](scripts/seed_ui_config.py) shim `PUT`s `{"labels": {"device": "Reader"}}` to **`PUT /ui-config/tenant`** (the admin-gated tenant-default layer), importing the value from the canonical [`tagpulse.services.ui_config.WM_LABEL_SKIN`](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) registry rather than hardcoding it (so the demo can never drift from the backend's source of truth), and verifies the skin resolved in the response before returning. Wired into the demo composer ([scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py](scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py)) as a new gated step via a `DemoProfile.seed_ui_config` flag — **enabled for the WM-facing `combined` tenant only**; the neutral cold-chain / asset-fleet demos stay on system defaults so the `Device`→`Reader` simplification is a WM-specific value, not a platform-wide default. The admin API key Bearer-auths as the tenant admin, satisfying the route's `require_role("admin")`. Idempotent (the `PUT` replaces the tenant-default leaves wholesale). Coverage in [tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py](tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py): the shim PUTs the canonical skin to the right endpoint with the right auth headers, the composer-CLI-flag contract test now covers `seed_ui_config.py`, and the per-profile scoping is pinned (`combined` applies it, `inventory`/`asset` do not). `scripts/` is outside the `make check` gate; the gated test additions pass lint + the full suite (1549 passed). `make check` green.
- **Sprint 60 increment 5 — theme-variant catalogue: the curated `theme` leaf (ADR-032 §7 step 5).** Closes the rollout by curating the last free-form leaf, mirroring the increment-4 `labels` treatment. [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) adds two allow-list catalogues — **`THEME_VARIANTS`** (`default`, `operator`, `power`) and **`CARD_STYLES`** (`default`, `sparkline`) — and two `@field_validator`s on `ThemeConfig` so a `theme` override may only select a **registered** persona variant or card style; an unknown value is a `ValidationError` → **422** on the `PUT /ui-config/*` write paths, never a silently-stored string. This realises the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) §4 intent — `theme.cardStyle` "rides ADR-029 tokens: 2–3 curated variants (sparkline is one), **not unbounded styling knobs**" — and the UI maps each catalogued value onto its [ADR-029](docs/adr/029-ui-design-tokens.md) design tokens. Both catalogues lead with `"default"` (today's UI) and the system default stays `default`/`default`, so configuring nothing is unchanged; both are additive tuples (a new approved variant/style ships as an entry, never a fork). **Latent-bug fix surfaced by the new route test:** a custom-validator `ValueError` lands in pydantic's error `ctx` carrying the original exception object, which is **not JSON-serializable** — the three `PUT /ui-config/*` handlers in [src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py) passed `exc.errors()` straight into the 422 `detail` and would have 500'd on any custom-validator rejection (the increment-4 `labels` validator shared this latent fault; no route test had exercised it). All three now use `exc.errors(include_context=False)`, dropping the unserializable context while keeping the human-readable `msg`. [openapi.json](openapi.json) regenerated (the `ThemeConfig` schema is structurally unchanged — `variant`/`cardStyle` stay `str`, validated at the model layer — only the description updates). Coverage extends [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py) (catalogue contents, every registered value accepted, unknown variant/card-style + override rejection, sparse theme override resolves with the sibling falling through) and [tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py) (`PUT /ui-config/me` unknown-variant → 422). With this the ADR-032 §7 rollout is complete; only the `locked` leaf-pinning flag stays **deferred** (it earns its complexity once the tenant/role floor layers are in real use).
- **Sprint 60 increment 4 — label skins: the curated `labels` registry + validation (ADR-032 §7 step 4).** Gives the previously free-form `labels` leaf real meaning, closing the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) §6.1 gap (the one leaf with no curation). [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) adds **`LABEL_KEYS`** — a curated registry mapping each skinnable entity/nav term to its canonical default display label (`device`→`Device`, `telemetry`→`Telemetry`, `asset`, `tag`, `tagRead`, `zone`, `site`, `lot`, `stockItem`, `alert`, `rule`), grounded in the primary entities of [docs/data-models.md](docs/data-models.md); the set is additive (a new skinnable term ships as a registry key, never a fork). The registry does double duty: (1) it is the **allow-list** a `labels` override is validated against — a new `@field_validator("labels")` on `UiConfig` rejects any unregistered key, so a typo'd or behaviour-smuggling label key is a `ValidationError` → **422** on the `PUT /ui-config/*` write paths rather than silently stored; (2) it is the **bottom layer** of the `labels` merge — `UiConfig.labels` now defaults to the full registry (`default_factory`), so the resolved `GET /ui-config` always carries the **complete** effective label map (canonical defaults overlaid with overrides) and the UI reads one authoritative `labels[key]` instead of re-deriving defaults client-side. Sparse override semantics are preserved (`validate_ui_config_override({"labels": {"device": "Reader"}})` still persists only `{"labels": {"device": "Reader"}}`, so every other term falls through). The system default `labels` = the canonical defaults — which *are* today's UI terms, so configuring nothing still reproduces today's UI byte-for-byte. **`WM_LABEL_SKIN = {"device": "Reader"}`** captures the one WM-facing value decided for Sprint 60 ([ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) §4); it is applied **per-tenant** via `PUT /ui-config/tenant` (or the demo seed), **not** baked into the system default, and the `Telemetry` rename stays TBD-with-WM so it is intentionally not skinned. [openapi.json](openapi.json) regenerated (the `UiConfig` schema is structurally unchanged — `labels` stays `dict[str, str]` — only the description updates). Coverage extends [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py) (registry default, sparse re-skin keeps the catalogue, WM skin resolves, unknown-key `ValidationError`, sparse-override persistence) and [tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py) (resolved `GET` carries the full map, tenant-default skin folds with siblings preserved). The `locked` leaf-pinning flag and the theme/`cardStyle` variant catalogue (§7 step 5) stay **deferred**.
- **Sprint 60 increment 3 — `tenants.ui_config` + the tenant & role default layers (ADR-032 §7 step 3).** Completes the four-layer fold by lighting up the **two middle layers** beneath the per-user overrides: a tenant-wide default and a per-role default, both admin-managed. New migration [migrations/versions/053_tenant_ui_config.py](migrations/versions/053_tenant_ui_config.py) adds a nullable **`tenants.ui_config`** JSONB column — **resolving the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) D8 storage question for the tenant/role tiers by the existing tenant-JSONB precedent** (`tile_provider` / `rate_limit_overrides` / `position_strategy`), in deliberate contrast to the dedicated `user_ui_prefs` table the per-*user* tier uses. The blob holds the **tenant-default leaves at the top level** and a reserved **`roles` sub-object** keyed by role name (e.g. `{"theme": {…}, "roles": {"viewer": {…}}}`), documented in the migration + ORM docstrings; it carries **no RLS** — the request path already writes `tenants` (the existing `PATCH /tenant/config`) without the `app.current_tenant_id` GUC, so an RLS policy keyed on the unset GUC would error, and every read is by the explicit `tenant_id` PK. SQLAlchemy `TenantModel.ui_config` is added to [src/tagpulse/models/database.py](src/tagpulse/models/database.py); persistence is a new [src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/tenant_ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/tenant_ui_config.py) `TenantUiConfigRepository` (`get`, `set`).
