[src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) gains `tenant_role_layers(stored, role)` which splits the stored blob into the ordered `[tenant-default, role-default]` layer list the resolver folds (tenant beneath role beneath user). [src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py) now folds **all four layers** in `GET /ui-config` (System→Tenant→Role→User), and adds two **admin-gated** (`require_role("admin")`) write paths: **`PUT /ui-config/tenant`** sets the tenant-default leaves (preserving the existing `roles` sub-object, empty body clears them) and **`PUT /ui-config/role/{role}`** sets one role's layer (`role` constrained to admin/editor/viewer → 422 otherwise; empty body removes that role; sibling roles + tenant defaults preserved). Both reuse `validate_ui_config_override` (so an admin can't smuggle a `roles` key through the tenant endpoint — it's `extra="forbid"`), are audited (`ui_config.tenant.update` / `ui_config.role.update`), and return the caller's freshly-resolved document. **This lights up "Reset to team default"** — a user-override delete now falls through to a meaningful tenant/role default rather than the bare system default. [openapi.json](openapi.json) regenerated with the two new paths. The `locked` leaf-pinning flag stays **deferred** to a later increment. Coverage: [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py) (the `tenant_role_layers` split — none/tenant-only/tenant+role/role-absent/role-only/empty-role/round-trip) and [tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py) (four-layer GET precedence, both admin PUTs incl. role-subtree preservation, empty-body clears, admin-gating 403, unknown-role + unknown-key 422).
- **Sprint 60 increment 2 — `PUT /ui-config/me` + the per-user override layer (ADR-032 §7 step 2).** Lands the *write path and persistence* the read-only step 1 deferred: a viewer's own presentation overrides now fold into the resolved document, and **user overrides alone satisfy the bulk of the WM ask** (hide TID/`metadata`, hide cards, pick a card style, sort default) without any tenant/role admin. New migration [migrations/versions/052_user_ui_prefs.py](migrations/versions/052_user_ui_prefs.py) creates the **`user_ui_prefs`** table (`user_id` UUID **PK** FK→`users.id` `ON DELETE CASCADE`, `tenant_id` FK→`tenants.id`, `prefs` JSONB `NOT NULL DEFAULT '{}'`, `updated_at`), **resolving the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) D8 storage question by precedent: a dedicated keyed table (sibling of `users`), not tenant-JSONB**. It carries **no RLS** — deliberately, and documented in the migration + ORM docstrings: the request path never sets the `app.current_tenant_id` GUC (only `tenant_context()` and the MQTT subscriber do), so an RLS policy keyed on the unset GUC would error on every request-path read; the table mirrors its `users` sibling and is queried by the globally-unique `user_id` PK. SQLAlchemy `UserUiPrefsModel` is added to [src/tagpulse/models/database.py](src/tagpulse/models/database.py); persistence is a new [src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/user_ui_prefs.py](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/user_ui_prefs.py) `UserUiPrefsRepository` (`get_for_user`, idempotent `upsert` via `INSERT … ON CONFLICT (user_id) DO UPDATE`). [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) gains `validate_ui_config_override(payload)` — validates the body against the `extra="forbid"` schema then returns a **sparse** `model_dump(by_alias=True, exclude_unset=True)` (only the keys the caller set, canonical camelCase) so the per-leaf deep-merge fall-through is preserved (a user who hides one column still inherits every other leaf). [src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py): `GET /ui-config` now folds the caller's stored override (when `user_id` is present — the X-Tenant-ID back-compat path has no user identity and still gets the system default) via a `_resolve_for_user` helper; new `PUT /ui-config/me` (`response_model=UiConfig`) validates → upserts → returns the freshly resolved document, mapping a schema `ValidationError` to **422** and refusing a missing user identity with **403**. **"Reset to team default" = `PUT` an empty body** (`{}` → empty override row → resolves to the layer below). [openapi.json](openapi.json) regenerated with the new `PUT /ui-config/me` path. Tenant/role default layers + the `locked` compliance pin stay **deferred to increment 3**. Coverage: [tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py) (GET folds a stored override, GET with no user identity = system default, PUT upserts a sparse override + resolves, PUT empty body resets, PUT rejects unknown key / bad leaf type = 422, PUT with no user identity = 403) and `validate_ui_config_override` cases in [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py) (sparse dump keeps only set keys, snake→camel normalization, empty→empty, unknown/bad-leaf rejection, round-trips through `resolve_ui_config`).
- **Sprint 60 increment 1 — `GET /ui-config` + the server-side presentation-config resolver (ADR-032 §7 step 1).** Lands the *mechanism's first slice*: a schema-validated UI config document and the deep-merge resolver, exposed read-only — **no DB, no persistence, no write path yet** (those are steps 2–3). New [src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/services/ui_config.py) defines the [ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) §4 leaf schema as `extra="forbid"` Pydantic v2 models (`UiConfig` → `labels` / `theme` / `nav` / `cards` / `columns` / `tables`, with `columns.*.advanced` carrying the default-OFF TID/metadata surface and `tables.*.defaultSort` the sort spec), wired to the **camelCase wire keys** via `alias` + `populate_by_name=True` so the JSON contract matches the ADR exactly while Python stays snake_case. `SYSTEM_DEFAULT_UI_CONFIG = UiConfig()` is intentionally **empty — today's UI, byte-for-byte unchanged**. `deep_merge(base, override)` does the per-leaf recursive System→Tenant→Role→User fold (nested mappings recurse, lists/scalars replace wholesale, no input mutation) and `resolve_ui_config(overrides=())` validates the merged document; step 1 calls it with **no overrides**, so every authenticated caller gets the system default. New [src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/ui_config.py) serves it at `GET /ui-config` (`response_model=UiConfig`, camelCase out); the `get_current_user` dependency is already wired in so steps 2–3 can fold the caller's role/user layers **without an endpoint-signature change**. Registered in [src/tagpulse/api/main.py](src/tagpulse/api/main.py); [openapi.json](openapi.json) regenerated with the new path + `UiConfig` schema family. The `locked` flag and write-path validation are **deliberately deferred** (no tenant/role/user layers exist yet — no speculative code). Coverage: [tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_resolver.py) (system-default shape, `extra="forbid"` rejection at top level + leaf, camelCase round-trip, advanced-columns leaf, bad sort-dir rejection, `deep_merge` precedence / list-replace / no-mutation, `resolve_ui_config` layering + reset-via-absent-layer) and [tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py](tests/unit/test_ui_config_route.py) (GET returns system default, serialises camelCase, requires auth). `make check` green.
- **[ADR-032](docs/adr/032-configurable-ui.md) — Configurable UI: presentation config as a per-viewer projection (proposed, chore).** Responds to the June 2026 WM focus-group wireframes (non-technical operators asking to hide plumbing columns like TID + the `metadata` JSONB, hide unused dashboard cards, sparkline card visuals, sort-by-header, free search). Reframes "make it simpler" away from *build a simpler app* toward **one sophisticated engine rendered as a per-viewer projection** — the governing invariant is **configure _presentation_ (visibility, order, density, theme, presets), never _behavior/semantics_** (the line [ADR-021](docs/adr/021-configurable-sensing-events.md) already draws for sensing-event behavior). Defines a single schema-validated UI config document (label skins / theme / nav / cards / columns / tables) resolved server-side across a **System→Tenant→Role→User deep-merge** (per-leaf, with "Reset to team default" = delete the user-override row, and a `locked` flag for compliance hides); stores it on the existing tenant-JSONB precedent (`tile_provider` / `rate_limit_overrides` / `position_strategy`) as `tenants.ui_config` + a small `user_ui_prefs` table — **resolving the open D8 storage question (tenant-settings JSONB vs. dedicated tables) by precedent: JSONB**; serves it via one resolved `GET /ui-config` endpoint family. The TID/metadata ask is handled by `columns.*.advanced` (default-OFF, revealed by an "Advanced columns" toggle — default-hidden, never deletion). Builds on [ADR-029](docs/adr/029-ui-design-tokens.md) (theme/card-style tokens) and [ADR-030](docs/adr/030-list-page-column-filters.md) (sort/search/column-filter convention) as the persistence + resolution layer they were missing. 5-step rollout where **user overrides (step 2) alone satisfy the bulk of the WM ask**. Doc-only; no code change.
- **Sprint 59 Track 2 (Phases F–G) — spatial foundation schema + EPC→asset fusion (§59.9, §59.10).** Lands the *schema and the lookup*, defers the *math* — exactly the scope the amended [ADR-024](docs/adr/024-position-estimation.md) calls for. New migration [migrations/versions/051_spatial_foundation.py](migrations/versions/051_spatial_foundation.py) creates: a normalized **`antennas`** table holding per-antenna `(x, y, z)` + `gain_dbi` + `label` keyed `UNIQUE(device_id, port)` (positioning is **per-antenna, not per-device** — a fixed reader fans 2–8 antennas across tens of metres of coax; tenant isolation flows through the `device_id` FK, no `tenant_id`/RLS of its own, faithful to the ADR DDL); a **`sites.coord_system`** JSONB column for the floor-plan transform; an **`asset_positions`** TimescaleDB hypertable (`id + time` composite PK — the v1 DDL sketch omitted a PK, but the hypertable + ORM need a partition-keyed one, same precedent as `external_locations`; `asset_id` carries **no FK**, matching the established hypertable convention) with a `source` CHECK enum (`precomputed | zone | computed`), a `confidence BETWEEN 0 AND 1` check, RLS tenant isolation, and per-asset / per-site time-descending indexes; and a **`tenants.position_strategy`** JSONB placeholder (D8 "tenant-settings JSONB" shape). **Nothing writes to `asset_positions` in Sprint 59** — `precomputed` is Sprint 60 BYO ingest, `computed` is the Sprint 61 estimator, `zone` is the Sprint 60 retrieval fallback. SQLAlchemy `AntennaModel` / `AssetPositionModel` + the two new columns are added to [src/tagpulse/models/database.py](src/tagpulse/models/database.py). The **EPC→asset multi-binding fusion** lookup ships as [src/tagpulse/services/asset_fusion.py](src/tagpulse/services/asset_fusion.py) `AssetFusionService` (`resolve_asset`, `active_tags`, batch `fuse`) backed by a new `TimescaleAssetTagBindingRepository.list_active_by_values` ([src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/assets.py](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/assets.py)) — a multi-tag asset resolves from **any** of its bound EPCs (any face an antenna can see) and `bound_at` / `unbound_at` history is honoured so a rebound tag maps to its current owner. Unit coverage in [tests/unit/test_asset_fusion.py](tests/unit/test_asset_fusion.py) pins 1-tag / 3-tag / rebound / batch-grouping / tenant-isolation (7 tests). Migration verified clean up → down → up against the live TimescaleDB; `make check` green. **Honest scope:** no RF positioning math, no `rssi_weighted_centroid` estimator, no `rpk` peak-RSSI wire-format change, and no new endpoint — all deferred per the ADR amendment.
- **Sprint 59 Track 1 Phase E — demo docs split into a combined overview + two domain tours (§59.5).** [docs/guides/demo-guide.md](docs/guides/demo-guide.md) is restructured from a single combined-tenant walkthrough into the **shared hub** for all three demo tenants: a new "Three demo tenants, one composer" table maps each tenant → slug → profile / `make` target → tour link, the TL;DR lists `make demo-tenant` / `demo-inventory` / `demo-asset` plus all three resets, and the combined `demo-wm-dc` content is demoted under a "The combined tenant" divider so the **shared mechanics** (the continuous simulator, a new **"Driving several tenants at once"** section documenting the Phase D `$SIM_TENANTS` multi-tenant `slug:key` driving + aggregate rate split + per-reader heartbeat + `make sim-start` accepting either env var, reset / restart, troubleshooting, dev tips) live in one place that the two domain tours link back to. Two new focused tours: [docs/guides/demo-inventory-tour.md](docs/guides/demo-inventory-tour.md) (cold-chain `demo-inv-coldchain` — identity + UUID, the 13-lot multi-category catalog table, the 5-zone Receiving→…→Quarantine pipeline, the near-expiry / low-stock / quarantine-divert business events, and a 6-click tour) and [docs/guides/demo-asset-tour.md](docs/guides/demo-asset-tour.md) (returnable `demo-asset-fleet` — identity + UUID, the 7-zone geofenced yard, the 3-category 24-asset roster table, the geofence-breach `FORK-06` / gone-dark `IBC-08` / in-flight-transfer events, and a 6-click tour). Each tour documents which composer steps its profile **drops** (inventory drops the asset roster + transfer; asset drops the inventory catalog) and links back to the hub for shared mechanics. The **per-domain reset** section now spells out `make demo-inventory-reset` / `demo-asset-reset` and that only the combined reset removes the shared `demo-wm-recipient`. **Honest scope:** the cold-chain tour carries the §59.6 caveat — catalog / lots / zones / quarantine topology seed correctly, but live **Stock Levels** population still depends on the ingest auto-create gate fix; the asset tour is unaffected (direct EPC→asset bindings, no ingest gate). Doc-only; no behaviour change, `make check` unaffected.
- **Sprint 59 Track 1 Phase D — multi-tenant `sim_loop` + reader heartbeat (§59.4, §59.7).** [scripts/sim_loop.py](scripts/sim_loop.py) can now drive **several demo tenants from one process** via a new `--tenants slug:key,slug:key,…` flag (or `$SIM_TENANTS`); each entry's tenant UUID is derived with the same deterministic `uuid5("<slug>.tagpulse.local")` the composer uses, so no ids are duplicated across scripts. Each tenant gets its **own API key, token bucket, and `SimState`** (independent device roster, outage schedule, and alert cadence). The `--rate` ceiling is now an **aggregate across all driven tenants** — the hard 600/min cap is preserved and the requested aggregate is split evenly (`aggregate / N`) so adding tenants never raises total load on the shared dev cluster. The legacy single-tenant path is unchanged and remains the default: with no `--tenants`, the loop runs exactly one tenant from `--tenant-id` / `--api-key` (the combined `demo-wm-dc` build stays byte-for-byte). **§59.7 fix — idle tenants no longer fall to "0 active devices":** a per-reader heartbeat (`_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL_SECONDS = 4 min`, comfortably under the Dashboard's 5-min `devices_online` window) emits one keep-warm read per stale reader each minute, so a low-traffic or freshly-seeded tenant keeps every reader `online` between organic reads. New [Makefile](Makefile) `sim-start` accepts either `$SIM_TENANTS` (multi-tenant) or `$TAGPULSE_API_KEY` (single); [docker-compose.yml](docker-compose.yml) passes `SIM_TENANTS` through to the `sim` service. Unit tests in [tests/unit/test_sim_loop.py](tests/unit/test_sim_loop.py) pin the deterministic slug→UUID mapping, `--tenants` parsing (multi/colon-in-key/duplicate/garbage rejection), the aggregate rate split, per-tenant `SimState` isolation, and the heartbeat staleness logic (cold-start warms all, fresh excluded, offline excluded). **Honest scope:** this delivers the per-tenant keys + per-tenant caps + heartbeat. Auto-sourcing each tenant's key from Key Vault is the existing dev-cluster `azd-job.sh` path; locally the operator supplies keys via `$SIM_TENANTS` (printed by the matching `make demo-*` runs). `scripts/` is outside the `make check` gate; the gated `test_sim_loop.py` additions pass lint + typecheck.
- **Sprint 59 Track 1 Phase C — scenario depth (richer per-domain simulator presets).** Each domain simulator gains a `--scenario` flag backed by a `SCENARIOS` registry; the composer's `DemoProfile` now carries `inventory_scenario` / `asset_scenario` and forwards them. `combined` runs both simulators in their `baseline` preset, which reuses the legacy Sprint-58 module objects verbatim (`simulate_inventory.SCENARIOS["baseline"]` *is* the original `CATALOG` / `ZONE_PIPELINE` / `SITE_NAME`; `simulate_assets.SCENARIOS["baseline"].is_topology is False` keeps the unchanged Sim-Pallet flow) — so `make demo-tenant` stays byte-for-byte. The deep presets: [scripts/simulate_inventory.py](scripts/simulate_inventory.py) `coldchain` adds a ~13-row multi-lot cold-chain catalog (pharma/vaccine/biologic + food/dairy/produce/dry-goods, multiple lots per SKU incl. near-expiry + critical-expiry + low-stock rows), a 5-zone pipeline with a dedicated **Quarantine / Hold** zone, and a quarantine-divert path; [scripts/simulate_assets.py](scripts/simulate_assets.py) `fleet` stands up its own geofenced site (7 zones incl. an **Authorized Area** + **Yard / Exit**), 3 returnable categories, a 24-asset named roster (forklifts / totes / IBCs), and a bounded movement pass that drives zone transitions plus a deliberate **geofence breach** (one asset routed to the exit zone) and **gone-dark** (one asset never read) narrative. Contract tests in [tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py](tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py) pin that every profile's scenario name resolves to a registered preset, that `combined` uses `baseline` for both, that the domain profiles select `coldchain` / `fleet`, and that each `baseline` preset still equals the legacy constants. **Honest scope:** this delivers the scenario *data + plumbing*. The asset-fleet tenant's Assets / Zones / zone-changed pages populate cleanly (direct EPC→asset bindings, no ingest gate); the cold-chain tenant's catalog, lots, zones, and quarantine topology seed correctly, but **live Stock Levels population still depends on the §59.6 ingest auto-create gate fix** (the composer seeds inventory with `--seed-only`, and the tag-registry gate blocks stock-item auto-create until tags are promoted). `scripts/` is outside the `make check` gate; the gated test additions pass lint + typecheck.
- **Sprint 59 Track 1 Phase B — profile-driven demo composer (three tenants from one script).** [scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py](scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py) gains a `DemoProfile` registry + a `--profile {combined,inventory,asset}` flag (default `combined`). `combined` reuses the frozen Sprint-58 constants verbatim — same `demo-wm-dc` slug, deterministic `uuid5` id, admin email, and KV secret name — so `make demo-tenant` runs the identical seven steps in the identical order (byte-for-byte unchanged). The two new profiles stand up **purpose-built per-domain tenants** whose identity is deterministic `uuid5("<slug>.tagpulse.local")` like the original: `inventory` → `demo-inv-coldchain` (cold-chain inventory story — toggles off the asset roster + cross-tenant transfer) and `asset` → `demo-asset-fleet` (returnable / high-value asset-fleet story — toggles off the inventory catalog). The composer's step counter renumbers to the enabled steps. [scripts/reset_demo_tenant.py](scripts/reset_demo_tenant.py) gains `--slug {demo-wm-dc,demo-inv-coldchain,demo-asset-fleet}` (the deterministic tenant UUID is derived from the slug); the shared `demo-wm-recipient` tenant is auto-included only for the combined build so a per-domain reset can't orphan a recipient another demo shares. New [Makefile](Makefile) targets `demo-inventory` / `demo-asset` (seed) and `demo-inventory-reset` / `demo-asset-reset` (teardown). Contract tests in [tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py](tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py) pin the `combined`-profile==legacy-constants identity, deterministic+distinct per-profile UUIDs, the domain step toggles, and that every composer profile slug is resettable. This is the *plumbing* — extended catalogs/rosters + business-event shims (the scenario **depth**) land in Phase C. `scripts/` is outside the `make check` gate; the gated test additions pass lint + typecheck.
- **`make demo-creds` — rotate + reprint the demo admin login without re-seeding (chore).** Recovering working demo credentials previously meant either remembering the four `smoke_setup.py` flags (and the frozen `--tenant-id` / `--admin-email` — getting the email wrong silently rotates a *different* user's key and the login fails with "Invalid email or API key") or running the full `make demo-tenant` seed. New thin target wraps a new `--creds-only` mode on [scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py](scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py) that runs only step 1 (`smoke_setup`: rotate the admin key + ensure the tenant/admin/editor/viewer users), prints the login email + freshly issued key, and skips all data seeding (devices, inventory, assets, backfill, alerts, transfer). The frozen tenant id / slug / admin email stay defined in exactly one place (the composer constants), so the Makefile carries no duplicated identifiers. `DEMO_KEEP_KEY=1 make demo-creds` reuses an already-exported `$TAGPULSE_API_KEY` instead of rotating. Documents the underlying "local keys are hashed at rest, shown only once — rotation is the retrieval mechanism" reality in [scripts/README.md](scripts/README.md). `scripts/` is outside the `make check` gate, so no CI impact.
- **Demo tenant display name genericized to "SuperMart Distribution Center" (chore).** Renamed the `DEMO_TENANT_NAME` constant in [scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py](scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py) and every living reference (Makefile target help, [docs/guides/demo-guide.md](docs/guides/demo-guide.md), [docs/measurements/sprint-58-baseline.md](docs/measurements/sprint-58-baseline.md), sprint-58/59 design docs, roadmap §58) off the real partner brand to the fictional "SuperMart". The `demo-wm-dc` slug, the deterministic `uuid5` tenant id (`241d9b81-…`), and all unrelated **WM wire-format / partner-reader** references (ADR-025, `test_wm_*`, `wm-wire-format-v2.md`, `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_*` metrics) are intentionally unchanged. Display-name only; no behavior change, no test impact (no test asserts the name).
- **Demo-data scripts promoted from `/tmp` into `scripts/` + usage doc (chore).** Six seeders/checks discovered while enriching the `demo-wm-dc` tenant with non-perishable general-merchandise SKUs now live in the tree with module docstrings, standard env vars (`TAGPULSE_API_KEY` / `TAGPULSE_API_URL` / `DEMO_TENANT_SLUG`, tenant id derived via `uuid5`), `httpx` + type hints, and a new [scripts/README.md](scripts/README.md) usage table. Reusable tooling: [scripts/seed_nonperishable_skus.py](scripts/seed_nonperishable_skus.py) (5 SKUs across apparel/electronics/home with no-expiry lots + zone reads), [scripts/verify_catalog.py](scripts/verify_catalog.py), [scripts/check_devices_online.py](scripts/check_devices_online.py), [scripts/cleanup_demo_stock_items.py](scripts/cleanup_demo_stock_items.py) (soft-retires units via PATCH `state=consumed` — a hard `?force=true` delete 500s on any moved unit because of the `ON DELETE RESTRICT` ledger FK; see §59.6 below). Two scripts ([scripts/seed_stock_items.py](scripts/seed_stock_items.py), [scripts/register_inventory_tags.py](scripts/register_inventory_tags.py)) are explicitly marked **temporary workarounds** for the latent ingest auto-create gate bug and are slated for removal once that bug is fixed. `scripts/` is outside the `make check` gate, so no CI impact. The bug + the two simulator gaps (serial alignment, dwell-vs-heartbeat) these scripts paper over are recorded in [docs/backlog.md](docs/backlog.md) under the Post-Sprint-58 demo-data chore cluster.
- **[ADR-030](docs/adr/030-list-page-column-filters.md) — list-page column-filter convention (proposed, chore).** Standardizes the ad-hoc filtering across the ~28 UI list pages on AntD's header `filters` + `filterSearch` (checkbox + search) for low-cardinality enumerable columns, with a hard client-vs-server rule (server-paginated lists must drive a query param, not client `onFilter`, which only filters the current page) and a shared `makeEnumFilterColumn` factory next to `ListPageShell`. Prompted by an operator request to filter Products by `category`. Recorded a `[ui]` backlog item to track the incremental migration, and back-filled the missing ADR-029 row in the ADR index. Doc-only; no code change.
- **Sprint 59 demo-scenario plan ([docs/design/sprint-59-demo-scenarios.md](docs/design/sprint-59-demo-scenarios.md)) (chore).** Captures the planned split of the combined `demo-wm-dc` tenant into two purpose-built domain tenants (cold-chain inventory + high-value asset fleet) with extensive business scenarios, a profile-driven composer, and a multi-tenant `sim_loop`. Promoted from scratch notes; to be moved onto the `sprint-59/demo-scenarios` kickoff branch. A reset-and-run-through validation of the promoted scripts added two carried-in items to the plan: **§59.6** — `DELETE /stock-items/{id}?force=true` 500s on any moved unit (unhandled `IntegrityError` from the `stock_movements_stock_item_id_fkey` `ON DELETE RESTRICT`, migration 021); needs an ADR on force-delete semantics + a route-level 409. **§59.7** — a static demo tenant reports "0 active devices" ~5 min after seeding (the Dashboard's online window with no live stream); fold a heartbeat/keep-warm into §59.4. Both also recorded in [docs/backlog.md](docs/backlog.md).
- **SuperMart inventory scenario + Stock-Levels debugging record ([docs/design/supermart-inventory-scenario.md](docs/design/supermart-inventory-scenario.md)) (chore).** Promotes the Sprint 58/59 working notes that document the multi-mode (inventory + asset) demo narrative and the full anatomy of the latent inventory auto-create gate bug (decoded GS1 URI compared against the hex-keyed `tags.epc_hex` column → every SGTIN auto-create blocked → empty Stock Levels), the two demo workarounds, and the Sprint 59 fix candidates. The retail brand in the narrative is genericized to the fictional "SuperMart"; technical identifiers (`demo-wm-dc` slug, deterministic `uuid5` tenant id) are unchanged. Doc-only.
- **Resilience hardening for `make demo-tenant` + `make demo-tenant-reset` (chore).** A round of fixes uncovered while running the Sprint 58 composer against a clean local stack:
  - **`scripts/smoke_setup.py`** — the `/health` check at step 4 now retries on transient `httpx.ConnectError` / `httpx.ReadError` for up to 30 s, replacing the single-shot probe that failed with `[Errno 104] Connection reset by peer` whenever the API container was still finishing its uvicorn reload after a `docker compose up`. Also fixes a stale endpoint reference in `ensure_telemetry_model` — `GET /telemetry-models/rfid_reader` (Sprint 14 path, removed in Sprint 28 H6) now becomes `GET /telemetry-models/device/rfid_reader` (the subject-scoped replacement); the legacy 404 was triggering a re-POST that hit the Sprint 18 unique constraint and surfaced as a 500.
  - **`scripts/seed_transfer.py`** — bumps the active-EPC wait window from 30 s to a configurable 120 s default (`--wait-timeout-s`) to ride out the tag-registrar worker's promotion tick under heavy backfill load, and adds a `_bootstrap_transferable_epcs()` self-heal: when no `tag` row is `active` after the wait, it now POSTs 3 deterministic EPC tag rows + 3 matching `/tag-reads` so the registrar can flip them to `active`, then retries the pick. Without this, a brand-new tenant has no tag-registry rows the transfer API will accept and step 7 of the composer fails on every fresh seed.
  - **`scripts/reset_demo_tenant.py`** — discovery query now walks `pg_constraint` to find every FK pointing at `tenants.id` instead of column-name matching `tenant_id`. Fixes two regressions: (1) tables with non-standard FK columns (e.g. `tag_transfers.from_tenant_id` / `.to_tenant_id`) were silently skipped and left dangling rows that blocked the final `DELETE FROM tenants`; (2) views (`asset_current_location`, `stock_levels`) were matched and produced `cannot delete from view` warnings on every run. Adds an iterative retry loop so cross-table FK chains (`tag_transfers.requested_by → users.id`) resolve without a hand-maintained topological order. Also adds a `_fail_connect_with_guidance()` helper so a missing local Postgres exits with `"Try: docker compose up -d db migrations"` instead of a raw asyncpg traceback.
- **Dev-only `PYTHONPATH=/app/src` on the docker-compose `app` + `worker` services (chore).** Edits to `src/tagpulse/...` on the host were not taking effect because Python loaded the `tagpulse` package from `/usr/local/lib/python3.12/site-packages/tagpulse/` (baked into the image by the Dockerfile's `pip install`), and the `--reload-dir /app/src` bind mount was being shadowed. Setting `PYTHONPATH=/app/src` makes Python search the bind-mounted source first, restoring hot-reload semantics for backend edits without requiring `docker compose up -d --build app`. Production images don't set `PYTHONPATH` and continue to import from the installed wheel unchanged — this is strictly a docker-compose dev affordance. The worker still needs `docker compose restart worker` (its CMD doesn't include `--reload`), but the restart now picks up source without a rebuild.

### Added

- **Docs — dedicated demo tenant guide (chore).** New [docs/guides/demo-guide.md](docs/guides/demo-guide.md) is the single content-oriented reference for the Sprint 58 demo tenant: tenant identity, login credentials per role, the seven seed steps with what each one creates, the static-vs-live distinction that operators kept hitting (e.g. `devices_online = 0/14` immediately after `make demo-tenant` is **expected** until the simulator runs — the 5-min `last_seen` window slams shut once the seed-time burst ages out), an "expected dashboard state" comparison table, a guided UI tour, reset / restart procedure, troubleshooting table (covers the recent UI proxy / cached-bundle / SPA-API path-collision symptoms), and developer hot-reload tips (`PYTHONPATH=/app/src` for backend edits). [docs/operator-quickstart.md](docs/operator-quickstart.md) §"Demo tenant" now opens with a one-line pointer to the guide so it stays the *operational* reference (laptop vs dev-cluster invocation, env-cluster commands) and the guide owns the *content* view. [README.md](README.md) Status block adds a fourth bullet pointing demo / walkthrough readers at the guide. No code changes; no roadmap update needed (chore branch).

- **Chore — `make demo-tenant-dev` runs the Sprint 58 demo composer against the deployed dev cluster via the tools-job.** Lifts the Sprint 58 Phase B/C composer (`scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py`) off the localhost-only path: operators can now seed the live dev API + Postgres for UI review, Lighthouse-against-real-CDN runs, and cross-tenant transfer demos without standing up a local docker stack. No new infra — the Sprint 26 B1 tools-job ([deploy/azure/bicep/modules/tools-job.bicep](deploy/azure/bicep/modules/tools-job.bicep)) already exposes `ENVIRONMENT`, `POSTGRES_HOST/DB/USER/PASSWORD`, `TAGPULSE_API_URL=https://${apiFqdn}`, and `TAGPULSE_SMOKE_KEY_VAULT_NAME=${keyVaultName}` to every ad-hoc script invoked via `scripts/azd-job.sh`. Three composer changes plumb that env through: (1) new `_assert_environment_safe()` reads `$ENVIRONMENT`, refuses `prod`/`production` with `SystemExit(2)` (defense-in-depth — the Make target's own `ENV=dev` guard is the first layer), returns `"local"` if unset; (2) when `$TAGPULSE_SMOKE_KEY_VAULT_NAME` is set, the composer appends `--key-vault-name <kv>` to its `smoke_setup.py` step, then re-reads the rotated key back out of Key Vault via `SecretClient` + `DefaultAzureCredential` (the tools-job UAMI already has `Key Vault Secrets Officer`) — necessary because `smoke_setup.py --key-vault-name` redacts the plaintext from stdout to keep it out of Log Analytics, breaking the existing `_EXPORT_KEY_RE` regex parse; (3) `--days` default is now mode-dependent: `3.0` locally (existing behaviour) vs `1.0` in-cluster, because the deployed API enforces the 24 h `MAX_PAST` clock window (`INGEST_CLOCK_ENFORCE=true` per [docs/design/edge-device-contract.md](docs/design/edge-device-contract.md) §3.5) so a wider backfill silently dead-letters most writes. New `make demo-tenant-dev` target wraps `scripts/azd-job.sh dev seed_demo_tenant.py -- --days 1` and bails non-zero unless `ENV=dev`. Final stdout differs by mode: local prints the existing `export TAGPULSE_API_KEY=<plaintext>` recipe; in-cluster prints the `export TAGPULSE_API_KEY=$(scripts/azd-kv-get.sh dev tagpulse-demo-wm-dc-admin-key)` recipe + az-cli fallback so plaintext never lands in operator scrollback or LA. Sprint 58 PR #83 is the predecessor work this builds on. No Bicep changes, no new container images, no new RBAC. Files: `scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py` (env guard, KV fetch helper, in-cluster default-days resolution, dual-mode stdout), `Makefile` (`demo-tenant-dev` target + `.PHONY`), `docs/operator-quickstart.md` (new "Demo tenant (dev cluster)" subsection — invocation, guard behaviour, `--days 1` rationale, KV retrieval recipe, reset-not-yet caveat), `tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py` (+6 tests: `_assert_environment_safe` × 8 parametrized cases covering prod refusal, dev/staging passthrough, case-folding, unset→"local", + 2 invariants pinning `DEMO_ADMIN_KV_SECRET_NAME` to the `smoke_setup._kv_secret_name` format and the local/in-cluster default-days constants; existing `test_composer_subprocess_args_match_target_cli[_step_smoke_setup]` picks up `--key-vault-name` via the flag-union update). 27/27 unit tests pass.

- **Sprint 58 Phase D — baseline capture (`scripts/measure_baseline.py` + `docs/measurements/sprint-58-baseline.md`).** Closes the §58.4 design-doc Phase D pass bar: get concrete numbers in the tree before Sprint 59 (terminology + nav rework) starts so that sprint has something to compare its stopwatch + Lighthouse results against. New `scripts/measure_baseline.py` issues one warmup + N timed GETs against the five hot-path endpoints the §55.C primary metric touches (`/assets?q=<epc>&limit=25`, `/alerts?status=open&limit=10`, `/device-registry?limit=100`, `/stock-levels?limit=100`, `/bulk-operations?limit=50`), reports p50/p95/p99 with min/max/status-code histogram, emits a markdown table sized to paste straight into the measurement doc, and dumps full per-iteration samples on `--json`. Tenant id + slug baked in to match `scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py` (`demo-wm-dc` / `241d9b81-…`). The 'find asset by EPC' task resolves a real EPC from `/assets` + `/assets/{id}/bindings` so the `?q=` filter exercises the binding-value branch the way the UI does; falls back to a known-deterministic urn on HTTP error so the script never blocks on data-shape drift. New `docs/measurements/sprint-58-baseline.md` records (1) the design-doc R4 escape hatch — Sprint-54 SHA rebuild explicitly NOT attempted because Sprint 54→57 schema drift (telemetry-charting migrations, ADR-028 tag registry, `?asset_type=` removal) would make the comparison meaningless; WM's qualitative "this was painful before" feedback anchors the before-state instead, (2) the API-side latency table captured from a 30-iter run against the populated demo tenant — all five tasks at p99 < 65 ms (widest spread on `/device-registry` because the list joins to the per-device connection-state view, narrowest on `/bulk-operations` and `/stock-levels` at ~37 ms p99), (3) `_TBD_` templates for the §55.C 5-task × 3-run stopwatch and the §57.G Dashboard/Assets/Devices/Alerts × Light/Dark × Perf+A11y Lighthouse runs the human will fill in before flipping the three roadmap items, (4) explicit closeout state — API-side ✅, UI-side stopwatch + Lighthouse pending human run; §55.C / §56.B / §57.G remain `[deferred]` until the human numbers land. Files: `scripts/measure_baseline.py` (new), `docs/measurements/sprint-58-baseline.md` (new).

- **Sprint 58 Phase C — continuous demo-tenant simulator (`scripts/sim_loop.py` + `sim` docker-compose profile + `make sim-{start,stop,status}` + ACA Job invocation path).** Long-running asyncio orchestrator that keeps the demo tenant animated for review sessions; sits on top of the Phase B seed bundle and is meant to be started after `make demo-tenant` finishes. Per the Phase A design doc D1 the loop is an **internal tick scheduler**, not a cron-of-oneshots — it needs stateful behaviour (reader outage holds for 3–8 min, alert injector self-rate-limits to 1/15 min, shift schedule smooths the rate across minutes) that subprocess-per-tick can't preserve. Per D5 the emission rate is gated by a `TokenBucket` (default **200 reads/min/tenant** from `SIM_RATE_PER_MIN`, hard ceiling **600/min** enforced before bucket construction; the Sprint 38 per-tenant rate limit is ~1k/min so 200 leaves comfortable headroom). Per D6 the same binary runs as a manual-trigger ACA Job in dev via the existing `scripts/azd-job.sh dev sim_loop.py -- --duration 8h --rate 200` wrapper — **no new Dockerfile target, no new ACR push, no new Key Vault plumbing**: it reuses the `api` image and the tools-job env wiring (`TAGPULSE_API_URL` + `TAGPULSE_API_KEY` from KV) already in place. Per HC6 the script aborts non-zero if `ENV` is set to anything other than `dev` (locally `ENV` is unset so docker-compose runs unimpeded; ACA bicep sets `ENV=dev` explicitly for the dev tools job). HTTP-only (POST /tag-reads): no MQTT broker access from the job. Behaviours: shift schedule applies a 1.5× multiplier in a ±30 min window around 08:00 and 13:00 local, 0.3× during 20:00–06:00, 1.0× otherwise; each minute a 5 % chance to take one non-offline device offline for `uniform(3,8)` minutes; every ~15 min injects one high-temperature read (35–42 °C) routed through normal ingest so the existing high-temp rule fires; status line every 60 s prints uptime / total reads / running rate / total alerts / offline device count. SIGINT/SIGTERM trigger graceful shutdown via an `asyncio.Event`. Duration parser accepts `30s`/`5m`/`2h`/`1d`/bare integer seconds; `0` means run forever. `--seed N` makes the PRNG deterministic for repeatable runs. Docker-compose `sim` service is opt-in (`profiles: ["sim"]`) so `docker compose up -d` continues to start exactly the same six containers as before; the `sim-start` Makefile target refuses to launch without `$TAGPULSE_API_KEY` exported. 26 new unit tests covering token bucket starts-full / consumes / refills / never-exceeds-capacity, shift multiplier across 9 hour-of-day cases, duration parser happy paths × 6 + rejections × 5, and `SimState.active_devices` filtering of expired vs in-progress outages. Files: `scripts/sim_loop.py` (new, ~470 lines), `docker-compose.yml` (+1 service under `profiles: ["sim"]`), `Makefile` (+3 targets `sim-start` / `sim-stop` / `sim-status`, `.PHONY` updated), `tests/unit/test_sim_loop.py` (new, 26 cases via `importlib.util` since `scripts/` isn't on `sys.path`), `docs/operator-quickstart.md` (new "Continuous simulator" subsection under "Demo tenant (local only)").

- **Sprint 58 Phase B (2/N) — `make demo-tenant` composer + four new seed scripts.** Wires the seven-step demo-tenant build path locked in the Phase A design doc (D1–D7) into a single idempotent shell entry point. Composition-not-rewrite stays load-bearing: the four existing simulators (`simulate_devices.py` / `simulate_assets.py` / `simulate_inventory.py` / `mqtt_canary.py`) are untouched; `scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py` is a thin orchestrator that pins each child invocation's CLI args explicitly (no `**kwargs` pass-through per R1) and streams subprocess stdout/stderr inline. Adds three genuinely new shims: (a) `scripts/backfill_history.py` replays N reads (default 5000 over 3 days) across the discovered device set via `POST /tag-reads/batch?backfill=true` so the historical pipeline runs end-to-end through ingest, hypertable write, telemetry rollup — but the alert-evaluation + reads-per-minute counters stay suppressed by the Phase B (1/N) flag wired in commit `248052b`; payloads are timestamp-sorted before batching so TimescaleDB chunk inserts stay sequential; (b) `scripts/seed_alerts.py` produces D4's hybrid alert set — 4 *natural* alerts by `POST /tag-reads` of high-temperature reads (35–42 °C) round-robined across devices to defeat the 60s per-(tenant, rule, device) cooldown and ride the existing rule path, plus 3 *resolved* alerts inserted directly via asyncpg with `status='resolved'` and `triggered_at` staggered 6–60h ago so the UI's resolution timeline has data without re-implementing rule eval; (c) `scripts/seed_transfer.py` upserts a deterministic `demo-wm-recipient` tenant (`uuid5(DNS, "demo-wm-recipient.tagpulse.local")`) and creates one in-flight cross-tenant transfer of 3 active EPCs (guarded by a `COUNT(*) FROM tag_transfers WHERE status='requested' > 0` idempotency check). Composer respects two env knobs documented in `docs/operator-quickstart.md`: `DEMO_KEEP_KEY=1` (skip step 1's key rotation, reuse `$TAGPULSE_API_KEY` for in-progress browser sessions) and `DEMO_SKIP_BACKFILL=1` (skip step 5 for fast iteration). Demo tenant identity per D2: slug `demo-wm-dc`, name "SuperMart Distribution Center", id `uuid5(DNS, "demo-wm-dc.tagpulse.local")`. Reset path via new `scripts/reset_demo_tenant.py` + `make demo-tenant-reset`: discovers tenant-scoped tables dynamically from `information_schema` (future-proof against new migrations adding tenant_id columns), `DELETE FROM <table> WHERE tenant_id = ANY($1)` per table, deletes the tenant rows last; refuses to run unless the target DB host smells local (`localhost`, `127.0.0.1`, `tagpulse-pg`, `host.docker.internal`) — override with `DEMO_RESET_FORCE=1`. Makefile gets two new targets in the `## ----- Sprint 58 ... -----` block. No new tests beyond the Phase B (1/N) suite: per HC3 in the design doc the seed scripts are local-dev-only utilities and not part of CI. Pass bar from Phase A holds: clean `docker compose up` → `alembic upgrade head` → `make demo-tenant` produces a demo-ready tenant in ≤ 5 min, re-run is idempotent, `make demo-tenant-reset` returns to zero. Files: `scripts/backfill_history.py` (new), `scripts/seed_alerts.py` (new), `scripts/seed_transfer.py` (new), `scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py` (new), `scripts/reset_demo_tenant.py` (new), `Makefile` (`.PHONY` + `demo-tenant` + `demo-tenant-reset` targets), `docs/operator-quickstart.md` (new "Demo tenant (local only)" section with the 7-step flow + env-knob table + reset recipe).

- **Sprint 58 Phase B (1/N) — `POST /tag-reads[?backfill=true]` + `/tag-reads/batch?backfill=true` skip alert evaluation while running the full ingest pipeline.** Resolves Q1 from the Phase A design doc: the demo-tenant seed bundle replays ~3 days of historical reads through HTTP ingest, which used to race the curated alert set the seed step is also trying to establish (and could spuriously trip `read_frequency` anomaly flags on the freshly-empty tenant). The new query param wires a request-scoped `ContextVar` in `IngestionService.ingest` / `ingest_batch`; every event payload published by the service (`TAG_READ_CREATED` ×2, `TELEMETRY_RECORDED` for tag-borne sensor mirror, `SUBJECT_ZONE_CHANGED` ×3 for asset reader-bound + geofence + stock-item reader-bound) is wrapped through a one-line `_event_payload()` helper that stamps `"backfill": True` when the ContextVar is set. The `RuleEvaluator`'s three handlers (`on_tag_read`, `on_subject_zone_changed`, `on_telemetry_recorded`) and `ReadFrequencyModule.on_event` early-return on that flag, so the full pipeline (validation, enrichment, hypertable insert, telemetry rollups via downstream `TELEMETRY_RECORDED` subscribers) still runs as the Phase A design doc requires — only alert evaluation and reads/minute counters are suppressed. ContextVar isolation tested: backfill flag on one ingest call does not leak to the next plain ingest on the same shared service instance. No new endpoints (HC5 honored — query param on existing route is a behaviour toggle per the cross-ref added in commit `00973fc`). Files: `src/tagpulse/ingestion/service.py` (ContextVar + helper + ingest wrappers + 6 payload sites), `src/tagpulse/api/routes/ingestion.py` (`backfill: bool = Query(False)` on both routes), `src/tagpulse/rules/evaluator.py` (3 early-returns), `src/tagpulse/analytics/read_frequency.py` (1 early-return), `tests/unit/test_ingestion_service.py` (new `TestBackfillFlag` × 4: default no flag, single ingest stamps + persists, batch stamps every payload, ContextVar no-leak), `openapi.json` (regenerated — new query param on both routes).

- **Sprint 58 Phase A polish — design doc + roadmap reconciliation.** Closeout edits to the Phase A planning artifacts after the audit pass: (1) Hard Constraint 5 ("no new API endpoints") now carries a one-line cross-reference to the resolved Q1 clarifying that a query param on an existing route (`?backfill=true`) is a behaviour toggle, not a new resource surface, so it does not violate the constraint; (2) D3's trailing "Open question for Phase A" line replaced with a forward-pointer to the resolved Q1 section to remove internal contradiction; (3) deliverable #2 and roadmap §sprint-58 Phase C aligned to use the canonical script name `sim_loop.py` (the design doc was authoritative; roadmap had drifted to `run_continuous_sim.py`); (4) PR #83 cross-repo plan section filled in (was `_TBD_` placeholders) — backend-only, no UI PR, OpenAPI regenerates in Phase B for the `?backfill=true` query param, independent merge. No code changed, no scope changed. Files: `docs/design/sprint-58-demo-and-simulation.md`, `docs/roadmap.md`.
- **Sprint 58 kickoff — demo data & simulation foundation planning.** Plans a backend-only sprint to compose the four existing simulator scripts (`simulate_devices.py`, `simulate_assets.py`, `simulate_inventory.py`, `mqtt_canary.py`) into (1) a repeatable `make demo-tenant` seed that stands up a "SuperMart Distribution Center" tenant in ≤ 5 min, (2) a continuously-running simulator service (docker-compose profile locally; `azd-job.sh` Container Apps invocation in dev), and (3) the first realistic baseline + Lighthouse capture for the §55.C / §56.B / §57.G measurement items deferred across the last three sprints — closing all three in this sprint. Sequenced before Sprint 59 (WM-driven terminology + nav rework) so that sprint's stopwatch + Lighthouse numbers compare against a real baseline rather than a noise-dominated empty-tenant one. Out of scope: terminology renames (Sprint 59), nav changes beyond Sprint 54/56, new device types, new chart types, rule-engine changes, load testing at scale. Files: `docs/roadmap.md` (§sprint-58 entry).
- **Sprint 58 design doc — demo data & simulation foundation.** Phase-A artifact locking the seven design decisions (D1 long-running asyncio orchestrator over cron-of-oneshots, D2 deterministic `demo-wm-dc` tenant UUID, D3 backfill via HTTP not direct DB insert, D4 hybrid alert seeding, D5 token-bucket rate cap default 200/min ceiling 600/min, D6 Container Apps job with 8 h hard ceiling not perpetual service, D7 no demo tenant in CI), five risks with mitigations, and three open questions for Phase B. Composition-not-rewrite is the load-bearing constraint: the four existing simulators stay untouched; three thin shims (`backfill_history.py`, `seed_alerts.py`, `seed_transfer.py`) are the only genuinely new code paths in Phase B. Files: `docs/design/sprint-58-demo-and-simulation.md` (new).

### Fixed

- **Sprint 58 audit cleanup — `scripts/seed_transfer.py` no longer races the tag-registrar worker on first run.** The composer (`scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py`) invokes `seed_transfer.py` as step 7, immediately after the step-5 `backfill_history.py` batch lands. Both run synchronously, but `tags.status='registered' → 'active'` promotion happens out-of-band on the tag-registrar worker's next tick (a few seconds), so `_pick_active_epcs()`'s `WHERE status='active'` query returned zero rows on a fresh demo tenant — `seed_transfer.py` then printed `WARN: no active tags on source tenant — skipping transfer` and the D5 in-flight transfer deliverable silently didn't ship. The audit pass caught this as a benign race (the seed run still returned 0); the worker would catch up minutes later but the operator had already moved on. Fix: replaced the one-shot pick with `_wait_for_active_epcs(..., timeout_s=30.0)` that polls `_pick_active_epcs` every 1 s until the target count is met or the budget expires. Hardened the WARN message to call out the worker-lag root cause and point at `docker compose ps worker` for triage. No schema change, no API change, no public-CLI change. Operator-quickstart updated with the same wait-then-fail story so first-time operators know what "WARN" actually means when they see it. Files: `scripts/seed_transfer.py`, `docs/operator-quickstart.md`.

- **Sprint 58 Phase D drive-by — four endpoint-URL drift bugs in demo-tenant seed scripts surfaced when actually running the end-to-end seed against a live API.** Phase B/C composer happy-path was tested in isolation but the full bundle hadn't been re-run against the current router prefixes since Sprints 34/49/50 refactored them. Fixed: (1) `scripts/smoke_setup.py` line 632 and `scripts/simulate_assets.py` line 84 hit `/categories?limit=1000` which has returned 422 since Sprint 34 capped it at `le=500`; now request `limit=500`. (2) `scripts/simulate_assets.py` line 189 POST'd to `/ingest/tag-read` which no longer exists; correct route is `/tag-reads`. (3) `scripts/backfill_history.py` (4 spots: 1 real call + 3 docstring refs) and `scripts/seed_alerts.py` line 124 GET'd `/devices` which no longer exists; correct router prefix is `/device-registry`. (4) `scripts/sim_loop.py` Phase C deliverable shipped with the same `/devices` typo in `_discover_devices` — would have failed at startup the first time anyone ran `make sim-start` against a fresh demo tenant; now hits `/device-registry`. All four fixes are URL-only — no behaviour change, no schema change, no test change. Bundled into the Phase D commit per `start-sprint.sh` policy (drive-by fixes that block the sprint's pass bar ride alongside the sprint deliverable, not in a separate chore PR). Verified by a successful end-to-end `python scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py` run yielding 14 devices, 17 assets, 1673 backfilled reads, 4+3 alerts, 1 cross-tenant transfer.

- **Pre-Phase D editor-format drift in 4 seed scripts re-aligned with `ruff format`.** `scripts/reset_demo_tenant.py`, `scripts/seed_demo_tenant.py`, `scripts/seed_transfer.py`, and `scripts/sim_loop.py` had accumulated cosmetic whitespace drift from editor-on-save reformats while their authoring branches were in flight. Pure formatting; no semantic change. Bundled into the Phase D commit because `make lint` now enforces `ruff format --check` (per the Sprint 54.3 follow-up entry above) and these files would otherwise have failed the gate on the next unrelated PR.

(5) New [tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py](tests/unit/test_seed_demo_tenant.py) — 16 hermetic contract tests (2 uuid5 idempotency pins for `DEMO_TENANT_ID` / `DEFAULT_RECIPIENT_ID`, 7 target-script existence checks, 7 AST-parsed argparse-flag drift checks) closing the R1 mitigation. Pure-Python, no DB / HTTP / subprocess; located under `tests/unit/` rather than `tests/integration/` (as originally sketched) because `make test` only picks up `tests/unit` and the test set has no external dependencies. (6) [docs/operator-quickstart.md](docs/operator-quickstart.md) step-5 gains a gotcha block explaining the 24 h `MAX_PAST` clock window in `src/tagpulse/ingestion/clock.py` and how `INGEST_CLOCK_ENFORCE=false` or `--days 1` lets the operator land the full backfill window vs. the default ~24 h slice (`backfill=true` does *not* bypass the clock check — it only suppresses rule eval); step-7 gains the worker-promotion-race gotcha that mirrors the `seed_transfer` fix above. No production-code change beyond the `seed_transfer` race fix already covered above; no API contract change. No backend code change; pure roadmap reconciliation. Files: `docs/roadmap.md`.

### Added

- **Sprint 57 Phase 57.6 — `GET /dashboard/sparklines?days=7&bucket_hours=6` 9-tile trend bundle.** Backs the inline `<TpSparkline>` chips on each Dashboard KPI tile (TagPulse-UI PR #68 Phase F) in one round-trip. Returns a `tiles` dict keyed by the same tile `id` strings the UI uses in `src/pages/Dashboard.tsx` so client wire-up is a direct lookup; tiles whose schema lacks point-in-time history get a flat series (current value repeated, `trend="flat"`) and the two with real time-series tables (`reads-per-hour` from `tag_reads`, `alerts-open` from `alerts.triggered_at`) get bucketed counts via PG14+ `date_bin(:stride, col, :origin)` — picked over the existing two-repo `time_bucket()` abstraction in `metrics.py` because `alerts` isn't a hypertable, so a Timescale-only path would have meant adding a Postgres-fallback branch we don't otherwise need. `alerts-open` is documented as "alerts triggered per bucket" (volume): `AlertModel` has `triggered_at` but no `resolved_at`, so a historical "open count at time T" can't be reconstructed; the docstring on `SparklineSeries` calls this out. Default 28 points (6h × 7d). `trend` ("up"/"down"/"flat") compares last-quarter mean vs first-quarter mean with a ±5% dead-band so noisy series don't flicker between refreshes; empty/zero-baseline cases are special-cased. Open to `admin` / `editor` / `viewer` (parity with `/dashboard/summary`); `days ∈ [1, 30]`, `bucket_hours ∈ [1, 24]` 422 on out-of-range. Files: `src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py` (`SparklinePoint`, `SparklineSeries`, `DashboardSparklines`), `src/tagpulse/services/dashboard.py` (`get_sparklines` + 4 helpers), `src/tagpulse/api/routes/dashboard.py` (new route + module docstring update), `tests/unit/test_dashboard_sparklines.py` (11 cases: route dispatch, query-param forwarding, role parametrize × 3, role rejection, query-param validation × 4, `_classify_trend` thresholds), `openapi.json` (regenerated).

- **Sprint 54 follow-up — `tags_total` / `sites_total` / `zones_total` on `GET /dashboard/summary` + per-tenant `dashboard_tags_count_mode`.** The Sprint 54.3 endpoint shipped eight aggregates but the UI dashboard rewrite (TagPulse-UI PR #66) revealed two missing rollups that operators wanted on the landing page: a Tags KPI and a combined Sites+Zones "Locations" KPI. Extends `DashboardSummary` with three new ints: `sites_total` and `zones_total` are simple per-tenant `COUNT(*)` from `sites` / `zones`; `tags_total` is per-tenant `COUNT(*)` from `tags` with the predicate chosen by a new per-tenant `dashboard_tags_count_mode` config (`"all"` counts every row, `"live"` (default) counts `status IN ('registered', 'active')` to match the Tags page's default filter, `"non_terminal"` counts `status NOT IN ('retired', 'defective', 'transferred_out')`). Reuses the existing `_LIVE_TAG_STATUSES` / `_TERMINAL_TAG_STATUSES` tuples in `dashboard.py` so the dashboard tile click-through to `/tags` lands on consistent numbers regardless of which mode is picked. The new column is gated by the same admin-only branch in `PATCH /tenant/config` as `low_stock_threshold` and audit-logged as `tenant_config_updated` with the `{from, to}` diff; Literal-typed on the schema so unknown values 422 before hitting the DB. Service issues twelve queries now (eleven aggregates + one tenant row that batches the `low_stock_threshold` + `dashboard_tags_count_mode` lookup into a single SELECT). Files: `migrations/versions/050_tenant_dashboard_tags_count_mode.py` (new), `src/tagpulse/models/database.py` (`TenantModel.dashboard_tags_count_mode`), `src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py` (3 new `DashboardSummary` fields), `src/tagpulse/services/dashboard.py` (3 new aggregates + batched tenant lookup), `src/tagpulse/api/routes/tenant_config.py` (`DashboardTagsCountMode` literal + `TenantConfig` + `TenantConfigUpdate` + PATCH branch + `_to_response`), `tests/unit/test_dashboard_summary.py` (extended payload contract), `tests/unit/test_tenant_config.py` (3 new cases: accept all three modes, reject unknown, default `"live"` in response), `openapi.json` (regenerated).

- **Sprint 54 Phase 54.3 — `GET /dashboard/summary` landing-page KPI endpoint.** Single tenant-scoped read returning eight aggregate counts (plus a `generated_at` timestamp for cache-busting) that the new Dashboard tiles consume in one round-trip: `devices_online` / `devices_total` (5-min `last_seen` + `connection_state='connected'`), `alerts_open_24h` (`status='open' AND triggered_at >= now-24h`), `reads_per_hour_now` (`tag_reads` in last hour), `assets_active`, `tag_transfers_in_flight` (`status='requested'` matching either `from_tenant_id` or `to_tenant_id`), `tag_recon_backlog` (sum of registered-unread + unregistered-reading + bindings-on-retired, mirroring the existing `tag_reconciliation` predicates so the tile click-through to `/tags/reconciliation` lands on consistent numbers), `low_stock_count` (per-product `count(*) < tenants.low_stock_threshold` for `state='in_stock' AND consumed_at IS NULL`). Open to `admin` / `editor` / `viewer` — aggregates only, no row-level data. New `tenants.low_stock_threshold` column (default 3) configurable via `PATCH /tenant/config`; gated by the same admin-only branch as the existing bulk-action thresholds and audit-logged as `tenant_config_updated` with `{from, to}` diff. Files: `migrations/versions/049_tenant_low_stock_threshold.py` (new), `src/tagpulse/models/database.py` (`TenantModel.low_stock_threshold`), `src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py` (new `DashboardSummary`), `src/tagpulse/services/dashboard.py` (new), `src/tagpulse/api/routes/dashboard.py` (new), `src/tagpulse/api/routes/tenant_config.py` (`TenantConfig` + `TenantConfigUpdate` + PATCH branch + `_to_response`), `src/tagpulse/api/main.py` (router include), `tests/unit/test_dashboard_summary.py` (new, 5 cases: payload contract + per-role gate matrix + reject unknown role), `openapi.json` (regenerated).

- **Sprint 54 kickoff — UI overhaul planning artifacts.** Plans a two-sprint UI overhaul (54 + 55) replacing the flat 45-route nav + `react-grid-layout` Dashboard + page-by-page list inconsistencies with a sectioned single left nav, a titled-KPI-tile Dashboard with click-through to pre-filtered list pages, and a uniform `<ListPageShell>` pattern — all dual-theme via design tokens up front (no retrofit). 80% UX polish + 20% Dashboard rewrite. Vendor-neutral docs (no third-party product names in committed files). Backend side ships only one new endpoint (`GET /dashboard/summary`, 8 tenant-scoped counts, p95 ≤200 ms) in Sprint 54.3, backend-first; the rest lives in `TagPulse-UI` (backend PR #74, UI PR #62 — first sprint to exercise the `--with-ui` kickoff flow from PR #73). Success metrics: primary stopwatch (5 operator tasks, 3 runs, drop high+low, ≥30% faster on 4 of 5, none slower >10%); secondary Lighthouse (Perf ≥90, A11y ≥95 on Dashboard + Assets + Devices + Alerts in both themes). Baseline pinned to the sprint-54 kickoff commit SHA. Out of scope: i18n, custom illustrations, onboarding tour, new chart library, WCAG audit beyond Lighthouse, phone (<768 px), 14 admin list pages (→ Sprint 56). Files: `docs/design/sprint-54-ui-overhaul.md` (new), `docs/adr/029-ui-design-tokens.md` (new — two-layer primitive + semantic token catalog, dual theme via `[data-theme]` attribute, AntD `ConfigProvider` mirror, four hard rules including zero hardcoded hex and zero `!important`, `/dev/tokens` debug page as Phase 54.1 acceptance artifact), `docs/roadmap.md` (Sprint 54 + Sprint 55 entries appended), `docs/backlog.md` (14 admin list pages entry — drained into a Sprint 56 promotion task during Sprint 55 Phase D).

### Changed

- **`scripts/smoke_setup.py` — new `--print-full-key` flag for local dev bootstrap.** The script truncates the freshly issued admin API key to a 10-char preview by default (safe for shared terminals and tools-job logs); operators bootstrapping a local UI session previously had to re-issue and copy from a side channel. The new opt-in flag prints the full key on a second line after the preview so it can be pasted directly into the browser. Ignored when `--key-vault-name` is set (the key goes to KV instead of stdout). Never use in CI or shared environments. Files: `scripts/smoke_setup.py`.

- **`make lint` now enforces `ruff format --check`; one-shot reformat baseline across the tree.** CI ran `ruff check` only, so format drift accumulated silently — by Sprint 54 ~60 files had collapsed-statement diffs that re-appeared on every editor-save touch, creating noisy "pending change" surprises mid-sprint (see Sprint 54.3 commit `3a0c5ea` for the most recent symptom). Added `ruff format --check src tests clients/pi` to the `lint` Makefile target (CI picks it up via `make lint`) and ran a one-shot `ruff format` pass on the 61 drifted files (308 insertions / 662 deletions, no semantic change). All 1363 unit tests still pass. Going forward, an editor-on-save reformat that diverges from the repo style fails CI immediately instead of bleeding into the next feature PR. Files: `Makefile` (+ 61 reformatted source/test files).

- **Cross-repo workflow documented + encoded in tooling.** TagPulse ships as two repos (this backend + `TagPulse-UI`) but until now the rules for how they share sprint numbers, route work, and hand off the OpenAPI contract lived only in the operator's head. Codified the model in three places so Copilot agents and humans both follow it automatically: (1) new `## Cross-Repo Workflow` section in [.github/copilot-instructions.md](.github/copilot-instructions.md) covering shared sprint numbering, the three work shapes (sprint / chore / in-flight follow-up), OpenAPI as contract handoff, backend-roadmap-as-source-of-truth with `[UI]` tags, the `docs/backlog.md` scratch list, and backend-first merge order when both repos touch a sprint; (2) new [docs/backlog.md](docs/backlog.md) as the lightweight in-flight idea capture (drain at sprint planning); (3) `scripts/start-sprint.sh` now accepts `--with-ui` to create a matching `sprint-NN/<topic>` branch + cross-linked draft PR in `$TAGPULSE_UI_PATH` (default `~/ws/TagPulse-UI`), and the kickoff PR body now includes a `## Cross-repo plan` section so the cross-repo intent is declared upfront even when the answer is "backend only". [CONTRIBUTING.md](CONTRIBUTING.md) gains a pointer to the new section. No process change for existing sprints already in flight; chores remain unscripted (`chore/<topic>` off `main` manually). Mirrored chore branch in `TagPulse-UI`.

### Fixed

- **`scripts/smoke_setup.py` — `_seed_reserved_tag_labels` no longer crashes with `asyncpg.exceptions.AmbiguousParameterError` on fresh tenants.** asyncpg could not infer the SQL type for `$2` because the parameter is used in two positions with different inferred types (the bare `SELECT $1, 'tag', $2, ...` column list lets it be `unknown`, but `lower($2)` in the `NOT EXISTS` predicate forces it to `text` — and asyncpg refuses to bind a single parameter under two inferred types). Added explicit `$2::text` casts at both call sites so the type is unambiguous. Unblocks `make smoke-setup` against a brand-new local Postgres where the labels table is empty and the seeding path runs for the first time. Files: `scripts/smoke_setup.py`.

- **Sprint 53 Phase H follow-up — `scripts/azd-kv-get.sh` no longer truncates multi-line Key Vault secrets to their last line.** The script's final `printf '%s\n' "$(echo "$PAYLOAD" | tail -1)"` collapsed multi-line PEM secrets to just `-----END CERTIFICATE-----`, so operators following the Phase H recipe (`scripts/azd-kv-get.sh dev mqtt-tls-ca > ~/.tagpulse/dev-mqtt-ca.pem`) ended up with a 26-byte single-line file that paho-mqtt rejected at `client.tls_set()` with `ssl.SSLError: [X509: NO_CERTIFICATE_OR_CRL_FOUND]`. The `tail -1` was vestigial — the awk extraction above already sentinel-bounds the payload between `===KV_SECRET_BEGIN===` / `===KV_SECRET_END===` printed by [scripts/get_kv_secret.py](scripts/get_kv_secret.py) L94-95, so no further trimming is needed. Now `printf '%s\n' "$PAYLOAD"` preserves the value verbatim; the single-secret path and `--list` path now match. Verified end-to-end: edge smoke publisher reaches the dev broker over TLS, message lands in TimescaleDB, surfaces in Data Explorer. Files: `scripts/azd-kv-get.sh`.

### Changed

- **Sprint 53 Phase I — `_mirror_tag_borne_sensors` now reads numeric metrics from both `tag_reads.sensor_data` and `tag_reads.tag_data`.** Closes a real gap surfaced while writing the Phase G doc: the v2 MQTT parser ([src/tagpulse/ingestion/mqtt_subscriber.py](src/tagpulse/ingestion/mqtt_subscriber.py) `_wm_sensor_data`) puts `cnt`/`tmp`/`hum` into the `sensor_data` column as `read_count`/`temperature_c`/`humidity_pct`, but the bridge in [src/tagpulse/ingestion/service.py](src/tagpulse/ingestion/service.py) only iterated `tag_data`, so v2-borne sensor reads landed in `tag_reads.sensor_data` and never reached `telemetry_readings`. Cold-chain `telemetry.threshold` rules built on the existing rule template ([src/tagpulse/rules/templates.py](src/tagpulse/rules/templates.py) `metric_name="temperature_c"`) could not fire on MQTT-borne sensor data. The bridge now merges numeric values from both blobs (skipping `_`-prefixed keys and rejecting `bool` which is a subclass of `int` in Python); on key collision `tag_data` wins so an explicit HTTP client value still overrides the wire-parser default. v1 callers that only populate `tag_data` are unaffected (same iteration, same metric_names, same provenance `source="tag"`). Tests: `test_subject_fanout_mirrors_v2_sensor_data_blob` (3 metrics fan out to one opted-in subject with `source="tag"`) and `test_subject_fanout_tag_data_overrides_sensor_data_on_collision` (one row, `tag_data` value wins) in [tests/unit/test_sprint19_subject_telemetry.py](tests/unit/test_sprint19_subject_telemetry.py); existing 8-case suite continues to pass. Doc: [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md) §4.6 mapping table corrected — the prior table claimed `avg_temp_c`/`avg_humidity_pct` keys that do not exist anywhere in the code; real keys are `read_count`/`temperature_c`/`humidity_pct`. Files: `src/tagpulse/ingestion/service.py`, `tests/unit/test_sprint19_subject_telemetry.py`, `docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md`.

- **Sprint 53 Phase H — `.tp_paho_edge.env.example` and edge README now default to 8883 + TLS for the dev broker.** Sprint 28 C6 stood up the TLS listener on dev (the ACI exposes both 1883 and 8883, with `MOSQUITTO_TLS_CA/CERT/KEY` mounted from KV) and platform consumers like the WM developers have been using 8883 for a while, but the operator-facing edge sidecar config still defaulted to plaintext 1883 with `TLS_CA` commented out and the password instructions pointed at the slow in-VNet `azd-kv-get.sh` job. Flipped [clients/pi/examples/.tp_paho_edge.env.example](clients/pi/examples/.tp_paho_edge.env.example) to `BROKER_PORT=8883` with `TLS_CA=$HOME/.tagpulse/dev-mqtt-ca.pem` uncommented, swapped the password comment to the fast `azd env get-value AZURE_MQTT_PASSWORD` path (the broker password is already exported in the azd env; `azd-kv-get.sh` stays documented as the fallback when azd env isn't available), and added inline instructions for pulling the CA pem from the `mqtt-tls-ca` Key Vault secret. [clients/pi/README.md](clients/pi/README.md) "TLS (port 8883)" gains a new "Pulling the dev CA pem from Key Vault" block with the `scripts/azd-kv-get.sh dev mqtt-tls-ca > ~/.tagpulse/dev-mqtt-ca.pem` recipe, the `chmod 600`, and a note that the call sits silent for 30s–3min because KV is `publicNetworkAccess=Disabled` and the secret has to be fetched from an in-VNet Container Apps job. Plaintext 1883 fallback is still documented for backward compat. No code change; the publisher's existing TLS auto-enable logic (port 8883 *or* `TLS_CA` set) is unchanged. Files: `clients/pi/examples/.tp_paho_edge.env.example`, `clients/pi/README.md`.

- **Sprint 53 Phase G — documented the `_mirror_tag_borne_sensors` bridge end-to-end.** The v2 wire-format spec stopped at the `tag_reads` insert and ADR-015's producer table predated Sprint 46, leaving the path `v2 tag-read with tmp/hum → _mirror_tag_borne_sensors → telemetry_readings → Topic.TELEMETRY_RECORDED → telemetry.threshold rule` undocumented in one place. Added [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md) §4.6 (wire→metric mapping table, subject fan-out, tenant gating, off-hot-path role of telemetry models). Updated the [ADR-015 §2](docs/adr/015-telemetry-rules-and-deprecation.md) producer table to note that the `_mirror_tag_borne_sensors` row covers both v1 HTTP and v2 MQTT, with a cross-link to §4.6. Added a two-pipes-one-bridge ASCII diagram + narrative to [docs/guides/domain-concepts-101.md](docs/guides/domain-concepts-101.md) so newcomers can see how sensor-tag readings (cold-chain stickers) and external telemetry converge at `telemetry_readings` without a second producer. No code change. Files: `docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md`, `docs/adr/015-telemetry-rules-and-deprecation.md`, `docs/guides/domain-concepts-101.md`.
- **Sprint 53 Phase F — operator docs for v2 wire-format testing.** Added a `v2 wire format (Sprint 46+, ADR-025)` subsection to [clients/pi/README.md](clients/pi/README.md) "Smoke-publish from the CLI" with three v2 recipes (appeared / snap / disappeared), the spec §6 `invalid_epc` validation note, the `--wire v2` + `--topic` interaction rule, and a cross-link to `scripts/mqtt_canary.py` as the in-VNet canary equivalent. Added a callout to [docs/runbooks/mqtt-outage.md](docs/runbooks/mqtt-outage.md) §1 explaining that the canary now exercises the v2 dispatch + presence reconciler end-to-end (broker → subscriber → v2 → DB), so a passing canary is a stronger health signal but a failing one no longer isolates which hop is broken without §2 metrics. No code change. Files: `clients/pi/README.md`, `docs/runbooks/mqtt-outage.md`.
- **Sprint 53 Phase F — `scripts/mqtt_canary.py` publishes a v2 `t=1` (appeared) message instead of the legacy v1 `{tag_id,timestamp}` shape.** The Sprint 28 C2 in-VNet canary (used by the D2 alert and the C4 outage runbook) was still emitting the v1 wire format after Sprint 46/47 shipped v2 (ADR 025/026/027), so the canary's broker → subscriber → ingestion path never exercised the v2 dispatch + presence reconciler branch in production. The canary now publishes `{"t":1, "sn":1, "ts":<ms>, "lat":null, "lon":null, "an":0, "epc":"CA<22 hex>", "rssi":-50, "cnt":1}` with a per-run 24-hex-char EPC derived from `uuid4()` (uppercase, even length, hex — satisfies the spec §6 `invalid_epc` validator). The Postgres polling loop now binds the canary EPC to `tag_reads.tag_id` (per spec §4.4: `_wm_appeared_to_tag_read` maps `msg.epc → tag_id`). Verifies broker → subscriber → v2 dispatch → presence reconciler → ingestion → DB end-to-end on every 5-minute alert run. Files: `scripts/mqtt_canary.py`.

### Added

- **Sprint 53 Phase F — `clients/pi/examples/paho_smoke_publisher.py` gains a `--wire v2` mode.** Manual operator-facing publisher (paho-mqtt v5) gains `--wire {v1,v2}` (default `v1`, no behaviour change for existing recipes), `--v2-type {snap,appeared,disappeared}` (default `appeared`), and `--sn N` (default 1). When `--wire v2 --topic tag-reads` is set, the new `make_v2_tag_read_payload(args)` builder emits one inline `t=0` / `t=1` / `t=2` envelope shaped to match the discriminated union enforced by `tagpulse.ingestion.wm_wire_format` and `WmV2Producer` — including the spec §6 `invalid_epc` validation (uppercase hex, even, 8..124 chars) so a malformed `--epc-hex` fails client-side instead of producing a silently-DLQ-ed payload. `--wire v2` with `--topic {location,events}` exits 2 (only `tag-reads` carries v2 today). Top-of-file usage block gains three new example invocations (`--once --wire v2`, `--once --wire v2 --v2-type snap`, `--once --wire v2 --v2-type disappeared`) and a new doc cross-link to [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md). Files: `clients/pi/examples/paho_smoke_publisher.py`.

### Added

- **Sprint 53 — Sprint 50 Phase G reconciliation observability (per-view row counter).** Closes the "reconciliation worker emitting Prometheus gauges" item that Sprint 50 Phase F explicitly deferred to Phase G (recorded in [ADR 028](docs/adr/028-tags-as-first-class-entity.md) v1.0). The Phase E reconciliation route handler ([src/tagpulse/api/routes/tags.py](src/tagpulse/api/routes/tags.py) `tag_reconciliation_endpoint`) now bumps a new OTel counter `tagpulse_tag_reconciliation_rows_returned_total{view}` by `len(rows)` after each successful query — labelled by the view name (`registered-unread` / `unregistered-reading` / `bindings-on-retired`). A monotonically rising series with a flat tail tells operators the exception queue is no longer being reviewed; a sudden spike on `unregistered-reading` typically signals a reel was deployed without a prior CSV import. The counter is wired as a counter rather than the gauge originally sketched in the audit table — counters compose correctly over Prometheus `rate()` / `increase()` windows for "rows surfaced per hour", which is the actual operator question; a gauge would either need a scheduled worker (also deferred) or would represent only the most-recent response size. The `.add()` call is wrapped in a defensive `try/except` per the Sprint 46 Phase E counter convention so OTel SDK failures cannot fail the response. New module-level export `tag_reconciliation_rows_returned_counter` in [src/tagpulse/core/otel_metrics.py](src/tagpulse/core/otel_metrics.py) (Counter, unit `rows`). Tests: 2 new cases appended to [tests/unit/test_tag_reconciliation.py](tests/unit/test_tag_reconciliation.py) — `test_reconciliation_counter_bumped_by_row_count` (asserts a 3-row response produces exactly one `.add(3, {"view": "registered-unread"})` call via a `_RecordingCounter` stand-in monkeypatched into the route module) and `test_reconciliation_counter_failure_does_not_break_response` (an `_ExplodingCounter` that raises from `.add()` cannot turn a 200 into a 500). The route's existing 8 case suite continues to pass unchanged. **Out of scope** (deferred to a follow-up if operators want it): a scheduled worker emitting these as periodic gauges per tenant — the route-driven counter covers the "operator is actively looking" signal which is the dominant query pattern; a worker is additive on top. Files: `src/tagpulse/core/otel_metrics.py`, `src/tagpulse/api/routes/tags.py`, `tests/unit/test_tag_reconciliation.py`.

### Changed

- **`scripts/start-sprint.sh` learned `--carry` for in-flight planning artifacts.** Resolves the chicken-and-egg between the "plan first — write ADRs / design docs / roadmap edits before coding" rule and the "clean tree before branching" enforcement in `start-sprint.sh`. The canonical flow is unchanged: run `scripts/start-sprint.sh <NN> <topic>` from a clean `main`, then commit planning artifacts onto the new `sprint-NN/<topic>` branch so they ride into the draft kickoff PR. New escape hatch `scripts/start-sprint.sh --carry <NN> <topic>` covers the case where planning already started on `main` — it `git stash push --include-untracked`s the WIP, creates the branch, pops the stash, and commits the carried files as `chore(sprint-NN): start branch with planning artifacts` (instead of the usual empty kickoff commit). `--carry` only works from `main` (errors out otherwise). Documented in [docs/guides/contributor-workflow.md](docs/guides/contributor-workflow.md) §"Planning artifacts and the chicken-and-egg" and cross-linked from `.github/copilot-instructions.md` so the agent picks the right path. Files: `scripts/start-sprint.sh`, `docs/guides/contributor-workflow.md`, `.github/copilot-instructions.md`.

- **Sprint 51 / 52 roadmap reconciliation.** Flipped `## Sprint 51 — Tag registry UI` from `(planned)` → `(shipped)` and tagged each phase bullet (A–F) with the merged cross-repo PR that shipped it ([TagPulse#69](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/pull/69) for the Phase A design doc; [TagPulse-UI#55](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/55), [#57](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/57), [#58](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/58), [#59](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/59), [#60](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/60) for phases B/D/E/F/C respectively — #60 replaces stack-merge-auto-closed #56). Phase G marked `partial`: this PR flips the roadmap entry; the ADR 028 v1.2 status update + runbook "Operator UI quick reference" section land in a follow-up since they're scoped to operator-runbook curation rather than the UI delivery itself. Added a new `## Sprint 52 — GET /bulk-operations list endpoint (shipped — PR #71)` entry between Sprint 51 and the Backlog covering the C3-deferred list surface that Phase F needed; cross-links to the existing Sprint 52 CHANGELOG bullet and to [docs/design/tag-registry-ui.md §7.2](docs/design/tag-registry-ui.md). Resolved the open `tag_known=NULL` UX policy item in Sprint 51's risk list inline ("option (a) — registry list is over the `tags` table, reads in the brief unclassified window appear nowhere by design"). Files: `docs/roadmap.md`.

### Added

- **Sprint 52 — `GET /bulk-operations` list endpoint (closes Sprint 50 Phase C3 deferred surface).** New endpoint `GET /v1/bulk-operations` (admin or editor; tenant-scoped via the standard `require_role` + RLS plumbing) returns the per-tenant inbox of `pending_bulk_operations` rows so the Phase F admin UI in TagPulse-UI can render the two-person-rule review queue. Sprint 50 Phase C3 shipped the `pending_bulk_operations` substrate + `GET/POST .../bulk-operations/{id}{,/approve,/reject}` but deliberately deferred the list surface — the route module's own docstring carried the caveat *"The list endpoint (`GET /bulk-operations?status=pending`) is intentionally out of scope for C3 — operators query `pending_bulk_operations` directly via the admin UI's existing audit-log surface until the C5 unified shape lands"*. C5 landed and operators want a typed surface, so this PR closes that gap. Query params: `?status` (validated as `^(pending|approved|rejected|executed|expired)$` — 422 on typo so operators get a real signal instead of an empty list), `?operation` (1..64 chars, free-form filter on the operation discriminator — `tags.import` / `tags.bulk_patch` / `tags.bulk_retire` today, future bulk ops without route changes), `?limit` (1..500, default 100), `?offset` (>=0, default 0). Order: `created_at DESC` (newest-first matches the operator triage pattern — review the most-recent submits first). Response is `list[PendingBulkOperationResponse]` — the **existing** schema from Phase C3, which already omits the raw `payload` bytes (operators inspect via the `sample` first-10-EPCs field; the full CSV would inflate response sizes uselessly and bypass the C3 review-surface contract). Role: `require_role("admin", "editor")` mirrors the existing `GET /bulk-operations/{id}` endpoint in the same router so a reviewer who can fetch a single row can also list — symmetric with the per-id detail endpoint.
