§4 documents the three reconciliation views with their query semantics (`registered-unread` honors `?days=`, `unregistered-reading` honors `?days=`, `bindings-on-retired` ignores it — point-in-time), curl examples for JSON and CSV export, the spreadsheet-binding CSV contract (verbatim column order per view from `src/tagpulse/services/tag_reconciliation.py:_HEADERS` — adding columns OK, renaming/reordering is breaking), interpretation guidance per view ("rising registered-unread = onboarded inventory never deployed", "rising unregistered-reading = check registrar worker lag first" with the p95 < 10 s SLI, "rising bindings-on-retired = bind/retire ordering bug"), and known gotchas (the empty-result-still-emits-header property, `unregistered-reading` may include reads the registrar hasn't classified yet). [docs/runbooks/README.md](docs/runbooks/README.md) gains a new row under "Migrations & cutovers" tagged Sprint 50 Phase F2. **F3 (ADR + remediation flips).** [docs/adr/028-tags-as-first-class-entity.md](docs/adr/028-tags-as-first-class-entity.md) status flipped `Accepted (Sprint 50, May 2026)` → **`Implemented (Sprint 50, May 2026)`** with a new v1.0 (2026-05-23, Implemented) decision-history entry enumerating Phases A through G with migration numbers (043/044/045/046/047/048) and file paths so a future ADR-audit grep finds the runtime artefacts without spelunking through CHANGELOG. [docs/adr/README.md](docs/adr/README.md) ADR 028 row flips `accepted` → `implemented` — first ADR to use the `implemented` lowercase status string in the README (matches the existing `accepted` / `proposed` / `deferred` convention). [docs/design/reference-design-remediation.md](docs/design/reference-design-remediation.md) row 2.14 "Tag identity & ownership registry" flipped `Reopened — Accepted` / `TBD` → `✅ Done` / Sprint 50 with the shipped-feature summary in the notes cell (registry CRUD, cross-tenant transfers, bulk CSV with five governance controls, registrar worker, three reconciliation views, unified audit log). **F4 (roadmap close-out).** [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) Sprint 50 header flipped `(planned)` → **`(shipped)`**; goal preamble updated `Accepted 2026-05-23` → `Implemented 2026-05-23`. Each Phase A–F tagged `[shipped]` with inline migration numbers, file paths (`src/tagpulse/services/tags.py`, `src/tagpulse/services/tag_reconciliation.py`, `src/tagpulse/workers/tag_registrar_worker.py`), and runbook cross-links so a future sprint planner reading the roadmap sees the artefact pointers without opening CHANGELOG. **Phase G is explicitly tagged `[deferred to a follow-up sprint]`** — the 1335-test unit suite (`make check` clean across all phases) covers schema, service layer, governance invariants, and reconciliation queries; the deferred items are the optional polish (integration suite against live Postgres, `tagpulse_tag_reconciliation_rows{view}` Prometheus gauges, dedicated soft-asset-gate unit test, registrar `lag_seconds` histogram for the SLI dashboard) — none are blockers, all can land in a future cleanup sprint without ADR or schema change. `make check` clean: **1335 passed, 1 skipped** (unchanged from Phase E). Files: `docs/data-models.md`, `docs/adr/028-tags-as-first-class-entity.md`, `docs/adr/README.md`, `docs/design/reference-design-remediation.md`, `docs/roadmap.md`, `docs/runbooks/README.md`, `docs/runbooks/tag-registry-operations.md` (new).

- **Sprint 50 (planned) — Tag registry v1 ([ADR 028](docs/adr/028-tags-as-first-class-entity.md), gap 2.14).** [ADR 028](docs/adr/028-tags-as-first-class-entity.md) promoted Proposed → **Accepted (Sprint 50, May 2026)** with all five open questions resolved inline: (OQ 1) soft gating via nullable `tag_reads.tag_known` populated by a registrar worker — ingest hot path unchanged; (OQ 2) `epc_hex` as the natural key with a denormalized `gs1_uri TEXT NULL` and partial index, plus lenient GS1 parse; (OQ 3) **never** auto-register on first read (no setting — TagPulse is pre-GA, dropped `'first_read'` from the `source` enum); (OQ 4) CSV import capped at 10 000 rows with `413` above, 10/hr per-tenant rate limit, all-or-nothing validation; (OQ 5) **dropped the `tag_batches` table** — batches modelled as [ADR 020 labels](docs/adr/020-labels-first-class.md) with a reserved `batch.*` key namespace (`batch`, `batch.received_at`, `batch.description`, `batch.supplier`), reverse lookup is O(1) via `entity_labels`, range-based optimization for sequential reels deferred under YAGNI. ADR also fixes a 7-control governance section (default `status='registered'` on import never `active`, every bulk op is dry-run-first with a single-use confirmation token, scope-required filters via `labels[batch]=` or `epc_list[]≤1000`, two-person rule above `tenants.tag_bulk_two_person_threshold` default 10 000, scheduled read-only reconciliation reports, soft-state-only lifecycle transitions, single audit log keyed on `(actor, action, batch, count, request_id)`). [ADR 020](docs/adr/020-labels-first-class.md) Related line cross-links ADR 028 as the downstream consumer that reserves the `batch.*` key namespace. [docs/design/reference-design-remediation.md](docs/design/reference-design-remediation.md) row 2.14 flipped Reopened/Proposed → Reopened/Accepted; row 2.16 already noted dropped. [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) gains **Sprint 50 — Tag registry v1 (planned)** with Phases A–G (schema migrations including reserved label-key registration at tenant provisioning; registry CRUD + transfers API; bulk import with 5 governance controls; registrar worker that owns `tag_known` writes and confirms ADR 022 soft-asset interaction; read-only reconciliation reports; docs + ADR status flip + gap 2.14 → Done; validation), out-of-scope list pulling ADR 028's 5 non-goals through verbatim, and two risks locked at planning (**registrar worker lag SLI: p95 < 10 s**; **reserved-label-key collision policy: refuse migration + manual-intervention error**, no auto-rename). No code yet — implementation lands in Sprint 50. ### Added

- **Sprint 47 — Edge wire format v2: Pi-gateway producer + reader-to-edge LAN contract (ADR-027).** Closes the producer side of the v2 wire-format work begun in Sprint 46 ([roadmap §Sprint 47](docs/roadmap.md)). Three deliverables. **Phase A (LAN contract).** New companion spec [docs/design/reader-to-edge-contract.md](docs/design/reader-to-edge-contract.md) (v0.1, Proposed) and ratifying [ADR-027](docs/adr/027-reader-to-edge-contract.md) resolve every open question in [edge-wire-format-v2 §8.4](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md) (Q-LAN-1..Q-LAN-7): CSV-over-line-stream is the only normative transport (TCP/file/serial all reuse the same row schema; UDP rejected for lossy semantics); the Pi owns the wall clock (reader emits a monotonic `reader_ts_ms` boot counter only — resolves spec v2 §8 Q7); explicit cycle boundaries mandatory via `record_kind ∈ {read, cycle_end, cycle_empty, reset, error}`; sensor failure is encoded by **column omission** never by sentinel values (so the Pi-gateway producer's "omit `tmp`/`hum` when None" rule from §3.4 has a matching reader-side contract); per-SKU JSON capability descriptor mandatory at startup (`antenna_count`, `supports_cycle_empty`, `max_epcs_per_cycle`, etc.); reset signalling via explicit `reset` record OR a `reader_ts_ms` regression (either is normative); the spec v2 §1 header typo `issi`→`rssi` is rejected at startup so producers can't accidentally honour the typo. LAN side is physically trusted (no auth in v0.1 — Pi and reader share a private subnet); auth moves to v0.2 if/when a reader vendor wants to skip the Pi. ADR-027 status is Proposed, promotes to Accepted after at least one vendor reviews. **Phase B (Pi-gateway producer).** New pure-logic producer at [clients/pi/tagpulse_edge/wm_v2_producer.py](clients/pi/tagpulse_edge/wm_v2_producer.py) (~330 LOC): `WmV2Producer` dataclass + `CycleEpcObservation` frozen dataclass. Public API is two methods — `begin_session()` (called by the MQTT client wrapper on reconnect; clears in-memory diff state and forces the next emit to be a `t=0` snap) and `emit_cycle(ts_ms, lat, lon, cycle) -> list[dict]` (returns JSON-ready dicts the caller publishes via MQTT — producer is transport-agnostic on purpose so unit tests don't need an MQTT broker and so the same module can later back a non-MQTT egress). Cycle-diff state is keyed by `(antenna, EPC)` so a tag moving antennas inside the same field surfaces correctly: tag adds an antenna → `t=1` add for that `(an, epc)`; tag drops one antenna while still present on another → no message (the EPC is still globally present); tag leaves all antennas → single per-EPC `t=2` with the minimal `{t, sn, ts, epc}` payload per spec §2.2. EPC validation, antenna/RSSI/count ranges, lat/lon ranges, and the 5000-entry snap soft-cap are duplicated locally from `src/tagpulse/ingestion/wm_wire_format.py` (NOT imported) so the Pi-gateway package stays self-contained for Pi-side packaging (Debian / OS image / wheel). The duplication is intentional and is called out in the module docstring; any future wire-format change must be matched in both places — Phase C catches this via the round-trip parse test (see below). Two snap-trigger profiles: **Profile A** (`snap_period_s=300.0, snap_cycle_count=100`, the default — snap when wall-clock elapsed >= 300 s OR consecutive delta cycles >= 100) and **Profile B** (`snap_period_s=-1, snap_cycle_count=0` — snap every cycle, for the conformance harness and for high-churn / low-cycle-count debug scenarios). Sentinel convention: `> 0` is the threshold, `0` triggers every cycle (Profile B), `< 0` disables that gate. Sensor field omission rule: `tmp` / `hum` are omitted from the entry dict when their `CycleEpcObservation` value is `None` so the dict serializes to JSON without `null` (the subscriber's `_reject_explicit_null_*` validators would reject `null` per spec §6 `explicit_null`). Soft-cap warning logs `len(entries) > SNAP_SOFT_CAP_ENTRIES` but does not truncate. 34 unit tests in [clients/pi/tests/test_wm_v2_producer.py](clients/pi/tests/test_wm_v2_producer.py) cover first-emit-is-snap (empty + non-empty), delta correctness, antenna-move semantics, snap-period and snap-cycle-count triggers (with the "initial snap + 3 deltas + 1 snap" pattern asserting the `>=` semantics), `begin_session()` clearing state and forcing the next snap, Profile B's snap-every-cycle behaviour, sensor omission, EPC normalization to uppercase hex, parametrized invalid-EPC and out-of-range field rejection, duplicate `(an, epc)` key in cycle rejection, lat/lon range, negative ts rejection, the `t=2` minimal-keys constraint (no `lat`/`lon`/`an` for bandwidth — matches `WmDisappearedMessage` defaults), and the soft-cap warning log assertion. **Phase C (end-to-end conformance harness).** New [clients/pi/tests/test_wm_v2_producer_e2e.py](clients/pi/tests/test_wm_v2_producer_e2e.py) (12 tests across 7 spec-section test classes plus 4 parametrized cases) drives the producer through scripted scenarios for all 7 of [edge-wire-format-v2 §5](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md): §5.1 steady-state (initial snap then zero messages for 10 identical cycles), §5.2 mixed deltas (5 adds + 3 disappearances → 5 × `t=1` + 3 × `t=2`), §5.3 periodic snapshot (snap trigger fires at 11 s with `snap_period_s=10.0`), §5.4 empty snapshot (both session-start and periodic trigger paths), §5.5 reboot (post-`begin_session` emit is a snap regardless of cycle content), §5.6 subscriber outage (post-reconnect `begin_session` produces a snap with the full current present-set, not just the recent deltas), §5.7 lost `t=2` healed by next snap (the composite scenario where a hypothetical lost `t=2` is reconciled at the next periodic snap whose authoritative EPC set forces the absent EPC into `gone` on the subscriber). Every emitted dict from every scenario is **round-tripped through `pydantic.TypeAdapter[WmMessage].validate_json`** — the same discriminated-union parser the production subscriber uses in `_handle_wm_v2_message`. This closes the duplication loop from Phase B: the producer cannot emit a message the subscriber would reject under spec §6, and any future wire-format change that breaks the duplication will fail every test in this file at parse time. Lives in `clients/pi/tests/` (not `tests/conformance/` or `tests/unit/`) because it imports both the Pi-gateway producer (`tagpulse_edge.*`) and the backend wire-format parser (`tagpulse.ingestion.wm_wire_format.*`); only the Pi test environment has both on its path. The backend-side §5 conformance harness at [tests/unit/test_wm_v2_conformance.py](tests/unit/test_wm_v2_conformance.py) (Sprint 46 Phase D) remains the subscriber-side companion; together the two suites span the full conformance matrix end-to-end. **Out of scope for Sprint 47** (deferred): the LAN-side CSV parser that produces `CycleEpcObservation` records on the Pi from a reader's TCP/file/serial stream (Sprint 48, gated on first concrete reader integration — the producer module is reader-agnostic on purpose); WM reader-direct firmware speaking v2 directly to the cellular broker (gated on WM dev capacity + vendor sign-off on the new `reader-to-edge-contract.md`); server → reader config push (spec §9.3 #1 — v2.1); heartbeat / reader-error `t=3` / `t=4` (spec §9.3 #2 — v2.1); binary wire format v3 (spec §9.3 #3). **Spec follow-ups now closed**: v2 spec §8.4 Q-LAN-1..Q-LAN-7 resolved; v2 spec §8 Q7 (clock discipline) resolved by ADR-027 §3 Decision 3; spec §11 review-checklist item "`reader-to-edge-contract.md` drafted — Sprint 47 companion" checked off. Files: `docs/design/reader-to-edge-contract.md`, `docs/adr/027-reader-to-edge-contract.md`, `docs/adr/README.md`, `docs/roadmap.md`, `clients/pi/tagpulse_edge/__init__.py`, `clients/pi/tagpulse_edge/wm_v2_producer.py`, `clients/pi/tests/test_wm_v2_producer.py`, `clients/pi/tests/test_wm_v2_producer_e2e.py`.

- **Sprint 46 Phase E + F — v2 wire-format OTel counters and operator-facing docs.** Closes the last two phases of Sprint 46 per [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) and [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md §10](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md). **Phase E (observability)** wires the seven metric objects spec §6 promised but Phases C/D explicitly deferred: four counters added at the v2 ingest call sites (`tagpulse_mqtt_wm_rejections_total{reason}` bumped alongside the existing `_record_rejection("wm_v2", reason)` + `_persist_mqtt_drop(...)` pair inside `_handle_wm_v2_message`'s `except ValidationError`, labels match the §6 reason table for the ones the Phase C handler can actually emit — `missing_type`, `unknown_type`, `invalid_epc`, `missing_required_field`, `epcs_wrong_type`, `invalid_snap_entry`, `explicit_null`, `invalid_json`, `invalid_schema`; the §6 reasons `device_not_found`/`sn_jwt_mismatch`/`clock_skew` are not emitted yet because they require the §4.5 `sn → device_id` resolution + JWT cross-check still deferred to a later sprint; `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_snap_large_total{sn}` bumped on the soft-cap path with `sn` as a string label per spec — cardinality bounded by device count, which is the same axis the existing per-device counters scale on; `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_sub_no_presence_total` bumped in `apply_disappeared` when `prior_status is None` so the dashboard can distinguish "subscriber lost state across rolling deploy" from "producer never sent a snap"; `tagpulse_presence_reconcile_duration_seconds` histogram labelled `t ∈ {snap, appeared, disappeared}` wrapping each of the three reconciler dispatch branches in `_handle_wm_v2_message` via `time.perf_counter()` — measures reconciler work only, not the surrounding GUC set or `IngestionService.ingest()` fan-out which already have their own instrumentation); two presence-write counters added at the reconciler write sites (`tagpulse_presence_entries_total{status}` with `status ∈ {present, gone}` bumped `+= len(snap_state)` after the upsert in `reconcile_snap`, `+= len(gone_epcs)` after the gone-marking UPDATE, `+= 1` after `apply_appeared`'s single upsert, and `+= 1` in `apply_disappeared`'s transition branch — gives operators a denominator for the duration histogram and a "is the DB actually getting writes" health signal that doesn't depend on the broker); two signaling counters added at the event-bus emission chokepoint (`tagpulse_signaling_tag_appeared_total{source}` and `tagpulse_signaling_tag_disappeared_total{source}` with `source ∈ {snap, delta}` bumped inside `presence_reconciler._emit()` via a topic-based branch on `Topic.SIGNALING_TAG_APPEARED` vs `Topic.SIGNALING_TAG_DISAPPEARED` — single chokepoint guarantees no caller can emit without a counter bump, and the `source` label lets dashboards prove the reader is sending real-time deltas rather than relying on snap-only reconciliation). All seven definitions live in a new `# -- Sprint 46 Phase E ... --` section at the top of [src/tagpulse/core/otel_metrics.py](src/tagpulse/core/otel_metrics.py) (~96 lines, inserted before the Sprint 35 ADR-020 labels block so they sort together with the rest of the MQTT-ingest counters). Every `.add()` / `.record()` call site is wrapped in `try: ... except Exception: logger.exception(...)` mirroring the existing `_record_rejection` defensive pattern — instrumentation failures cannot stall the MQTT loop (already a critical-path guarantee from Sprint 28 C1). The histogram uses `meter.create_histogram(...)` — first histogram in `otel_metrics.py`, but the OTel SDK API is identical to the counter path and the in-memory metric reader test pattern from `test_sprint28_mqtt_metrics.py` extends to histograms via `p.count` / `p.sum` instead of `p.value`. **Phase E tests** — new file [tests/unit/test_wm_v2_metrics.py](tests/unit/test_wm_v2_metrics.py) (9 tests across 6 test classes, all passing) installs an OTel `InMemoryMetricReader` at module scope, rebinds every Phase E metric object on the shared `tagpulse` meter (and the captured imports in both `mqtt_subscriber` and `presence_reconciler` since those modules captured the originals at import time), then drives the real `MqttSubscriber._handle_tag_read` against scripted `_FakeSession` + `_FakeBus` instances per scenario and asserts the counter snapshot includes the expected `(name, labels) → value` tuple: rejection counter bumps with `reason=invalid_epc` on a `t=1` body with non-hex EPC; snap-large counter bumps with `sn="7777"` on a 5001-entry snap AND does NOT bump on a 1-entry snap; sub-no-presence counter bumps exactly once on a `t=2` for an unknown EPC; presence-entries counter accumulates `status=present` and `status=gone` correctly across a mixed snap (2 new + 1 gone); signaling counters bump with `source=snap` from a snap reconcile and with `source=delta` from a `t=1` (with a baseline-diff assertion since the in-memory reader accumulates across all tests in the module); histogram records points with `t=snap` after a snap reconcile and with both `t=appeared` and `t=disappeared` labels after running an appeared + disappeared in sequence. Test infrastructure mirrors `test_wm_v2_conformance.py` (`_FakeSession` with FIFO `select_results`, `_SessionCtx` async-context-manager, `_FakeBus` capturing `(topic, event)`) but adds the meter-rebind fixture pattern from `test_sprint28_mqtt_metrics.py` plus a new `_collect_histogram(reader, name)` helper alongside the existing `_collect_counters(reader)` helper. **Phase F (docs)** — two doc deliverables targeting the two distinct audiences for the v2 contract. [docs/guides/device-developer-guide.md](docs/guides/device-developer-guide.md) gains a new **§3.4 "v2 wire format — presence-oriented (Sprint 46+)"** inserted between the existing §3.3 first-message walkthrough and §4 HTTP reference, positioned so a producer-side developer reading top-to-bottom hits v1 first (the older, still-supported path) and then v2 with explicit "both supported indefinitely per spec §9.1 #4" language up front so nobody thinks they have to migrate. Coverage: the `t ∈ {0, 1, 2}` table mapping each message kind to "when to publish" semantics (snap cadence default 300 s OR every 100 read cycles AND on every successful MQTT reconnect — without snaps the subscriber has no recovery primitive for a missed `t=2`); explicit callout that v2 ships on the SAME `tag-reads` topic as v1 with integer `t` as the discriminator, which matters because operators reading topic-subscription configs shouldn't expect a new topic; one minimal JSON example per message type (snap with two EPCs and no GPS, appeared with full GPS, disappeared with only `epc`); the MQTT settings table pinning QoS 1, retain false, `clean_session=false`, TLS per-environment, and auth unchanged (key callout: `clean_session=false` is what lets the broker queue messages across short disconnects, which combined with snap-on-reconnect is the v2 reliability story); a seven-item producer-responsibility list covering EPC hex casing (uppercase, no separators, rejected as `invalid_epc` otherwise), `sn` semantics (monotonic per-device, 32-bit unsigned wrap fine, informational only this sprint), `ts` units (epoch ms integer, UTC), the explicit-null rejection rule (omit unsupported sensor fields, never send `null` — the §6 `explicit_null` reason exists specifically so the subscriber can tell "no GPS this cycle" from "config drift, field shouldn't be here"), snap cadence rationale, multi-antenna entries explicitly allowed in the same `epcs[]` array (not duplicates), and the soft-cap behavior (5000-entry snap accepted but bumps `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_snap_large_total{sn}`); a pointer at the Shape-2 reference implementation in `clients/pi/tagpulse_edge/`; and a final `tag_presence` SELECT template for "what did the subscriber actually store" with the cross-link to the operator runbook. New runbook [docs/runbooks/wm-wire-format-v2.md](docs/runbooks/wm-wire-format-v2.md) (~165 lines) is the operator-side companion: §1 "What's at reader X right now?" — three SQL templates against `tag_presence` (currently-present with required `set_config('app.current_tenant_id', ...)` GUC for the RLS policy from migration 042; tags recently gone within the last hour; per-device present-EPC counts; EPC-history-across-devices lookup) plus an important gotcha that `tag_presence` is **state**, not history, so "where was this EPC at 14:32" still needs `tag_reads`, and `t=2` writes no `tag_reads` row per spec §4.3 (only transitions `tag_presence.status`); §2 Phase E counter cheat-sheet — a row-per-counter table giving operators "what rising means" + "operator action" for all seven counters, plus the explicit rule that single `wm_sub_no_presence_total` bumps post-rolling-deploy are normal but a sustained non-zero rate is the canonical signal that snap-on-reconnect isn't firing; §3 the spec §9.2 #1 "two subscriber replicas during ACA rolling deploy" gotcha — what operators may see in the metric spikes (brief duplicate `entries_total` rows, two `_emit()` publishes for the same transition that the event bus dedups for a short TTL, RSSI/antenna flap), the explicit self-heal time bound ("never act unless inconsistency persists > 10 minutes" with rationale "next snap cadence puts every row back to authoritative state — 300 s default") and an `az containerapp revision list` + `revision deactivate` diagnosis recipe if it doesn't heal; §4 the "tag stuck present" customer-support triage walkthrough — find the row, check producer health via most-recent `tag_reads`, check rejection counters against the `mqtt_drops` audit table for the same device, and as a last-resort emergency-only "manual gone" UPDATE template (with explicit "file a follow-up: the reader either lost its presence cache without snap-on-reconnect or its exit-timeout is misconfigured" so the manual healing doesn't become a habit); and §5 the standard "where to go next" cross-link table to producer guide, spec, reconciler code, dispatch code, and the `otel_metrics.py` Phase E section. Listed under "Sprint 16 conformance stubs" sister directory but in the new operator-runbook style. `make check` clean: **1176 passed, 1 skipped** (+9 from Phase D's 1167). `ruff check` and `mypy --strict` both clean. **Sprint 46 closes**: Phase A (ADR 025 + 026), Phase B (`tag_presence` migration + Pydantic models), Phase C (dispatch + reconciler + two new event-bus topics), Phase D (12-scenario conformance suite), Phase E (7 OTel counters + 9 metric tests), Phase F (device-developer-guide §3.4 + operator runbook). **Out of scope for Sprint 46** (Sprint 47 + later): full §4.5 `sn → device_id` resolution + JWT cross-check (the three §6 reasons `device_not_found`/`sn_jwt_mismatch`/`clock_skew` get wired then), producer-side reference implementation in `clients/pi/tagpulse_edge/` end-to-end with golden-snapshot conformance harness (Sprint 47 per roadmap), reader-direct WM firmware proof-of-concept (Sprint 47), config-push / heartbeat / reader-error message types `t=3`/`t=4` (deferred to v2.1+ per spec §9.3). Files: `src/tagpulse/core/otel_metrics.py`, `src/tagpulse/ingestion/mqtt_subscriber.py`, `src/tagpulse/ingestion/presence_reconciler.py`, `tests/unit/test_wm_v2_metrics.py`, `docs/guides/device-developer-guide.md`, `docs/runbooks/wm-wire-format-v2.md`, `docs/roadmap.md`.

- **Sprint 46 Phase D — v2 wire-format conformance suite.** New file [tests/unit/test_wm_v2_conformance.py](tests/unit/test_wm_v2_conformance.py) (12 tests across 9 test classes) closes the Phase D coverage gap in [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md): drives the *real* `MqttSubscriber._handle_tag_read` → `_handle_wm_v2_message` → `presence_reconciler` → event-bus path from MQTT payload bytes, with only the SQLAlchemy session and `IngestionService.ingest()` faked. This is the end-to-end complement to the Phase C unit tests — `tests/unit/test_presence_reconciler.py` exercises the reconciler in isolation against a scripted session and `tests/unit/test_mqtt_subscriber_v2_dispatch.py` stubs the reconciler to inspect dispatch routing; the new conformance file runs *both* layers together so a regression in either the reconciler's SELECT-then-upsert sequence or the subscriber's dispatch wiring fails the scenario-level assertion (events emitted on the bus + `ingest()` call counts) rather than a unit-level proxy. Tests are organized one-per-spec-section against [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md §5](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md): **§5.1 steady-state** (no wire messages → no writes, no events — the trivial baseline that pins the "snap-only when changes happen" producer contract); **§5.2 mixed deltas** (5 `t=1` + 3 `t=2` messages → 5 appeared events, 3 disappeared events, 5 `ingest()` calls because `t=2` writes no `tag_reads` row per spec §4.3); **§5.3 periodic snapshot** (snap with 3 entries reconciles against scripted current-present-set `[B, C, X]` — B+C in both → no events, A in snap only → appeared, X in current only → gone, 3 `tag_reads` inserts per spec §4.4); **§5.4 empty snapshot** (`epcs:[]` against current `[A, B]` → 2 gone events, 0 `ingest()` calls — the "field empty" signal); **§5.5 producer reboot** (snap-on-reconnect against empty present-set → every entry surfaces as appeared, demonstrates the reboot self-heal property without any wire-level reboot signal per ADR-025 §3.6); **§5.6 subscriber replay** (split across two tests — replayed `t=1` for already-`present` EPC is a no-op upsert with no duplicate event but the `tag_reads` row still flows, and replayed `t=2` for never-seen EPC is silently dropped per spec §6 `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_sub_no_presence_total` semantics); **§5.7 lost-`t=2` healed by snap** (the composite scenario from spec §5.7 — a missed `t=2` leaves AAAA `present`, next snap omits AAAA → reconciler marks it gone and emits the missed event, no operator intervention). Plus **large-snap** (split — 1000-entry snap processes without error producing 1000 appeared events + 1000 `ingest()` calls, AND a 5001-entry snap exercises the spec §6 soft-cap path with a caplog assertion that "above soft cap" is logged but `_persist_mqtt_drop` is *not* awaited — the soft cap is a warning-only signal, Phase E will wire the `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_snap_large_total{sn}` counter on the same code path), and **v1/v2 coexistence** (split — interleaved v1-then-v2 messages on the same subscriber instance correctly route to their respective handlers with no cross-talk, and a v1 payload carrying a string-valued `t` field is NOT misclassified as v2 — the dispatch hook's narrow `isinstance(raw.get("t"), int)` guard rejects strings, which matters because v1 publishers historically use `t` as a free-form metadata key). Test infrastructure: a `_FakeSession` that scripts SELECT results in FIFO order (so the reconciler's "current present EPCs" query returns whatever the scenario specifies) and no-ops INSERT/UPDATE statements, paired with a `_SessionCtx` async-context-manager wrapper so the subscriber's `async with self._session_factory() as session:` pattern works unchanged; a `_FakeBus` that captures `(topic, event)` tuples for per-topic event-payload extraction; and a `_build_subscriber()` helper that wires a real `MqttSubscriber(session_factory=..., event_bus=...)` with `_build_ingestion_service` and `_persist_mqtt_drop` patched to AsyncMocks. File lives in `tests/unit/` (not `tests/conformance/`) because the latter is a stub-only directory waiting for a device-under-test harness ([tests/conformance/README.md](tests/conformance/README.md) — Sprint 16 spec stubs against `edge-device-contract.md` §3) and the `Makefile`'s `test` target only walks `tests/unit`; the "conformance" label refers to the file's spec-section organization rather than a separate test runner. `make check` clean: **1167 passed, 1 skipped** (+12 from Phase C's 1155); `ruff check` and `mypy --strict` both clean. Out of scope for Phase D (still ahead in Sprint 46): OTel counters per spec §6 (Phase E — `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_rejections_total{reason}`, `tagpulse_presence_reconcile_duration_seconds`, `tagpulse_presence_entries_total{status}`, `tagpulse_signaling_tag_appeared_total`, `tagpulse_signaling_tag_disappeared_total`, plus the soft-cap counter the large-snap test pins the call-site for), device-developer-guide v2 section and operator runbook addendum (Phase F). Files: `tests/unit/test_wm_v2_conformance.py`.

- **Sprint 46 Phase C — v2 wire format dispatch, presence reconciler, and two new event-bus topics.** Wires the [Phase B](src/tagpulse/ingestion/wm_wire_format.py) discriminated union into the runtime MQTT path per [ADR-025 §4.3](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md) and ratifies the [ADR-026](docs/adr/026-presence-model.md) reconciliation algorithm against the new `tag_presence` table. `_handle_tag_read` ([src/tagpulse/ingestion/mqtt_subscriber.py](src/tagpulse/ingestion/mqtt_subscriber.py)) gains a single-line dispatch hook at the top of its JSON-parse branch — `isinstance(raw, dict) and isinstance(raw.get("t"), int)` routes to a new `_handle_wm_v2_message` method; every other shape (lists, dicts without `t`, dicts with non-integer `t`) falls through to the unchanged v1 path per spec §9.1 #4 coexistence. The detection predicate is intentionally narrow — a v1 publisher that happens to send `{"t": "x"}` (string `t`) keeps working, because hex EPCs and `tag_id` strings have always been valid `t` field names in v1 metadata blobs. New module [src/tagpulse/ingestion/presence_reconciler.py](src/tagpulse/ingestion/presence_reconciler.py) (~290 LOC, three public coroutines) owns every write to `tag_presence` and every `SIGNALING_TAG_APPEARED` / `SIGNALING_TAG_DISAPPEARED` emission: `reconcile_snap()` implements spec §4.2 verbatim (SELECT current `present` epcs → upsert each `epcs[]` entry with `ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE` → UPDATE present-but-absent EPCs to `status='gone'` → emit one transition event per appeared/gone delta), pre-collapsing multi-antenna entries to one row per EPC by picking the strongest RSSI (spec §9 — RSSI is dBm, "stronger" means closer to 0) so the `ON CONFLICT` clause never needs a `GREATEST` and the event stream stays one-per-EPC; `apply_appeared()` checks the prior row state and only emits when the EPC was absent or `gone` (present→present is a no-op upsert so re-appearance signals on already-present tags don't spam the bus); `apply_disappeared()` silently ignores never-seen EPCs (spec §6 — future Phase E bumps `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_sub_no_presence_total`), refreshes `last_seen` without emitting on already-`gone` EPCs (idempotent under sub replay), and only emits on the present→gone transition. All three return `(emitted, ...)` or `bool` for caller logging/metrics. The `_handle_wm_v2_message` method validates via a module-level `TypeAdapter[WmMessage]` (built once at import so we don't pay the discriminated-union schema cost per message), classifies `ValidationError` into a spec §6 reason label via the new `_classify_wm_validation_error()` helper (handles `union_tag_not_found`/`union_tag_invalid` for missing/unknown `t`, EPC validator failures for `invalid_epc`, explicit-null messages for `explicit_null`, `extra_forbidden` on `epcs` for `epcs_wrong_type`, missing `epcs`/`lat`/`lon` for `missing_required_field`, missing snap-entry fields for `invalid_snap_entry`, generic fallback `invalid_schema`), and routes the drop through the existing `_record_rejection("wm_v2", reason)` + `_persist_mqtt_drop(...)` pair — no dedicated `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_rejections_total{reason}` counter yet (explicitly Phase E per [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md)). On successful validation it opens a session and sets `app.current_tenant_id` inline via `session.execute(text("SELECT set_config(...)"))` — the existing v1 path uses `_session_factory` directly without `tenant_context()`, so going inline here avoids refactoring unrelated paths while satisfying the `tag_presence` RLS policy from migration 042. Soft-cap check on `t=0` (`len(msg.epcs) > SNAP_SOFT_CAP_ENTRIES`) logs a warning but does NOT reject — full counter wiring is Phase E. Each variant dispatches to its reconciler coroutine, then maps to one-or-more `TagReadCreate` instances via two new module-level helpers `_wm_snap_to_tag_reads()` / `_wm_appeared_to_tag_read()` (and `_wm_location()` / `_wm_sensor_data()` for the shared per-row plumbing) per spec §4.4 — `sn` is informational this sprint (the topic-derived `device_id` wins per the existing v1 pattern; full §4.5 `devices.metadata->>'serial'` lookup + JWT cross-check defer to a later sprint), `ts` → `TagReadCreate.timestamp` via `datetime.fromtimestamp(ts/1000, tz=UTC)`, envelope-level `lat`/`lon` → `Location(source="reader_gnss")` shared across all reads in a snap (`None`/`None` collapses to no `Location`), per-entry `an` → `reader_antenna`, `epc` → both `tag_id` and `identity.epc_hex` (spec §4.4 explicit), `rssi` → `signal_strength` cast to float, and `cnt`/`tmp`/`hum` → a `sensor_data` JSONB dict using the field names `read_count`/`temperature_c`/`humidity_pct` (the latter two match the unit suffixes the dashboards already display); the dict is `None` not `{}` when all three fields are absent, so we don't write empty objects into the column. Each mapped `TagReadCreate` flows through the unchanged `IngestionService.ingest()` so the time-series side picks up full enrichment (zone lookup, binding resolution, dwell tracking, etc.) — `t=2` writes NO `tag_reads` row per spec §4.3 ("disappearance is a presence-table event only"). Two new topics on the event bus — `Topic.SIGNALING_TAG_APPEARED = "signaling.tag_appeared"` and `Topic.SIGNALING_TAG_DISAPPEARED = "signaling.tag_disappeared"` ([src/tagpulse/events/protocol.py](src/tagpulse/events/protocol.py)) — round out the v2 surface. Both carry the same payload shape `{tenant_id, device_id, epc, observed_at, source: "delta"|"snap"}` (`source` distinguishes synchronous reconcile-emitted transitions from delta-triggered ones for downstream rule fan-out). They join `Topic.SIGNALING_ATTRIBUTION_SETTLED` as the third input the future presence-based rule family (Sprint 47+) will subscribe to. **Supporting plumbing**: [src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py](src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py) `LocationSource` Literal extends from `"gps"|"fixed"|"inferred"` to also include `"reader_gnss"` (spec §4.4 mandates this exact tag for the GNSS fix embedded in v2 reader payloads); the DB column was already free-form `String(20)` with no CHECK constraint (migration 016), so adding the four-character tag is forward-only with no schema change. [src/tagpulse/models/database.py](src/tagpulse/models/database.py) gains the `TagPresenceModel` SQLAlchemy ORM class mirroring migration 042's table — PK `(tenant_id, device_id, epc)` with FKs to `tenants`/`devices` (CASCADE), `first_seen`/`last_seen` TIMESTAMPTZ, `status` String(16), `last_rssi`/`last_antenna` SmallInteger nullable. Docstring cross-references ADR-026 §3.1 and migration 042. **Tests** — two new files, 25 tests total, all passing under `make check`. [tests/unit/test_presence_reconciler.py](tests/unit/test_presence_reconciler.py) (14 tests) drives all three reconciler coroutines against a `_FakeSession` whose `execute()` returns scripted `_ScalarResult` objects (SELECTs return rows; INSERT/UPDATE statements are no-ops) and a `_FakeBus` that captures published events. Coverage maps to every spec §5 happy-path scenario — §5.2 first-snap-from-empty (3 EPCs → 3 appeared, 0 gone), §5.3 idempotent-snap (no events) + missing-from-snap-marked-gone, §5.4 empty-snap-marks-all-gone, §5.5 reader-rejoin (snap == prior present-set → no events, proves the self-healing property ADR-026 promised), §5.7 lost-`t=2`-healed-by-next-snap (composite scenario where a `t=2` was never delivered and the EPC's omission from the next snap produces the missed `disappeared` event without operator intervention), plus the multi-antenna-collapse property test (3 entries for the same EPC at different antennas → 1 row + 1 event), the event-payload-shape assertion (full key set + `source="snap"`), and the three `apply_appeared` state-machine cases (new EPC emits, present→present is no-op, gone→present emits) and three `apply_disappeared` cases (present→gone emits, never-seen silently ignored, already-gone idempotent). [tests/unit/test_mqtt_subscriber_v2_dispatch.py](tests/unit/test_mqtt_subscriber_v2_dispatch.py) (11 tests) exercises the dispatch hook end-to-end against the real `MqttSubscriber` with AsyncMock session + ingestion service + `_persist_mqtt_drop`, organized into four groups: `TestV2Dispatch` (integer `t` routes to v2; string `t` and `t`-absent fall through to v1 without touching the v2 handler; list payloads fall through), `TestV2HandlerHappyPaths` (snap with 2 EPCs invokes `reconcile_snap` + 2 `ingest()` calls + verifies one mapped `TagReadCreate` has `signal_strength=-60.0`, `reader_antenna=1`, `identity.epc_hex="AABBCCDD"`, `location.source="reader_gnss"`; appeared invokes `apply_appeared` + 1 ingest; disappeared invokes `apply_disappeared` + ZERO ingest calls per spec §4.3), `TestV2HandlerRejections` (unknown `t=99` → `_persist_mqtt_drop` called with `kind="wm_v2"` + `reason="unknown_type"` and the session is NEVER opened; invalid EPC `"XYZ"` → `reason="invalid_epc"`), and `TestClassifyValidationError` (direct unit coverage of `_classify_wm_validation_error()` against three real `ValidationError` instances from the actual `_WM_MESSAGE_ADAPTER`: missing `t` → `"missing_type"`, unknown `t=7` → `"unknown_type"`, short non-hex EPC → `"invalid_epc"`). `make check` clean: **1155 passed, 1 skipped** (+25 from Phase B's 1130); `ruff check` and `mypy --strict` both clean. **Out of scope for Phase C** (deferred to Phase D/E per spec §10 + [roadmap](docs/roadmap.md)): conformance suite covering the 7 §5 scenarios end-to-end against a real Postgres + broker (Phase D), large-snap stress test (Phase D), v1/v2 coexistence integration test (Phase D), dedicated OTel counters `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_rejections_total{reason}` / `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_snap_large_total{sn}` / `tagpulse_mqtt_wm_sub_no_presence_total` (Phase E), device-developer guide + operator runbook + producer-side reference impl (Phase F + Sprint 47), full §4.5 `sn → device_id` resolution via `devices.metadata->>'serial'` + JWT cross-check (later sprint — Phase C trusts the topic-derived `device_id` matching the v1 pattern, with a TODO pointing at spec §4.5). Files: `src/tagpulse/events/protocol.py`, `src/tagpulse/ingestion/mqtt_subscriber.py`, `src/tagpulse/ingestion/presence_reconciler.py`, `src/tagpulse/models/database.py`, `src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py`, `tests/unit/test_presence_reconciler.py`, `tests/unit/test_mqtt_subscriber_v2_dispatch.py`.

- **Sprint 46 Phase B — `tag_presence` migration + v2 wire-format Pydantic models.** Implements [ADR-026 §3.1](docs/adr/026-presence-model.md) storage schema and [ADR-025](docs/adr/025-edge-wire-format-v2.md) §2–§3 wire validation. New migration [`migrations/versions/042_tag_presence.py`](migrations/versions/042_tag_presence.py) creates the `tag_presence` regular table (not a hypertable per ADR 026 §3.1 — row count bounded by EPC fleet size, every update touches the current row) keyed on `(tenant_id, device_id, epc)` with a `status` CHECK constrained to `'present' | 'gone'`, two `WHERE status='present'` partial indexes covering `(tenant_id, device_id)` ("what's at this reader now") and `(tenant_id, epc)` ("where is this EPC now"), and RLS via the `app.current_tenant_id` session GUC per the migration 007 / 027 pattern. Deliberately omits the `last_seq` / `suspect` columns that earlier wire-format drafts called for — with the per-cycle counter removed from the wire (spec §3.1) and reconciliation synchronous on snap receipt (§4.2), there's no buffered state to be suspicious about. New module [`src/tagpulse/ingestion/wm_wire_format.py`](src/tagpulse/ingestion/wm_wire_format.py) defines a Pydantic v2 discriminated union (`WmSnapMessage` / `WmAppearedMessage` / `WmDisappearedMessage` keyed on integer `t`, with `WmSnapEntry` for `epcs[]` rows; `WmMessage` is the union root the subscriber will parse against in Phase C). `extra="forbid"` enforces both the §2.2 reserved-field rules (`v`, `hb`, `err`, `cfg`, `seq` rejected) and the shape constraints (`epcs` on `t=1`/`t=2` → §6 `epcs_wrong_type`; top-level `epc`/`an`/`rssi`/`cnt` on `t=0` rejected by the same mechanism). Field validators normalize EPCs to uppercase hex with 8..124 char even-length range check (§6 `invalid_epc`), and `mode="before"` model validators reject explicit `null` on optional sensor fields `tmp` / `hum` (§6 `explicit_null`) — distinguishing "key omitted" (default `None`, accepted) from "key supplied as `null`" (rejected). `lat` / `lon` are required-but-nullable on `t=0` / `t=1` and optional-nullable on `t=2`, matching the §2.2 presence table. New tests in [`tests/unit/test_wm_wire_format.py`](tests/unit/test_wm_wire_format.py) (24 cases) cover the spec §3 happy paths (snap with mixed sensor data, empty snap per §3.4, no-GNSS-fix snap, minimal `t=2`, `t=1` with and without sensors) and exhaustively pin every §6 rejection row (missing `t`, unknown `t` value, `epcs` on the wrong message type, missing `epcs` on `t=0`, missing `lat`/`lon` on `t=0`/`t=1`, snap entry missing a required field, explicit `null` on `tmp`/`hum` both at the envelope and inside `epcs[]`, malformed EPC parameterized across odd-length / non-hex / too-short / too-long, `rssi` above the dBm ceiling, `lat` outside `[-90, 90]`, and reserved field name `seq`). Identity resolution (`sn` → `device_id`), JWT cross-checks, clock-skew gating, and reconciliation against `tag_presence` are out of scope for Phase B — they ship in Phase C. `make check` clean: 1130 passed, 1 skipped (+24 from main). `alembic history` shows `041 -> 042 (head)`. Files: `migrations/versions/042_tag_presence.py`, `src/tagpulse/ingestion/wm_wire_format.py`, `tests/unit/test_wm_wire_format.py`, `docs/roadmap.md`.

- **Sprint 46 (proposed) — promote edge wire format v2 spec out of DRAFT + add Sprint 46/47 roadmap entries.** [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md) status flips from `DRAFT v0.2 — pre-review` to `ACCEPTED v1.0 (2026-05-23)`. Promotion is gated only on Phase-A items from §10 (§8 open questions resolved — done 2026-05-23 under Shape C; ADR 025 + ADR 026 landed — commit `58bbcc8`; roadmap entry — this commit). The two remaining §11 checklist items are intentionally scoped out of the promotion gate: §9.2 #5 (event-bus volume mitigation) gates *production rollout of high-churn readers*, not Sprint 46 ship; `docs/design/reader-to-edge-contract.md` is Sprint 47 companion work. [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) gains **Sprint 46 — Edge wire format v2: backend ingest + presence model (proposed)** with phases A–F mirroring spec §10 (Phase B: Alembic `042_tag_presence.py` + `src/tagpulse/ingestion/wm_wire_format.py` Pydantic discriminated union; Phase C: v2 branch in `_handle_tag_read` + new `presence_reconciler.py` + two new event-bus topics; Phase D: 7-scenario conformance suite + lost-`t=2` recovery + large-snap + reboot + v1/v2 coexistence tests; Phase E: OTel counters; Phase F: device-developer-guide + CHANGELOG + operator runbook), and **Sprint 47 — Edge wire format v2: producer side (proposed, gated on Sprint 46 ship)** covering both candidate producers (Pi-gateway reference impl in `clients/pi/tagpulse_edge/` and WM reader-direct firmware) plus a new `tests/conformance/` golden-snapshot harness that validates both producers against the same cases. Sprint 47 explicitly defers config-push, heartbeat / reader-error message types (`t=3`/`t=4`), and binary v3 to v2.1+ per spec §9.3. §11 review checklist updated — §9.2 #1/#2/#3 acceptance items checked off (single-replica trade-off, growth policy as backlog, two-table-write race mitigation path); roadmap-entry checkbox checked. Files: `docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md`, `docs/roadmap.md`.

- **Sprint 46 (proposed) — ADR 025 + ADR 026 ratify the v2 wire format and the server-side presence model.** New ADRs [docs/adr/025-edge-wire-format-v2.md](docs/adr/025-edge-wire-format-v2.md) and [docs/adr/026-presence-model.md](docs/adr/026-presence-model.md) promote the [edge-wire-format-v2 spec](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md) §3 wire contract and §4 server-side model out of "draft prose only" and into the architectural record. ADR 025 captures the high-order wire decisions (three message types `t ∈ {0=snap, 1=appeared, 2=disappeared}`; no on-the-wire `seq`; `epcs:[]` for empty cycles; MQTT-level atomicity instead of multi-message snap grouping; producer-agnostic — Pi-gateway or reader-direct firmware both honor the same contract; topic versioning reserved for v3) and explicitly references the KISS-pass commit (`155f1e5`) that collapsed snaps from N-messages-glued-by-seq into a single MQTT message with embedded `epcs[]`. ADR 026 captures the storage + reconciliation decisions (new `tag_presence` table — NOT a hypertable, current-state only, no `last_seq` or `suspect` columns; synchronous reconciliation per snap in a new `presence_reconciler.py` module — no window buffer, no timeout heuristic; single-replica subscriber constraint with the ACA-rolling-deploy caveat documented; two new event-bus topics `Topic.SIGNALING_TAG_APPEARED` / `Topic.SIGNALING_TAG_DISAPPEARED` join `Topic.SIGNALING_ATTRIBUTION_SETTLED` as the input set for the future presence-based rule family in Sprint 47+). Both ADRs registered in [docs/adr/README.md](docs/adr/README.md) at status `proposed`. No code or schema yet — Sprint 46 implementation lands them. Files: `docs/adr/025-edge-wire-format-v2.md`, `docs/adr/026-presence-model.md`, `docs/adr/README.md`.

- **Sprint 46 (proposed) — KISS-pass rewrite of edge wire format v2 spec.** Reworked [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md) on the back of WM-reader-developer feedback (informal, June 2026): (a) **dropped the per-cycle `seq` counter from the wire** — reboot is now opaque, snap-on-reconnect (§3.3 trigger 3) is the sole recovery primitive; (b) **restructured `t=0` snap from N messages glued by `(sn, seq)` into one MQTT message** carrying `epcs[]` array — QoS 1 + single-message atomicity replaces the snap-window state machine; (c) **replaced `empty:true` boolean flag with structurally-unambiguous `"epcs":[]`** in §3.4; (d) **dropped `last_seq` + `suspect` columns from `tag_presence` schema** in §4.1; (e) **collapsed §4.2 reconciliation algorithm from windowed-buffer pseudocode into synchronous-on-receipt** with `ON CONFLICT` upserts; (f) **error table simplified** in §6 — removed `empty_with_payload`, `empty_wrong_type`, two `seq`-related rows (gap + rollback), snap-window-timeout row; added `epcs_wrong_type`, `missing_required_field` for `epcs`, `invalid_snap_entry`, soft-warn `snap_large_total{sn}` at 5000-entry cap; (g) **payload guidance** in §7 updated to "~10 KB per snap message; 1 KB typical for t=1/t=2"; (h) **§8.3 "Removed in KISS pass"** records Q2 (seq persistence), Q10 (seq wrap), Q12 (snap terminator) as moot; (i) **§9.2 #2 (snap-window timeout) and #4 (per-reader seq state) deleted**, items renumbered; (j) **§11 checklist** updated to match the resolved/removed Q-set. Net diff: +197/-184 lines on a single file. The KISS pass cleaned the spec's internal consistency to the point where it could carry ADR-level signoff — see the companion ADR 025 + ADR 026 entry above. Files: `docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md`.

- **Sprint 46 (proposed) — draft edge wire format v2 spec for WM partner readers.** New design doc [docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md](docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md) capturing the flat per-tag JSON delta protocol (three-state discriminator `t ∈ {0=snap, 1=add, 2=sub}`, per-reader `seq` cycle counter, short field names, integer enums) for the WM-firmware RFID readers, plus the server-side two-table model (existing `tag_reads` + new `tag_presence`) and snap-window reconciliation algorithm. Document is **explicitly marked DRAFT v0.2** — pre-review, non-binding, with §8 listing 10 open questions to confirm with WM and §9 listing 8 unresolved concerns + 5 deferred items. No code, schema, ADR, or roadmap entry yet — those land in the Sprint 46 implementation PR after WM sign-off and ADR 025 / ADR 026 ratification. `docs/design/edge-wire-format-v2.md`.

- Updated `docs/azure-architecture.md` with an Azure-iconography Mermaid "At a glance" diagram that now shows explicit resource connections/flows and additional deployed resources (NSGs, private endpoints/DNS, UAMI, ACR, App Insights, Log Analytics).

- Added an Excalidraw source diagram for deployed Azure resources at `docs/assets/azure-deployed-resources.excalidraw`, linked from `docs/azure-architecture.md`.

- Added draw.io source diagram for the deployed Azure resource view at `docs/assets/azure-deployed-resources.drawio` (uses `mxgraph.azure2` icons; renders in diagrams.net, draw.io desktop, and the GitHub file viewer) and a pre-rendered PNG export at `docs/assets/azure-architecture.png` (rethemed to the Azure Architecture Center palette — supersedes the prior `azure-deployed-resources.png` export, which is removed). Both are linked from `docs/azure-architecture.md`. `.gitignore` updated to exclude draw.io desktop auto-backup files (`docs/assets/.*.bkp`).

- **Sprint 42 — multi-category filter on `GET /assets` via repeated `?category_ids=` query param (additive, ADR 019 close-out follow-up).** Generalises the Sprint 37 server-side categories filter from a singular FK match to an OR-of-categories `IN (...)` predicate so the upcoming TagPulse-UI side-panel filter (TagPulse-UI sprint-42) can multi-select categories without N round-trips or page-size cliffs. **Wire format**: `GET /v1/assets?category_ids=A&category_ids=B&category_ids=C` returns assets whose `category_id` is in `{A, B, C}`. Legacy `?category_id=<uuid>` still works — when both are supplied the service unions and dedupes before reaching the repo (so a client that accidentally sends the same id twice doesn't blow up the `IN` list, and a mixed-cardinality migration period round-trips cleanly). **Repo layer** [`src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/assets.py`](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/assets.py): `TimescaleAssetRepository.list` signature changes from `category_id: UUID | None` to `category_ids: list[UUID] | None`; emits `AssetModel.category_id.in_(category_ids)` when non-empty, no predicate when `None`. Empty list is treated identically to `None` so the route still works when no category filter is supplied — defends against the `IN ()` invalid-SQL edge case. The service layer is the one place that maps the (legacy singular, new plural) inputs to the single plural kwarg. **Service layer** [`src/tagpulse/api/services/asset_service.py`](src/tagpulse/api/services/asset_service.py): `AssetService.list_assets` accepts both `category_id: UUID | None` (legacy backwards-compat) and `category_ids: list[UUID] | None` (new); collapses them into a single deduplicated list before calling the repo. Set-based dedup preserves first-seen order — `category_id=A, category_ids=[A, B]` → `[A, B]`, not `[B, A]`. Empty inputs (no `category_id` and `category_ids` in `(None, [])`) collapse to `None` so the repo skips the predicate. **Route layer** [`src/tagpulse/api/routes/assets.py`](src/tagpulse/api/routes/assets.py): `GET /assets` gains `category_ids: list[UUID] | None = Query(default=None)` alongside the existing `category_id: UUID | None`. FastAPI's `list[UUID]` validator rejects malformed entries with HTTP 422 before reaching the service. The legacy singular description is updated to point at the new plural ("Kept for backwards compatibility; prefer `?category_ids=`"). The Sprint 41 Phase H `?asset_type=` 400 guard is untouched — that one-release migration hint still fires for clients that haven't migrated off the dropped column. **Tests** — three files touched. [`tests/unit/test_assets_repository_filters.py`](tests/unit/test_assets_repository_filters.py) refactored to assert the new `IN (...)` predicate shape across five cases: no filter (no `IN` predicate emitted), single-element list (still compiles to `IN (X)`, the service-collapse path), multi-element list, empty list treated as "no filter" (no `IN ()` invalid SQL), combines-with-other-filters (AND with `status` and `ILIKE`), and `literal_binds=True` UUID-binding regression that asserts every supplied UUID lands in the compiled SQL so the `IN` list can't silently truncate. [`tests/unit/test_asset_service.py`](tests/unit/test_asset_service.py) gains five new tests covering the service-level merge logic: legacy singular kwarg arrives as `[cid]`, plural kwarg flows through verbatim, both-supplied unions and dedupes, no kwargs ⇒ `None`, explicit empty plural ⇒ `None`. `_FakeAssetRepo.list` signature updated from `category_id=` to `category_ids=` to match the new repo contract. New file [`tests/unit/test_assets_route_category_ids.py`](tests/unit/test_assets_route_category_ids.py) (6 tests via FastAPI `TestClient` + `app.dependency_overrides` for `get_current_user` and `get_asset_service`) pins the route → service contract for each query-string shape: no filter, legacy singular, plural with one value, plural with multiple values, malformed UUID ⇒ HTTP 422 before the service is called, both singular and plural accepted on the same request. **OpenAPI regen** via `make export-openapi`: `+24/-2` lines, adds the `category_ids` array-of-UUID query parameter with the cross-pointing description; `openapi.json` 384,461 → 386,461 bytes. The upcoming `npm run generate-api` on TagPulse-UI picks up the new optional `category_ids?: string[]` field on the `AssetsService.listAssets` request type. **`make check` clean: 1106 unit tests passing** (+11 from sprint-41 main; +6 route + +5 service − 0 broken legacy tests), `ruff check src tests` ✓, `mypy --strict` ✓. No DB migration — the predicate change is query-only; the existing partial index `assets (tenant_id, category_id)` already supports the `IN` plan (PostgreSQL's planner converts a small `IN` list to a bitmap-OR of index scans). Phase H's one-release `?asset_type=` migration hint stays as-is; the inline `# Drop this guard in Sprint 42.` TODO note was intentionally left for a separate follow-up PR so this sprint stays scoped to the additive multi-category change. `src/tagpulse/api/routes/assets.py`, `src/tagpulse/api/services/asset_service.py`, `src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/assets.py`, `tests/unit/test_assets_repository_filters.py`, `tests/unit/test_asset_service.py`, `tests/unit/test_assets_route_category_ids.py`, `openapi.json`.

### Fixed

- **CI: complete the `build-and-push` GHCR attestation fix from PR #56 by also disabling buildx's embedded SLSA provenance attestation.** PR #56 swapped the attestation step's `subject-digest` from `steps.push.outputs.digest` (local image id) to `fromJSON(steps.push.outputs.metadata)['containerimage.digest']` (canonical buildx digest), but the post-merge `main`-branch run ([26066895103](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/actions/runs/26066895103)) still failed with the same `OCIError: 404` — just on a *different* digest. Root cause turned out to have a second layer the first PR missed: under `load: true` + `push: true`, buildx generates an **OCI image index** that wraps the image manifest + an embedded SLSA-provenance attestation manifest, but `load: true` forces single-manifest output to the docker daemon, so buildx pushes only the flat image manifest to the registry — never the index. `containerimage.digest` reports the **index** digest (`sha256:20f11062…`), which is what we now feed to `actions/attest-build-provenance@v1` — but that digest isn't at GHCR, only `sha256:5319a655…` (the flat image manifest that was actually pushed) is. Fix adds `provenance: false` to the `docker/build-push-action@v6` step, which tells buildx to skip the embedded provenance attestation and emit a flat single-platform manifest whose digest matches what's pushed. No supply-chain signal is lost — `actions/attest-build-provenance@v1` still generates SLSA provenance via GitHub's attestation API (the canonical source for this repo) and now successfully pushes the signed attestation as a referrer in GHCR. The inline comment in the workflow is updated to document both layers of the trap (`load: true` + `outputs.digest` bug AND the OCI-index-not-pushed bug) so the next person editing the workflow doesn't reintroduce either. Files: `.github/workflows/build-and-push.yml`.

- **CI: fix `build-and-push` workflow 404 in the GHCR provenance step on every push to `main`.** Symptom: each of the three image jobs (`api`, `worker`, `migrations`) succeeded at `docker/build-push-action@v6` (manifest pushed to both GHCR + the dev ACR) but then failed at `actions/attest-build-provenance@v1` with `OCIError: Error uploading artifact to container registry — Error fetching https://ghcr.io/v2/9owlsboston/tagpulse-<component>/manifests/sha256:<X> - expected 200, received 404`. Root cause: the attestation step's `subject-digest: ${{ steps.push.outputs.digest }}` was returning a **different** digest than what the build step actually pushed to GHCR — the build log showed e.g. `pushing manifest for ghcr.io/9owlsboston/tagpulse-worker:latest@sha256:ef4190cf…` while the attestation step requested `sha256:9be14d895c…`. This is the known [docker/build-push-action#1015](https://github.com/docker/build-push-action/issues/1015) interaction between `load: true` (which the Sprint 26 D2 tools-image smoke needs to `docker run` the api image locally) and `push: true` — `outputs.digest` falls back to the **local image id** instead of the remote **manifest digest** when both are set. PR runs were unaffected because the attestation step is gated on `if: github.event_name != 'pull_request'`, which masked the bug behind successful PR CI ever since the workflow landed in Sprint 22 B3. Fix replaces `subject-digest: ${{ steps.push.outputs.digest }}` with `subject-digest: ${{ fromJSON(steps.push.outputs.metadata)['containerimage.digest'] }}` in [`.github/workflows/build-and-push.yml`](.github/workflows/build-and-push.yml), which reads the canonical manifest digest from buildx's `--metadata-file` JSON (the same value buildx prints in the `pushing manifest for … @sha256:…` line) and is invariant under `load: true`. Inline comment documents the trap so the next person editing the workflow doesn't reintroduce it. **Note**: this fix turned out to be incomplete — see the follow-up entry above for the second layer (`provenance: false`) that was needed to close the 404. Files: `.github/workflows/build-and-push.yml`.

- **CORS: allow Azure Static Web App preview-slot URLs via `allow_origin_regex`.** Reported breakage: SPAs served from a SWA preview slot (per-PR hostnames like `https://<basename>-42.centralus.7.azurestaticapps.net`) failed every backend `fetch()` with a CORS preflight rejection because `cors_origins` is an exact-match comma list and preview hostnames cannot be enumerated ahead of time. Fix wires a new `CORS_ORIGIN_REGEX` env var end-to-end: [`Settings.cors_origin_regex`](src/tagpulse/core/config.py) (defaults to `""`, validated at boot with `re.compile` so a typo fails fast instead of surfacing as a 500 mid-request); [`api/main.py`](src/tagpulse/api/main.py) forwards it to Starlette `CORSMiddleware` as `allow_origin_regex` (empty string → `None`, so the explicit allow-list path is unchanged when the regex is unset); [`/health/ready`](src/tagpulse/api/routes/health.py) `_config_snapshot()` surfaces the value alongside `cors.allow_origins` so operators can verify the regex landed on the deployed revision without exec'ing into the container. **Bicep wiring**: [`modules/container-app.bicep`](deploy/azure/bicep/modules/container-app.bicep) accepts a new optional `corsOriginRegex` param and emits the `CORS_ORIGIN_REGEX` env var beside the existing `CORS_ORIGINS` entry; [`workload.bicep`](deploy/azure/bicep/workload.bicep) auto-derives a regex from `ui.outputs.defaultHostname` that matches the production hostname AND its preview slots (`^https://<basename>(-\d+)?(\.[a-z0-9-]+)?\.<tier>\.azurestaticapps\.net$`), with a new `corsOriginRegexOverride` param ([`main.bicepparam`](deploy/azure/bicep/main.bicepparam) reads it from the `CORS_ORIGIN_REGEX` env var) for the rare case an operator needs to tighten/broaden it. Worker container is unaffected (no ingress). **Tests** — [`tests/unit/test_cors_origin_regex.py`](tests/unit/test_cors_origin_regex.py) (new) covers: Settings default empty, invalid regex rejection, env-var wiring, `/health/ready` surface (set + unset), live `CORSMiddleware` preflight against three SWA hostname shapes (prod, preview no region, preview with region), rejection of three non-matching shapes (wrong basename / wrong suffix / wrong scheme), and Bicep wiring assertions for all five edits. `make check` clean. Files: `src/tagpulse/core/config.py`, `src/tagpulse/api/main.py`, `src/tagpulse/api/routes/health.py`, `deploy/azure/bicep/modules/container-app.bicep`, `deploy/azure/bicep/workload.bicep`, `deploy/azure/bicep/main.bicepparam`, `tests/unit/test_cors_origin_regex.py`.

### Changed

- **Sprint 41 Phase H — close ADR 019 by dropping `assets.asset_type` (breaking API change) + Phase G5 ADR 019 docs close-out.** Completes the Categories cutover that started in Sprint 34 ADR 019 ("`asset_type` is dropped in a future migration once UI + clients have switched"). Sprint 41 Phase F7 brought the UI side (visible `Type` field gone from Asset create/edit forms); this Phase H ships the backend half on the same Sprint 41 PR rather than deferring it as the immediately-preceding Phase G CHANGELOG entry originally suggested. The deferral note in that entry is now historical — Phase H landed in the same PR. **Breaking** for any external API caller that still sends `?asset_type=` or reads `asset_type` off `Asset*` payloads. **H1 migration** [`migrations/versions/041_drop_assets_asset_type.py`](migrations/versions/041_drop_assets_asset_type.py): four-step `upgrade()` runs as the table owner without `FORCE ROW LEVEL SECURITY` per the established Sprint 38 migration 037 pattern — (a) JOIN-backfills `assets.category_id` from `categories.name` keyed off the legacy `asset_type` so existing rows pick up the structured FK that ADR 019 introduced as nullable; (b) safety-net seeds a per-tenant `_uncategorized` Category (`category_type='object'`, `required_tags=1`) and assigns any remaining NULL `category_id` rows to it — defends against rows that were created via the asset_type-only legacy path between ADR 019 and Phase H without an explicit category and ensures the subsequent NOT NULL promotion can't fail mid-migration; (c) `ALTER TABLE assets ALTER COLUMN category_id SET NOT NULL` makes the FK permanent; (d) `DROP INDEX IF EXISTS ix_assets_tenant_type` then `ALTER TABLE assets DROP COLUMN asset_type`. Every step is guarded by `information_schema` checks so a partial rerun (e.g. after a migration crash) is idempotent. Symmetric `downgrade()` re-adds the column nullable, backfills from `categories.name`, promotes to NOT NULL, and recreates `ix_assets_tenant_type` — round-trippable. **H2 schemas** [`src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py`](src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py): removed `asset_type` from `AssetCreate` / `AssetUpdate` / `AssetResponse` / `ManifestEntry` / `ManifestResponse` / `AssetInZoneSummary`. `AssetCreate.category_id` is now **required** (was nullable during the ADR 019 compatibility window) and `AssetResponse.category_id` is now required non-Optional. `AssetUpdate.category_id` stays `UUID | None` with the "omit = no change" PATCH semantics; the API layer rejects an explicit `null` per the established Sprint 34 pattern. **H3 service + repos** — `AssetService.list_assets` ([`src/tagpulse/api/services/asset_service.py`](src/tagpulse/api/services/asset_service.py)) drops the `asset_type` parameter; `create_asset`'s audit-log `changes` dict now writes `{"name": ..., "category_id": str(asset.category_id)}` instead of the old `{"name", "asset_type", ...}` triple. `TimescaleAssetRepository` ([`src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/assets.py`](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/assets.py)) drops the `AssetModel.asset_type` filter branch + the `_asset_to_response` mapping, including both arms of the `get_descendants` recursive CTE (anchor + recursive — neither references the dropped column anymore). `asset_location.py` ([`src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/asset_location.py`](src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/asset_location.py)) drops the `a.asset_type` raw-SQL columns from `_ASSETS_IN_READER_BOUND_ZONE` and `_ASSETS_LATEST_GPS_READ`, and the `AssetInZoneSummary` list comprehensions that consumed them. **H4 route** [`src/tagpulse/api/routes/assets.py`](src/tagpulse/api/routes/assets.py): `GET /assets` drops the `asset_type: str | None = Query(...)` parameter and gets a one-release migration hint — any request that still carries an `?asset_type=` query param (including empty values) is rejected with **HTTP 400** before the label-filter parse, with detail `"The ?asset_type= query parameter was removed in Sprint 41 (ADR 019 close-out). Use ?category_id=<uuid> instead — list categories at GET /v1/tenants/{slug}/categories."`. The guard carries an inline `# Drop this guard in Sprint 42.` TODO so the next sprint can mechanically clear it; the hint is intentionally specific enough that a CI grep in a downstream consumer can map it to a concrete migration step. **H5 tests** — updated 8 unit/integration test files (plus 1 new regression file = 9 touched in total) to drop `asset_type` from fixtures and supply `category_id=uuid4()` where the schema now requires it: `tests/unit/test_asset_service.py` (factory + `_FakeAssetRepo` create signature + list signature + new audit assertion `audit.entries[-1]["changes"]["category_id"] == str(cid)`), `tests/unit/test_carrier_external.py` (factory + `_FakeAssetRepo.set_parent` clone + 3 test bodies dropping per-test `asset_type=` overrides), `tests/unit/test_categories.py` (7 `AssetCreate(...)` constructions switched from `asset_type="drum"` to `category_id=uuid4()`; renamed `test_category_id_optional_on_create` → `test_category_id_required_on_create` to reflect the schema change), `tests/unit/test_asset_location.py` (factory + `AssetInZoneSummary` construction), `tests/unit/test_sprint21_caches.py` (factory; `uuid4` was already imported), `tests/unit/test_sprint19_subject_telemetry.py` (2 `AssetResponse` constructions), `tests/unit/test_label_filter.py` (`asset_type` → `category_id` in the unrelated-params smoke test), `tests/unit/test_assets_repository_filters.py` (dropped the `asset_type="pallet"` kwarg + the `"assets.asset_type ="` SQL assert from the combines-with-other-filters test; status/category_id/ilike asserts retained). New file [`tests/unit/test_assets_route_asset_type_removed.py`](tests/unit/test_assets_route_asset_type_removed.py) covers the 400 guard with three FastAPI-TestClient tests using `app.dependency_overrides` for `get_current_user` (viewer role) and `get_asset_service` (stub returning `[]`): `test_asset_type_query_returns_400_with_migration_hint` (asserts `"asset_type"` + `"category_id"` + `"Sprint 41"` all appear in the detail), `test_asset_type_empty_value_still_returns_400` (defends against `?asset_type=` with an empty value sneaking past via FastAPI's empty-string coercion), and `test_list_assets_without_asset_type_still_works` (regression: the new guard doesn't false-positive on requests that don't carry the param). **H6 EPC parser stays** — [`src/tagpulse/rfid/epc.py`](src/tagpulse/rfid/epc.py)'s `asset_type_bits` / `asset_type` local variables and the `"asset_type"` dict key in its returned payload are GRAI URI bit-allocation semantics from the RFID protocol, not the dropped DB column; left untouched per the original roadmap plan. **Scripts** — [`scripts/simulate_assets.py`](scripts/simulate_assets.py) gains an `ensure_pallet_category(client, tenant_id)` helper that does a `GET /categories?limit=1000` lookup for the name "Sim-Pallet" and creates it on miss with `{"name": "Sim-Pallet", "category_type": "rti_container", "required_tags": 1}`; `ensure_assets()` calls it and uses `"category_id": category_id` in the POST payload instead of the dropped `"asset_type": "pallet"`. [`scripts/smoke_setup.py::ensure_assets_with_bindings`](scripts/smoke_setup.py) mirrors the same pattern inline at the top of the function. **G5 — ADR 019 close-out** ships in this same commit per the Phase G entry's original plan: [docs/adr/019-categories.md](docs/adr/019-categories.md) Status flipped to `**Completed** (Sprint 41 close-out, [PR #54](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/pull/54) — accepted Sprint 34, May 2026; compatibility window closed Sprint 41, Phase H)` with the migration paragraph rewritten in past tense citing migrations 037 + 041; [docs/data-models.md](docs/data-models.md) drops the `assets.asset_type` table row, flips `assets.category_id` to NOT NULL with a note about Sprint 41 Phase H migration 041, and updates the Migration provenance line to `"017 (base table); 037 adds category_id; 041 promotes category_id to NOT NULL and drops asset_type"`; [docs/design/assets-and-zones.md](docs/design/assets-and-zones.md) CREATE TABLE swaps `asset_type VARCHAR(50)` for `category_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES categories(id) ON DELETE RESTRICT`, the index renames `ix_assets_tenant_category`, the paragraph is rewritten to reference ADR-019 + Sprint 41 Phase H, the no-quantity callout's `GROUP BY` and the `AssetRepository.list` signature are updated to `category_id`; [docs/design/tracking-modes.md](docs/design/tracking-modes.md) example query changes to `WHERE category_id = '<forklift-category>'`; [docs/design/geofencing-and-map.md](docs/design/geofencing-and-map.md) two `asset_filter` blocks change `asset_type: pallet`/`container` to `category_id: <pallet-category-uuid>`/`<container-category-uuid>`; [docs/guides/domain-concepts-101.md](docs/guides/domain-concepts-101.md) curl example uses `"name": "Sim-Pallet-03", "category_id": "<pallet-category-uuid>"`. **Roadmap reconciliation** — [docs/roadmap.md](docs/roadmap.md) Phase H section drops its "(deferred to a follow-up sprint)" header + the standalone deferral status blockquote, flips H1–H6 from `[planned]` to `[done, this PR]` with implementation notes inline, F7's "(still carrying the column until Phase H)" / "Phase H ... is deferred" language reworded to past tense, and G5 flipped from `[deferred to a follow-up sprint]` to `[done, this PR]`. [ADR 021](docs/adr/021-configurable-sensing-events.md) v2.2 decision-history block rewritten — the "Phase H deferred" paragraph is replaced with "Phase H shipped in the same Sprint 41 PR as the original plan" + a recap of the migration strategy + the breaking-change scope + the one-release HTTP 400 hint. **openapi.json regenerated** via `python scripts/export_openapi.py` — `AssetCreate.category_id` is now `required`; `AssetResponse.category_id` is now `required` non-nullable; `AssetUpdate.category_id` stays optional; `ManifestEntry.asset_type` / `ManifestResponse.asset_type` / `AssetInZoneSummary.asset_type` / `AssetCreate.asset_type` / `AssetUpdate.asset_type` / `AssetResponse.asset_type` all removed; the `asset_type` query parameter on `GET /assets` removed. **`make check` clean.** Migration / API / SDK consumers need a one-line change: stop sending `?asset_type=`, send `?category_id=<uuid>` instead (categories listable at `GET /v1/tenants/{slug}/categories`). `migrations/versions/041_drop_assets_asset_type.py`, `src/tagpulse/models/schemas.py`, `src/tagpulse/models/database.py`, `src/tagpulse/api/routes/assets.py`, `src/tagpulse/api/services/asset_service.py`, `src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/assets.py`, `src/tagpulse/repositories/timescaledb/asset_location.py`, `scripts/simulate_assets.py`, `scripts/smoke_setup.py`, `tests/unit/test_asset_service.py`, `tests/unit/test_carrier_external.py`, `tests/unit/test_categories.py`, `tests/unit/test_asset_location.py`, `tests/unit/test_sprint21_caches.py`, `tests/unit/test_sprint19_subject_telemetry.py`, `tests/unit/test_label_filter.py`, `tests/unit/test_assets_repository_filters.py`, `tests/unit/test_assets_route_asset_type_removed.py`, `docs/adr/019-categories.md`, `docs/adr/021-configurable-sensing-events.md`, `docs/data-models.md`, `docs/design/assets-and-zones.md`, `docs/design/tracking-modes.md`, `docs/design/geofencing-and-map.md`, `docs/guides/domain-concepts-101.md`, `docs/roadmap.md`, `openapi.json`.

### Added

- **Sprint 41 Phase G — documentation reconciliation for Configurable Signaling Events (ADR 021 v2 ratification + remediation row flips + user-guide section).** Closes the docs half of Sprint 41 after backend Phases A–E (PR [#54](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse/pull/54), `e54332b` → `975ef6f`) and UI Phase F (TagPulse-UI [PR #46](https://github.com/9owlsboston/TagPulse-UI/pull/46), `ebb2f82`) shipped. **G1 — ADR 021 ratified Proposed → Accepted** in [`docs/adr/021-configurable-sensing-events.md`](docs/adr/021-configurable-sensing-events.md): Status header flipped to "Accepted (Sprint 41, May 2026)" with back-links to PR #54 (backend) and TagPulse-UI PR #46 (UI); v2.2 entry appended to the §"Decision history" recording the per-phase commit chain, the four v2.1 open-question leans resolving as leaned (kind="signaling" stays `VARCHAR + pattern` not Postgres ENUM; discriminator is the in-process two-level `split_signaling_condition_type` helper not Pydantic `Field(discriminator=...)`; per-rule `integration_ids` **replace** the global broadcast when non-empty per Phase E2 pinned by `test_webhook_per_rule_routing.py::TestPerRuleReplace`; default cap of 5 per `(event_type, category_id)` is hard-reject with admin-only `?override=true` writing one `audit_logs` row per Phase B2 pinned by `test_signaling_rules_api.py`); ADR §"Open questions" rewritten to mark all Sprint 41 questions resolved and forward-point only the cross-ADR items (ADR 024 trilateration Sprint 45, post-Sprint-41 rule taxonomy unification). The "signaling" terminology is now load-bearing across schema columns (`event_type`, `trigger`, `processor`), service classes (`SignalingScopeCapExceededError`, `validate_signaling_condition_config`), modules (`src/tagpulse/signaling/`), event-bus topics (`signaling.attribution_settled`), API discriminator (`?kind=signaling`), and UI components (`SignalingRuleModal`, `SignalingEventType`, `SIGNALING_VALID_PAIRS`) — a future revert to "sensing" would be a multi-PR sweep, so v2.2 explicitly notes the taxonomy choice is locked. **G2 — Four reference-design remediation rows flipped to ✅ Done** in [`docs/design/reference-design-remediation.md`](docs/design/reference-design-remediation.md) per the doc's own §7 "Updating this document" rule: §3.1 row 2.3 (Configurable Signaling Events backend) → ✅ Done with PR #54 commit range `e54332b → 975ef6f` covering Phases A–E; row 2.9 (Outbound event envelope) → ✅ Done with `feae604` (Phase C) and a per-event-type identity-key recap (`location` → `[asset_id, zone_id]`, `geolocation` → `[asset_id, site_id]`, `geofencing` → `[asset_id, zone_id]`, `temperature` → `[asset_id]`); §3.2 row 1.1 ("Unify Telemetry/Models/Rules/Alerts → Signaling Events & Data") → ✅ Done with TagPulse-UI PR #46 `ebb2f82` — column relabeled "Signaling Events & Data" (the v2.1 sensing→signaling rename is consistent across the surface so the sidebar group label matches schema + event-bus + React component naming); row 3.5 ("Signaling Events modal") → ✅ Done with the same UI commit and a callout that the 13-pair `SIGNALING_VALID_PAIRS` matrix rejects impossible pairs (`temperature.on_entry`, `geofencing.on_change`) client-side before submit. **G3 — User-guide section "Configurable Signaling Events"** added to [`docs/user-guide.md`](docs/user-guide.md) between the existing Rules and Alerts sections (TOC + anchor + ~150 lines): "What's new vs. legacy rules" comparison table; the authoritative 13-pair event-type × trigger matrix with a one-line rationale per restriction (`on_inference` is `location`-only because OverlappingZones is the only processor that publishes `signaling.attribution_settled`; `geofencing` triggers are spatial primitives that don't apply to subject-bound metric streams); a four-step "Creating a Signaling Event" walkthrough that maps to the Phase F2 modal screens; **four curl recipes** — Location `on_change` (high-value asset zone change with `cooldown_s=300`, scoped to one Category); Temperature `periodic` (daily cold-chain digest with `cadence_minutes=1440`, scoped to one Category); Geofencing `on_entry` (restricted-zone breach with explicit `zone_id` + `subject_kinds=["asset"]` + `cooldown_s=60`, broadcast scope); Geolocation `on_inactivity` (GPS asset silent > 60 min with `inactivity_minutes=60` + `cooldown_s=300`, scoped to one Category) — all POST to the unified `/v1/tenants/{slug}/rules` endpoint with `"kind": "signaling"` body (no `/sensing-events` URL, per Phase E1 deviation); plus sections on listing (`?kind=signaling` filter), the per-scope cap + admin override semantics (HTTP 409 / `?override=true` + audit-log row), and the per-rule webhook routing replace-not-augment behaviour pinned by `test_webhook_per_rule_routing.py::TestPerRuleReplace`. **Roadmap reconciliation** — every [planned] marker on Sprint 41 Phases A through G in [`docs/roadmap.md`](docs/roadmap.md) flipped to [done] with the implementing commit SHA inline; Phase E1 explicitly attributed to Phase B2 commit `9f02f38` (the discriminator filter shipped on the existing `/rules` endpoint at Phase B time, not Phase E time — the per-roadmap deviation from the original `/sensing-events` URL proposal);
